# ===== BEGIN RECIPE INDEX =====
Cookbook: Journalist Process  (CFT-FWK-COOKBK-JOURNALIST-PROCESS)   version v1.00a
Recipes: 18   |   Sub-categories: 8   |   Recipe-type: journalism
Jump to any recipe via its  # START RECIPE-ID: <id>  marker in the RECIPES section.

── SUBCAT-001-ORCHESTRATOR   (SME: Nellie) ──
  RCP-007-001-001  ·  Journalist Workflow Orchestrator  ·  Master coordinator for the 17-recipe, 7-stage journalism workflow.  ·  Advanced
── SUBCAT-002-RESEARCH   (SME: René) ──
  RCP-007-002-001  ·  Trend Discovery Engine  ·  Trend-to-angles ideation engine for journalists.  ·  Beginner
  RCP-007-002-002  ·  Story Viability Validator  ·  Eight-point story-viability assessment with a go/no-go verdict for journalists.  ·  Intermediate
  RCP-007-002-003  ·  Research Roadmap Builder  ·  Turns a validated angle into a phased, deadline-anchored investigation plan.  ·  Advanced
── SUBCAT-003-PITCHING-ASSIGNMENT   (SME: Nellie) ──
  RCP-007-003-001  ·  Pitch Architect  ·  Editor-ready story-pitch builder for journalists.  ·  Intermediate
  RCP-007-003-002  ·  Pitch Audience Strategist  ·  Multi-audience pitch-optimization and objection-prep engine.  ·  Advanced
── SUBCAT-004-WRITING-DRAFTING   (SME: Dominique) ──
  RCP-007-004-001  ·  Article Blueprint Architect  ·  Turns raw research into a structured, drafting-ready article outline.  ·  Beginner
  RCP-007-004-002  ·  Draft Composer and Refiner  ·  Composes and iteratively refines a complete article draft.  ·  Intermediate
  RCP-007-004-003  ·  Headline and Lead Generator  ·  Produces ranked headlines and leads with SEO and platform variations.  ·  Beginner
── SUBCAT-005-EDITING-FACTCHECK   (SME: Fernand) ──
  RCP-007-005-001  ·  Claim Verification Engine  ·  Systematic, claim-by-claim fact-checking engine for article drafts.  ·  Intermediate
  RCP-007-005-002  ·  Source Alignment Auditor  ·  Source-grounded, audit-trail verification of a draft against the writer's own sources.  ·  Advanced
  RCP-007-005-003  ·  Publication Risk Scanner  ·  Adversarial legal/ethical/reputation/clarity risk scan for pre-publication drafts.  ·  Advanced
── SUBCAT-006-FINAL-REVIEW   (SME: Nellie) ──
  RCP-007-006-001  ·  Editorial Quality Gate  ·  Five-dimension editorial quality gate that rates publication readiness before approval.  ·  Advanced
  RCP-007-006-002  ·  Publication Approval Panel  ·  Four-perspective publication approval panel that returns a go/no-go verdict with actions.  ·  Advanced
── SUBCAT-007-PUBLISHING-DISTRIBUTION   (SME: Auguste) ──
  RCP-007-007-001  ·  Publication Launch Coordinator  ·  Multi-channel publication launch coordinator for approved journalism content.  ·  Advanced
  RCP-007-007-002  ·  Content Amplification Strategist  ·  Tiered syndication, republishing, and PR amplification planner for published journalism.  ·  Advanced
── SUBCAT-008-ENGAGEMENT-ANALYTICS   (SME: Nellie) ──
  RCP-007-008-001  ·  Engagement Pulse Analyzer  ·  Post-publication sentiment, theme, and issue analyzer for editorial response.  ·  Intermediate
  RCP-007-008-002  ·  Feedback Action Strategist  ·  Turns engagement insights into drafted responses, follow-up stories, and a content calendar.  ·  Advanced

      "id": "RCP-007-005-002",

      "persona": "Fernand",
      "ai_to_ai_communication": {
        "schema_version": "1.1",

            "type": "prose",

                "key": "paraphrase_vs_quote",

          }

          },

      "id": "RCP-007-005-003",
      "fq": "CFT-FWK-COOKBK-JOURNALIST-PROCESS::RCP-007-005-003",

      "persona": "Fernand",
      "ai_to_ai_communication": {
        "schema_version": "1.1",
        "schema_profile": "Option-B typed-envelope (H041 LOCKED canonical)",
        "authored_by": "P062-Cat - SP11 Journalist-Process cookbook build (P062-H027)",
        "envelope": [
          {
            "type": "prose",
            "body": "HANDOFF CONTRACT: emits four severity-graded risk inventories (Legal [L#], Ethical [E#], Reputation [R#], Clarity [C#]), a risk report (counts by type and by severity + an overall risk level), a contextual analysis (compounding / most-likely / highest-impact), and an executive summary with a publication-readiness call. Upstream: RCP-007-005-002 (Source Alignment Auditor) supplies CONTRADICTED claims and discrepancies that become legal/reputation risk inputs. Downstream: RCP-007-006-001 (Editorial Quality Gate) consumes the overall risk level and any unresolved CRITICAL/HIGH risks as gate criteria."
          },

            "type": "prose",
            "body": "EXECUTION GUIDANCE: run as Fernand in adversarial red-team posture — read the draft as a hostile critic, a plaintiff's lawyer, and a screenshot-hunting reader would.           },
          {
            "type": "keyed_list",
            "preamble": "EDGE CASES:",
            "items": [
              {
                "key": "no_draft",
                "body": "If article_draft is missing, stop and issue the RequiredQuestion; do not assess risk from a description of the content."
              },
              {
                "key": "critical_high_legal",
                "body": "Any CRITICAL or HIGH legal risk MUST carry the explicit not-legal-advice disclaimer and a 'consult a qualified attorney' recommendation — never imply the flag is a legal clearance."
              },

                "key": "low_tolerance_noise",
                "body": "Under risk_tolerance 'high', suppress LOW/MEDIUM clarity/tone items so CRITICAL/HIGH legal and ethical risks are not buried; under 'conservative', surface them all."
              }
            ]

            "type": "prose",
            "body": "QUALITY BAR: every risk has a domain prefix (L/E/R/C), a severity, an exact quoted text in question, and a location; reputation risks include an adversarial reading; the report's by-type and by-severity counts reconcile to the total; and the summary gives a clear readiness call plus the not-legal-advice caution."
          }
        ],
        "lessons_learned": [
          {
            "key": "flag_dont_fix",
            "body": "The scanner's credibility depends on staying diagnostic — once it starts drafting legal fixes it implies a clearance it cannot give. Name the risk and route to a professional; let the human and their counsel decide the remedy."
          },
          {
            "key": "adversarial_reading_finds_the_real_risk",
            "body": "The highest-value reputation finds come from explicitly writing 'how a critic would frame this in a screenshot' — neutral reading misses lines that are fine in context but toxic in isolation."
          },
          {
            "key": "severity_must_drive_attention",
            "body": "Volume is noise; a clean by-severity rollup with the not-legal-advice disclaimer on every CRITICAL/HIGH legal item is what actually changes the publish decision at the editorial gate."
          }
        ]
      }
    },

      "ai_to_ai_communication": {

        "schema_profile": "Option-B typed-envelope (H041 LOCKED canonical)",

        "envelope": [
          {
            "type": "prose",
            "body": "HANDOFF CONTRACT: emits an editorial_memo (five dimension scores, top-3 strengths, top-3 improvements, headline alternatives, prioritized actions), an overall_score, and a readiness_rating of READY / NEEDS POLISH / MAJOR REVISION. Downstream: a READY draft plus its memo passes to RCP-007-006-002 (Publication Approval Panel); MAJOR REVISION routes back to RCP-007-004-002 (Draft Composer, Dominique). The overall_score may be carried into the panel as quality_gate_score."
          },
          {
            "type": "prose",
            "body": "EXECUTION GUIDANCE: run as Nellie (standards-first, verdict-first). Score each of the five dimensions against explicit criteria with concrete textual examples, never on impression; the rating thresholds (>=8.0 with every dimension >=7 = READY; >=6.0 = NEEDS POLISH) ARE the gate, so do not soften them. Assume the content is already fact-checked upstream; assess editorial quality, not factual accuracy."
          },
          {
            "type": "keyed_list",
            "preamble": "EDGE CASES:",
            "items": [
              {
                "key": "high_average_one_weak_dimension",
                "body": "A strong average does NOT make a draft READY if any single dimension scores below 7 — return NEEDS POLISH and name the weak dimension."
              },
              {
                "key": "missing_publication_style",
                "body": "If publication_style is absent, ASK before scoring tone/engagement; evaluating against the wrong style invalidates two of the five scores."
              },
              {
                "key": "fact_concern_surfaces",
                "body": "If an apparent factual or sourcing problem surfaces during the read, flag it and route to Fernand (RCP-007-005-001) rather than scoring it as an editorial defect; this gate does not re-fact-check."
              }
            ]
          },
          {
            "type": "prose",
            "body": "QUALITY BAR: every dimension carries a 1-10 score backed by at least one strength example and one improvement note; the memo lists exactly top-3 strengths and top-3 improvements with actionable recommendations; 2-3 headline alternatives are supplied; the readiness rating follows the thresholds exactly and names a concrete next step."
          }
        ],
        "lessons_learned": [
          {
            "key": "weakest_dimension_gates",
            "body": "Publication readiness is gated by the weakest dimension, not the average — a 9-clarity draft with 5-structure reads as polished but loses readers; enforce the per-dimension floor."
          },
          {
            "key": "examples_make_feedback_actionable",
            "body": "Scores without a quoted example are ignored by writers; every improvement note that cites a specific passage gets acted on, so anchor each finding to text."
          },
          {
            "key": "editorial_is_not_factual",
            "body": "Keeping the editorial gate separate from fact-checking prevents both from being done badly; a beautifully written but unverified piece must still fail upstream, not here."
          }
        ]
      }

# START RECIPE-ID: RCP-007-001-001
# ===========================================================
# CRAFT RECIPE: Journalist Workflow Orchestrator
# Created: January 2, 2026 (source v2.00a, JOURNALIST-PROCESS cookbook)
# Revised: v3.00a — 2026-06-27 (P062-SP11 Phase 9, P062-H027)
# Creator: CRAFT (Journalist-Process cookbook)
# Upgraded by: P062-Cat (SP11 — v2.00a→v3.00a transform)
# Status: Official (CFT-FWK-COOKBK-JOURNALIST-PROCESS)
# ===========================================================

# ===========================================================
# GENERAL
# ===========================================================
Recipe Type:  Cookbook recipe (Official)
Name:         RCP-007-001-001
Description:  Master coordinator for the 17-recipe journalism flow across 7 stages. Assesses where the user is,
              routes them to the correct stage and its recipes, enforces entry/exit conditions between stages,
              tracks working title / target publication / deadline / progress, and reports workflow completion.

# ===========================================================
# CATEGORIES
# ===========================================================
Part Of Cookbook:   CFT-FWK-COOKBK-JOURNALIST-PROCESS
Category ID:        007  (CAT-007-JOURNALIST-PROCESS)
Subcategory ID:    001  (SUBCAT-001-ORCHESTRATOR)
Recipe ID Number:  RCP-007-001-001
Fully-Qualified:   CFT-FWK-COOKBK-JOURNALIST-PROCESS::RCP-007-001-001
Status:            Official
Categories:        Journalist Process
Subcategories:     Orchestrator
Tags:              orchestrator · workflow · coordinator · journalism · routing · pipeline · entry-point · stages
Recommended Persona: Nellie — Managing Editor (namespaced: PERSONA-JOURNALIST-PROCESS-NELLIE-CARD.txt)
Difficulty:        Advanced

# ===========================================================
# INSTRUCTIONS
# ===========================================================
1. Confirm inputs (all optional, all with defaults): current_stage (default "assess"), content_title,
   target_publication, deadline.
2. Adopt Nellie's editorial framing: as Managing Editor she owns the workflow and the publish decision; she
   commissions each stage to its specialist and holds the line on entry/exit conditions.
3. INITIALIZE: load the Journalist Process Cookbook; announce that 17 recipes across 7 stages are available.
4. STAGE ASSESSMENT:
   - If current_stage == "assess", ask the user to describe their position (A) no idea yet · B) have idea, need
     to pitch · C) have assignment, need to write · D) have draft, need editing/review · E) approved, ready to
     publish · F) published, monitoring engagement).
   - If current_stage names a known stage, report the stage name, list that stage's recipes (by canonical id),
     and offer to begin the first recipe.
5. The 7 stages, their recipes (canonical ids + section persona), and conditions:
   - SUBCAT-002-RESEARCH (Idea Generation and Research) → René. Recipes: RCP-007-002-001 (Trend Discovery
     Engine), RCP-007-002-002 (Story Viability Validator), RCP-007-002-003 (Research Roadmap Builder).
     Entry: no story idea yet. Exit: validated idea with angle.
   - SUBCAT-003-PITCHING-ASSIGNMENT (Pitching and Assignment) → Nellie. Recipes: RCP-007-003-001 (Pitch
     Architect), RCP-007-003-002 (Pitch Audience Strategist). Entry: have validated story idea. Exit: approved
     pitch with scope.
   - SUBCAT-004-WRITING-DRAFTING (Writing and Drafting) → Dominique. Recipes: RCP-007-004-001 (Article Blueprint
     Architect), RCP-007-004-002 (Draft Composer and Refiner), RCP-007-004-003 (Headline and Lead Generator).
     Entry: have approved assignment. Exit: complete draft matching voice.
   - SUBCAT-005-EDITING-FACTCHECK (Editing and Fact-Checking) → Fernand. Recipes: RCP-007-005-001 (Claim
     Verification Engine), RCP-007-005-002 (Source Alignment Auditor), RCP-007-005-003 (Publication Risk
     Scanner). Entry: have complete draft. Exit: verified and risk-assessed.
   - SUBCAT-006-FINAL-REVIEW (Final Review and Approval) → Nellie. Recipes: RCP-007-006-001 (Editorial Quality
     Gate), RCP-007-006-002 (Publication Approval Panel). Entry: have verified draft. Exit: publication approval
     received.
   - SUBCAT-007-PUBLISHING-DISTRIBUTION (Publishing and Distribution) → Auguste. Recipes: RCP-007-007-001
     (Publication Launch Coordinator), RCP-007-007-002 (Content Amplification Strategist). Entry: have approved
     content. Exit: published across channels.
   - SUBCAT-008-ENGAGEMENT-ANALYTICS (Engagement and Analytics) → Nellie. Recipes: RCP-007-008-001 (Engagement
     Pulse Analyzer), RCP-007-008-002 (Feedback Action Strategist). Entry: content is published. Exit: analyzed,
     follow-up planned.
6. STAGE NAVIGATION — for each transition: (1) verify exit conditions of the current stage are met; (2) confirm
   entry conditions of the next stage; (3) summarize what was accomplished; (4) introduce the next stage and its
   purpose; (5) offer to begin the first recipe of that stage.
7. WORKFLOW TRACKING — maintain awareness of content_title, target_publication, deadline, progress through the
   7 stages, and which recipes have been completed (progress % = completed / 17).
8. COMPLETION — when all 7 stages are done, report the full path (Research 3 · Pitching 2 · Writing 3 · Editing 3
   · Final Review 2 · Publishing 2 · Engagement 2) and offer to (A) start a new project, (B) review what worked,
   or (C) explore follow-up content opportunities.

# ===========================================================
# CUSTOM FIELDS
# ===========================================================
Recipe FAQ:
  Q: What is this recipe? A: the master orchestrator (entry point) of the Journalist-Process cookbook — it routes
     a user through the 7-stage, 17-recipe journalism pipeline.
  Q: Does it write or verify anything itself? A: no — it coordinates. Each stage is executed by its own recipe
     and section persona (René/Nellie/Dominique/Fernand/Auguste).
How A.I. Reads This Recipe:
  Execute as Nellie (Managing Editor). Determine the user's current stage, route to the correct stage's recipes
  by their canonical ids, enforce entry/exit conditions before advancing, and track progress. Do not perform a
  downstream stage's work inline; hand off to the named recipe/persona.
Recipe Short Description: Master coordinator for the 17-recipe, 7-stage journalism workflow.
When To Use: at the very start of (or any time during) a journalism project, to locate the user in the workflow
  and route them to the right next recipe.
Actual Examples: current_stage="assess", content_title="EV battery supply-chain story",
  target_publication="trade outlet", deadline="2 weeks".
Recipe Name: RCP-007-001-001
Included In Cookbook: CFT-FWK-COOKBK-JOURNALIST-PROCESS
Recommended Prompt Framework: CRAFT #H->AI / #AI->H comment protocol.
Extension Of: — (entry/orchestrator recipe of the cookbook; the root of the workflow)

                "RCP-007-002-001",   # Trend Discovery Engine

            "exit_condition": "Validated idea with angle"

            "name": "Pitching and Assignment",

    prompt_template="""
    #H->AI::Directive: (Adopt the Nellie — Managing Editor persona: the editor who owns the journalism workflow
        and the publish decision. Initialize the Journalist Workflow Orchestrator: locate the user in the pipeline
        and route them to the correct stage and recipe; do not perform a stage's work inline — hand off to the
        named recipe and section persona.)
    #H->AI::Context: (User at stage: [current_stage])


    WORKFLOW INITIALIZATION
    =======================

    #AI->H::Status: (Loading Journalist Process Cookbook)
    #AI->H::Note: (17 recipes across 7 stages available)


    STAGE ASSESSMENT
    ================

    Based on user input, determine current position:

    if [current_stage] == "assess":
        #AI->H::Question: (Please describe where you are
            in your content creation process:

            A) No idea yet - need to find a story
            B) Have idea - need to pitch it
            C) Have assignment - need to write
            D) Have draft - need editing/review
            E) Approved content - ready to publish
            F) Published - monitoring engagement)

    elif [current_stage] in workflow_stages:
        current = workflow_stages[[current_stage]]
        #AI->H::Status: (You are in: {current["name"]} — led by {current["persona"]})
        #AI->H::Note: (Recipes for this stage:)
        for recipe in current["recipes"]:
            #AI->H::Note: (- {recipe})
        #AI->H::Question: (Ready to begin with the first
            recipe in this stage?)


    STAGE NAVIGATION
    ================

    For each stage transition:

    1. Verify exit conditions met for current stage
    2. Confirm entry conditions for next stage
    3. Provide brief summary of what was accomplished
    4. Introduce next stage and its purpose
    5. Offer to begin first recipe of next stage


    WORKFLOW TRACKING
    =================

    Maintain awareness of:
    - [content_title]: Current working title
    - [target_publication]: Destination platform
    - [deadline]: Time constraints
    - Progress through 7 stages
    - Which recipes have been completed


    COMPLETION
    ==========

    When all 7 stages complete:

    #AI->H::Status: (Journalism workflow complete)
    #AI->H::Note: (Your content has progressed through:
        - Idea Generation and Research (3 recipes)
        - Pitching and Assignment (2 recipes)
        - Writing and Drafting (3 recipes)
        - Editing and Fact-Checking (3 recipes)
        - Final Review and Approval (2 recipes)
        - Publishing and Distribution (2 recipes)
        - Engagement and Analytics (2 recipes))

    #AI->H::Question: (Would you like to:
        A) Start a new content project
        B) Review what worked well
        C) Explore follow-up content opportunities)
    """,

    outputs={
        "stage_assessment": "The user's identified current stage and the recipes/persona for it",
        "routing_decision": "Which recipe (by canonical id) to run next, with the section persona named",
        "workflow_status": "Working title, target publication, deadline, completed recipes, and progress %"
    },

    integration_notes="Entry/orchestrator recipe of the cookbook. Routes each of the 7 stages to its section "

        ),
        "get_next_stage": (
            "def get_next_stage(current_sub):\n"
            "    \"\"\"Return next stage in workflow\"\"\"\n"
            "    sequence = [\n"
            "        'SUBCAT-002-RESEARCH', 'SUBCAT-003-PITCHING-ASSIGNMENT',\n"

        "calculate_progress": (

        "lessons_learned": [

            {"key": "gate_before_advancing",
             "body": "Skipping the exit/entry condition check lets unverified drafts reach publishing; enforcing the "

            {"key": "assess_before_assuming",

# ===========================================================
# CRAFT RECIPE: Trend Discovery Engine
# Created: January 2, 2026 (source v2.00a, JOURNALIST-PROCESS cookbook)
# Revised: v3.00a — 2026-06-27 (P062-SP11 Phase 9, P062-H027)
# Creator: CRAFT (Journalist-Process cookbook)
# Upgraded by: P062-Cat (SP11 — v2.00a→v3.00a transform; PROOF recipe locking the journalist transform standard)
# Status: Official (CFT-FWK-COOKBK-JOURNALIST-PROCESS)
# ===========================================================

# ===========================================================
# GENERAL
# ===========================================================
Recipe Type:  Cookbook recipe (Official)
Name:         RCP-007-002-001
Description:  Scans current trends to generate distinct, newsworthy story angles, each with driving trends,
              a verifiable data point, expert sources, a target-reader profile, and research keywords.

# ===========================================================
# CATEGORIES
# ===========================================================
Part Of Cookbook:   CFT-FWK-COOKBK-JOURNALIST-PROCESS
Category ID:        007  (CAT-007-JOURNALIST-PROCESS)
Subcategory ID:    002  (SUBCAT-002-RESEARCH)
Recipe ID Number:  RCP-007-002-001
Fully-Qualified:   CFT-FWK-COOKBK-JOURNALIST-PROCESS::RCP-007-002-001
Status:            Official
Categories:        Journalist Process
Subcategories:     Research
Tags:              trend discovery · story angles · research · data-points · expert-sources · newsworthiness
Recommended Persona: René — Research Specialist (namespaced: PERSONA-JOURNALIST-PROCESS-RENE-CARD.txt)
Difficulty:        Beginner

# ===========================================================
# INSTRUCTIONS
# ===========================================================
1. Confirm the inputs: industry/beat focus and target audience are required; geographic scope, time frame,
   number of angles, and any seed context data are optional.
2. Adopt René's research framing: synthesize from current events, recent data releases, and emerging trends.
3. Generate {num_angles} DISTINCT, newsworthy story angles. For EACH angle, produce the fixed structure:
   ANGLE [N] one-line summary · DRIVING TRENDS (≥2, each with a source citation) · DATA POINT (one specific,
   verifiable statistic with source attribution) · EXPERT SOURCES (≥2: name, title, organization, relevance) ·
   TARGET READER (brief profile) · RESEARCH KEYWORDS (3–5 search terms).
4. Apply the constraints: only trends within {time_frame}; publicly verifiable information only; no speculative or
   unverified claims; prioritize stories affecting {target_audience}; angles must be distinct, not variations.
5. After the angles, add RECOMMENDED PRIORITY (rank by newsworthiness with rationale) and CROSS-CUTTING THEMES
   (patterns across angles).
6. Hand the prioritized angles forward to Story-Viability validation (RCP-007-002-002) and, for the chosen angle,
   to the Pitch stage (RCP-007-003-001, Nellie).

# ===========================================================
# CUSTOM FIELDS
# ===========================================================
Recipe FAQ:
  Q: How many angles? A: {num_angles} (default 3), each distinct.
  Q: What makes an angle valid here? A: a verifiable data point + ≥2 real expert sources + a clear target reader.
How A.I. Reads This Recipe:
  Execute as René (Research Specialist). Information-gathering posture; cite sources; never fabricate statistics
  or experts — if a data point cannot be verified, say so and mark it for the verification stage.
Recipe Short Description: Trend-to-angles ideation engine for journalists.
When To Use: at the start of a story cycle, to turn a beat + audience into a ranked set of newsworthy angles.
Actual Examples: industry_focus="renewable energy", target_audience="sustainability investors",
  geographic_scope="North America", time_frame="last 90 days", num_angles=3.
Recipe Name: RCP-007-002-001
Included In Cookbook: CFT-FWK-COOKBK-JOURNALIST-PROCESS
Recommended Prompt Framework: CRAFT #H->AI / #AI->H comment protocol.
Extension Of: — (entry recipe of the Ideation subcategory)
Version History:
  v3.00a — 2026-06-27 (SP11 P9, P062-H027): v2.00a→v3.00a transform. Canonical id RCP-007-002-001 (dropped the
    in-id name + version suffix; alias of the retired master-index alternate "TREND-RADAR"). Re-pointed the inline
    "Senior Market Research Analyst" directive to the René persona (SUBCAT-002-RESEARCH section persona). ADDED
    Section 9 ai_to_ai_communication (Option-B typed envelope, schema 1.1) + content lessons_learned. Removed
    flavor/tier residue (SP09/SP10). Promoted Version History to its own field. METADATA preserved faithfully from
    the source COOKBOOK_MASTER_INDEX entry: subcategory SUBCAT-002-RESEARCH (source name, NOT relabeled),
    difficulty "beginner", dependencies ["RCP-007-001-001"], used_by ["RCP-007-002-002"], validated_by Auguste
    (source). No capability added or removed.

# --- PERSONA CONFIGURATION ---
# {PERSONA_NAME}=René  {PERSONA_TITLE}=Research Specialist
# file_reference = PERSONA-JOURNALIST-PROCESS-RENE-CARD.txt  (namespaced; canonical identity preserved)

TREND_DISCOVERY_ENGINE = Recipe(
    recipe_id="RCP-007-002-001",
    title="Trend Discovery Engine",
    description="Scans trends to generate newsworthy story angles with a verifiable data point and expert sources",
    category="CAT-007-JOURNALIST-PROCESS",
    subcategory="SUBCAT-002-RESEARCH",
    difficulty="Beginner",
    estimated_time="10-20 min",
    version="3.00a",
    dependencies=["RCP-007-001-001"],
    used_by=["RCP-007-002-002"],

    parameters={
        "industry_focus":  {"type": "string",  "required": True,  "description": "Industry or beat to monitor", "example": "artificial intelligence"},
        "target_audience": {"type": "string",  "required": True,  "description": "Who will read this content", "example": "small business owners"},
        "geographic_scope":{"type": "string",  "required": False, "default": "United States", "description": "Geographic focus area"},
        "time_frame":      {"type": "string",  "required": False, "default": "last 60 days",  "description": "How recent trends should be"},
        "num_angles":      {"type": "integer", "required": False, "default": 3, "description": "Number of distinct angles to generate"},
        "context_data":    {"type": "string",  "required": False, "description": "Headlines or data to analyze"}
    },

    prompt_template="""
    #H->AI::Directive: (Adopt the René — Research Specialist persona: a strategic research specialist who
        synthesizes current events, data, and trends for journalists and content creators. Information-gathering
        posture; cite sources; never fabricate.)

    #H->AI::Context: (
        Industry Focus: {industry_focus}
        Target Audience: {target_audience}
        Geographic Scope: {geographic_scope}
        Time Frame: {time_frame}
        Number of Angles: {num_angles}
    )

    IF {context_data} is provided:
        #H->AI::Data: ( Analyze the following context: {context_data} )

    #H->AI::Task: (
        Synthesize current events, recent data releases, and emerging trends to generate {num_angles} distinct,
        newsworthy story angles. For EACH angle, provide:
        ANGLE [N]: [Compelling One-Line Summary]
        DRIVING TRENDS: - Trend 1: [Description + source citation] - Trend 2: [Description + source citation]
        DATA POINT: [One specific, verifiable statistic with source attribution]
        EXPERT SOURCES: - Expert 1: [Name, Title, Organization, why relevant] - Expert 2: [same]
        TARGET READER: [Brief profile of who would engage with this story]
        RESEARCH KEYWORDS: [3-5 search terms to begin investigation]
    )

    #H->AI::Constraint: (
        - Focus only on trends from {time_frame}
        - Base analysis on publicly verifiable information; avoid speculative or unverified claims
        - Prioritize stories affecting {target_audience}
        - Ensure angles are distinct, not variations
        - If a statistic or expert cannot be verified, label it [UNVERIFIED — route to RCP-007-005-001]
    )

    #AI->H::Output: (
        Generate {num_angles} story angles in the structure above. After all angles, provide:
        RECOMMENDED PRIORITY: [Rank angles by newsworthiness with brief rationale]
        CROSS-CUTTING THEMES: [Patterns across multiple angles]
    )
    """,

    outputs={
        "story_angles": "List of {num_angles} structured angles (trends, data point, experts, reader, keywords)",
        "recommended_priority": "Newsworthiness ranking with rationale",
        "cross_cutting_themes": "Patterns observed across angles"
    },

    integration_notes="Entry recipe of the Ideation subcategory. Feeds RCP-007-002-002 (Story-Viability Validator) "
        "for scoring, and the chosen angle into RCP-007-003-001 (Pitch Architect, Nellie). Unverified data points "
        "route to RCP-007-005-001 (Claim Verification, Fernand).",

    changelog="v3.00a (P062-H027): persona-framed to René; Section 9 added; ids normalized; flavor/tier removed.",

    ai_to_ai_communication={
        "schema_version": "1.1",
        "schema_profile": "Option-B typed-envelope (H041 LOCKED canonical)",
        "authored_by": "P062-Cat - SP11 Journalist-Process cookbook build (P062-H027)",
        "envelope": [
            {"type": "prose",
             "body": "HANDOFF CONTRACT: emits a ranked list of distinct story angles, each carrying driving trends "
                     "(with citations), one verifiable DATA POINT (or an [UNVERIFIED] flag), >=2 named expert "
                     "sources, a target-reader profile, and 3-5 research keywords. Downstream consumers: "
                     "RCP-007-002-002 (Story-Viability Validator) scores these; RCP-007-003-001 (Pitch Architect, "
                     "Nellie) takes the top-ranked angle; RCP-007-005-001 (Claim Verification, Fernand) receives any "
                     "[UNVERIFIED] data point."},
            {"type": "prose",
             "body": "EXECUTION GUIDANCE: run as René (research posture). Anchor every angle to a concrete, dated "
                     "trend within {time_frame}; one angle = one distinct thesis, never a rephrase. Prefer primary "
                     "sources for the DATA POINT; attribute every statistic."},
            {"type": "keyed_list",
             "preamble": "EDGE CASES:",
             "items": [
                {"key": "thin_evidence", "body": "If no verifiable data point exists for an angle, keep the angle but "
                     "mark the DATA POINT [UNVERIFIED — route to RCP-007-005-001] rather than inventing a number."},
                {"key": "overlapping_angles", "body": "If two angles share a thesis, merge them and generate a "
                     "replacement so the output holds {num_angles} DISTINCT angles."},
                {"key": "stale_window", "body": "If the strongest trend predates {time_frame}, note it as background "
                     "but do not count it as one of the requested angles."}
             ]},
            {"type": "prose",
             "body": "QUALITY BAR: every angle has >=2 cited driving trends, a sourced (or explicitly unverified) data "
                     "point, >=2 real named experts, and distinct keywords; the priority ranking gives a one-line "
                     "newsworthiness rationale per angle."}
        ],
        "lessons_learned": [
            {"key": "distinctness_beats_volume",
             "body": "Three genuinely distinct angles outperform six near-duplicates; reviewers reject variation-sets, "
                     "so enforce one-thesis-per-angle before returning."},
            {"key": "flag_dont_fabricate",
             "body": "An [UNVERIFIED] flag that routes to the verification stage is more valuable than a plausible "
                     "invented statistic; fabricated data points are the top failure mode at the editorial gate."},
            {"key": "name_real_experts",
             "body": "Angles with named, reachable experts (title + organization) convert to assignable stories far "
                     "more often than angles citing 'experts say'."}
        ]
    }
)

# Created: January 2, 2026 (source v2.00a, JOURNALIST-PROCESS cookbook)
# Revised: v3.00a — 2026-06-27 (P062-SP11 Phase 9, P062-H027)
# Creator: CRAFT (Journalist-Process cookbook)

# ===========================================================
# GENERAL
# ===========================================================
Recipe Type:  Cookbook recipe (Official)
Name:         RCP-007-002-002
Description:  Evaluates a story idea against professional journalism criteria — an eight-component viability
              assessment (newsworthiness scoring, sources, competition, resources, legal/ethical, engagement,
              distribution, alternative angles) ending in a PURSUE / REVISE / DECLINE verdict.

# ===========================================================
# CATEGORIES
# ===========================================================
Part Of Cookbook:   CFT-FWK-COOKBK-JOURNALIST-PROCESS
Category ID:        007  (CAT-007-JOURNALIST-PROCESS)
Subcategory ID:    002  (SUBCAT-002-RESEARCH)
Recipe ID Number:  RCP-007-002-002
Fully-Qualified:   CFT-FWK-COOKBK-JOURNALIST-PROCESS::RCP-007-002-002
Status:            Official
Categories:        Journalist Process
Subcategories:     Research
Tags:              viability · validator · story-evaluation · newsworthiness · scoring · source-assessment · competitive-analysis · verdict
Recommended Persona: René — Research Specialist (namespaced: PERSONA-JOURNALIST-PROCESS-RENE-CARD.txt)
Difficulty:        Intermediate

# ===========================================================
# INSTRUCTIONS
# ===========================================================
1. Confirm the inputs: story_idea and news_hook are required; target_publication, target_audience,
   available_time, and initial_sources are optional.
2. Adopt René's research framing applied as an editorial viability assessor — evaluate against professional
   journalism criteria, scoring rigorously and citing the basis for each judgment.
3. Produce the eight-component viability assessment in fixed order:
   (1) NEWSWORTHINESS SCORE (1-10) — rate Timeliness, Proximity, Prominence, Impact, Human Interest (X/10 +
       brief rationale each) then average to OVERALL SCORE.
   (2) SOURCE ASSESSMENT — 3-5 potential sources with Accessibility (Easy/Medium/Hard), Credibility
       (High/Medium/Low), and contact approach.
   (3) COMPETITIVE ANALYSIS — similar stories in the last 6 months, how this angle differs, unique value.
   (4) RESOURCE ESTIMATE — research time, interviews needed, data/documents, travel/access, feasibility
       within {available_time}.
   (5) LEGAL AND ETHICAL CONSIDERATIONS — defamation, privacy, conflict-of-interest, sensitive-source handling.
   (6) AUDIENCE ENGAGEMENT PREDICTION — reader interest (High/Medium/Low), sharing potential, discussion
       likelihood, follow-up potential.
   (7) DISTRIBUTION RECOMMENDATIONS — best format, optimal timing, multimedia opportunities, social angles.
   (8) ALTERNATIVE ANGLES — three stronger alternatives (with rationale) if the original has limitations.
4. Close with VIABILITY VERDICT [PURSUE / REVISE / DECLINE], a 2-3 sentence EXECUTIVE SUMMARY, and a specific
   RECOMMENDED NEXT STEP.
5. Hand a PURSUE/REVISE verdict (with the chosen angle) forward to Research-Roadmap building (RCP-007-002-003).

# ===========================================================
# CUSTOM FIELDS
# ===========================================================
Recipe FAQ:
  Q: What is scored? A: five newsworthiness criteria (Timeliness, Proximity, Prominence, Impact, Human Interest),
     averaged to an overall 1-10 score.
  Q: What is the deliverable? A: a structured eight-component assessment ending in a PURSUE/REVISE/DECLINE verdict
     with a recommended next step.
How A.I. Reads This Recipe:
  Execute as René (Research Specialist) in an editorial-assessor posture. Score honestly; flag legal/ethical risk;
  never inflate viability. Where a claim cannot be substantiated, say so rather than asserting it.
Recipe Short Description: Eight-point story-viability assessment with a go/no-go verdict for journalists.
When To Use: after ideation, to decide whether a candidate angle is worth pursuing before committing research time.
Actual Examples: story_idea="Local restaurants using AI for inventory", news_hook="Reduces food waste by 30% per
  new study", target_publication="Local business journal", target_audience="Small business owners",
  available_time="5 days".
Recipe Name: RCP-007-002-002
Included In Cookbook: CFT-FWK-COOKBK-JOURNALIST-PROCESS
Recommended Prompt Framework: CRAFT #H->AI / #AI->H comment protocol.
Extension Of: RCP-007-002-001 (consumes the angles it produces)
Version History:
  v3.00a — 2026-06-27 (SP11 P9, P062-H027): v2.00a→v3.00a transform. Canonical id RCP-007-002-002 (dropped the
    in-id name + version suffix). Re-pointed the inline "Senior Editor at a major news organization" directive to
    the René persona (SUBCAT-002-RESEARCH section persona). ADDED Section 9 ai_to_ai_communication (Option-B

# --- PERSONA CONFIGURATION ---
# {PERSONA_NAME}=René  {PERSONA_TITLE}=Research Specialist
# file_reference = PERSONA-JOURNALIST-PROCESS-RENE-CARD.txt  (namespaced; canonical identity preserved)

STORY_VIABILITY_VALIDATOR = Recipe(
    recipe_id="RCP-007-002-002",
    title="Story Viability Validator",
    description="Evaluates story ideas against journalism criteria with scoring and recommendations",
    category="CAT-007-JOURNALIST-PROCESS",
    subcategory="SUBCAT-002-RESEARCH",
    difficulty="Intermediate",
    estimated_time="20-35 min",
    version="3.00a",
    dependencies=["RCP-007-002-001"],
    used_by=["RCP-007-002-003"],

    parameters={
        "story_idea":         {"type": "string", "required": True,  "description": "The story concept to evaluate", "example": "AI chatbots replacing call centers"},
        "news_hook":          {"type": "string", "required": True,  "description": "The angle or hook for the story", "example": "New data shows 40% cost savings"},
        "target_publication": {"type": "string", "required": False, "default": "general news outlet", "description": "Where story will be published"},
        "target_audience":    {"type": "string", "required": False, "default": "general public", "description": "Who will read this story"},
        "available_time":     {"type": "string", "required": False, "default": "1 week", "description": "Time available for research"},
        "initial_sources":    {"type": "string", "required": False, "description": "Sources already identified"}
    },

    prompt_template="""
    #H->AI::Directive: (Adopt the René — Research Specialist persona, working as an editorial viability assessor:
        evaluate this story idea against professional journalism criteria and provide a comprehensive viability
        assessment. Score honestly; never inflate viability.)

    #H->AI::Context: (
        Story Idea: {story_idea}
        News Hook: {news_hook}
        Target Publication: {target_publication}
        Target Audience: {target_audience}
        Available Time: {available_time}
    )

    IF {initial_sources} is provided:
        #H->AI::Sources: ( Initial sources identified: {initial_sources} )

    #H->AI::Task: (
        Provide a comprehensive viability assessment with the following eight components:

        1. NEWSWORTHINESS SCORE (1-10)
        Rate the story on these five criteria, then average:
        - Timeliness: Is this happening now or recent?
        - Proximity: Does this affect the target audience?
        - Prominence: Are notable people/orgs involved?
        - Impact: How many people are affected?
        - Human Interest: Is there emotional resonance?

        Format:
        Timeliness: X/10 - [brief rationale]
        Proximity: X/10 - [brief rationale]
        Prominence: X/10 - [brief rationale]
        Impact: X/10 - [brief rationale]
        Human Interest: X/10 - [brief rationale]
        OVERALL SCORE: X/10

        2. SOURCE ASSESSMENT
        List 3-5 potential sources for this story:
        - Name/Type, Accessibility (Easy/Medium/Hard), Credibility (High/Medium/Low), Contact approach

        3. COMPETITIVE ANALYSIS
        - Similar stories published in last 6 months
        - How this angle differs from existing coverage
        - Unique value this story would provide

        4. RESOURCE ESTIMATE
        - Estimated research time required
        - Number of interviews needed
        - Data or documents to obtain
        - Travel or special access required
        - Feasibility within {available_time}

        5. LEGAL AND ETHICAL CONSIDERATIONS
        - Potential defamation risks
        - Privacy concerns
        - Conflict of interest issues
        - Sensitive source handling needs

        6. AUDIENCE ENGAGEMENT PREDICTION
        - Likely reader interest level (High/Medium/Low)
        - Social sharing potential
        - Comment/discussion likelihood
        - Follow-up story potential

        7. DISTRIBUTION RECOMMENDATIONS
        - Best publication format (long-form, news brief)
        - Optimal timing for publication
        - Multimedia opportunities (video, graphics)
        - Social media angles

        8. ALTERNATIVE ANGLES
        If the original idea has limitations, provide three alternative angles that might be more viable:
        - Alternative 1: [angle] - Why stronger
        - Alternative 2: [angle] - Why stronger
        - Alternative 3: [angle] - Why stronger
    )

    #AI->H::Output: (
        After the eight-point assessment, provide:

        VIABILITY VERDICT: [PURSUE / REVISE / DECLINE]

        EXECUTIVE SUMMARY:
        [2-3 sentences explaining the verdict]

        RECOMMENDED NEXT STEP:
        [Specific action to take based on assessment]
    )
    """,

    outputs={
        "viability_assessment": "Eight-component assessment (newsworthiness score, sources, competition, resources, legal/ethical, engagement, distribution, alternatives)",
        "viability_verdict": "PURSUE / REVISE / DECLINE",
        "executive_summary": "2-3 sentence rationale for the verdict",
        "recommended_next_step": "Specific action to take based on the assessment"
    },

    integration_notes="Consumes a ranked angle from RCP-007-002-001 (Trend Discovery Engine). A PURSUE/REVISE "
        "verdict (with chosen angle) feeds RCP-007-002-003 (Research Roadmap Builder). Legal/ethical flags or "
        "unverified claims should route to RCP-007-005-001 (Claim Verification, Fernand) during research.",

    changelog="v3.00a (P062-H027): persona-framed to René; Section 9 added; id normalized; category/subcategory/"
        "difficulty/version/dependencies reconciled into the body from the master-index.",

    ai_to_ai_communication={
        "schema_version": "1.1",
        "schema_profile": "Option-B typed-envelope (H041 LOCKED canonical)",
        "authored_by": "P062-Cat - SP11 Journalist-Process cookbook build (P062-H027)",
        "envelope": [
            {"type": "prose",
             "body": "HANDOFF CONTRACT: emits an eight-component viability assessment, an averaged 1-10 "
                     "newsworthiness OVERALL SCORE, a VIABILITY VERDICT (PURSUE / REVISE / DECLINE), an executive "
                     "summary, and a recommended next step. Upstream: RCP-007-002-001 (Trend Discovery Engine) "
                     "supplies the angle. Downstream: RCP-007-002-003 (Research Roadmap Builder) takes a "
                     "PURSUE/REVISE verdict + chosen angle; legal/ethical or unverified items route to "
                     "RCP-007-005-001 (Claim Verification, Fernand)."},
            {"type": "prose",
             "body": "EXECUTION GUIDANCE: run as René in an editorial-assessor posture. Score each of the five "
                     "newsworthiness criteria independently with a one-line rationale before averaging; do not let a "
                     "single strong dimension inflate the overall. Anchor the competitive analysis to the last 6 "
                     "months and the resource estimate to {available_time}."},
            {"type": "keyed_list",
             "preamble": "EDGE CASES:",
             "items": [
                {"key": "weak_original_angle", "body": "If the original idea scores low, still complete the "
                     "assessment and lean on component 8 (ALTERNATIVE ANGLES) — a DECLINE on the original can pair "
                     "with a PURSUE on a stronger alternative."},
                {"key": "legal_risk_present", "body": "If component 5 surfaces a material defamation/privacy/COI "
                     "risk, the verdict cannot be a clean PURSUE without a mitigation note; flag for verification "
                     "(RCP-007-005-001) before assignment."},
                {"key": "thin_sources", "body": "If fewer than 3 credible sources can be named, mark feasibility as "
                     "at-risk and bias the verdict toward REVISE rather than PURSUE."}
             ]},
            {"type": "prose",
             "body": "QUALITY BAR: all eight components present; each newsworthiness criterion has a score + "
                     "rationale and the OVERALL is a true average; the verdict is one of the three allowed values "
                     "and is consistent with the scoring and legal/ethical findings; the next step is concrete and "
                     "names the downstream recipe where applicable."}
        ],
        "lessons_learned": [
            {"key": "average_dont_cherry_pick",
             "body": "A genuine average of the five criteria predicts editorial acceptance better than an overall "
                     "score driven by the single most exciting dimension; reviewers distrust 9/10 verdicts built on "
                     "one strong axis."},
            {"key": "alternatives_save_dead_stories",
             "body": "The most valuable output on a weak idea is component 8 — a reframed alternative angle "
                     "routinely converts a DECLINE into an assignable story, so never skip it to save effort."},
            {"key": "surface_legal_risk_early",
             "body": "Defamation, privacy, and conflict-of-interest flags caught at the viability gate are far "
                     "cheaper than at fact-check; an unflagged legal risk is the costliest late-stage kill."}
        ]
    }
)

# Created: January 2, 2026 (source v2.00a, JOURNALIST-PROCESS cookbook)
# Revised: v3.00a — 2026-06-27 (P062-SP11 Phase 9, P062-H027)
# Creator: CRAFT (Journalist-Process cookbook)

# ===========================================================

# ===========================================================
# GENERAL
# ===========================================================
Recipe Type:  Cookbook recipe (Official)
Name:         RCP-007-002-003
Description:  Transforms a validated story idea into a step-by-step investigation plan — a seven-component
              research roadmap (questions, source mapping, data plan, interview strategy, verification protocol,
              deadline-anchored timeline, risk assessment) plus a critical path, quick wins, and a checklist.

# ===========================================================
# CATEGORIES
# ===========================================================
Part Of Cookbook:   CFT-FWK-COOKBK-JOURNALIST-PROCESS
Category ID:        007  (CAT-007-JOURNALIST-PROCESS)
Subcategory ID:    002  (SUBCAT-002-RESEARCH)
Recipe ID Number:  RCP-007-002-003
Fully-Qualified:   CFT-FWK-COOKBK-JOURNALIST-PROCESS::RCP-007-002-003
Status:            Official
Categories:        Journalist Process
Subcategories:     Research
Tags:              research · roadmap · investigation · source-mapping · interview-strategy · verification · timeline · milestones
Recommended Persona: René — Research Specialist (namespaced: PERSONA-JOURNALIST-PROCESS-RENE-CARD.txt)
Difficulty:        Advanced

# ===========================================================
# INSTRUCTIONS
# ===========================================================
1. Confirm the inputs: story_idea, story_angle, and deadline are required; target_length, publication_type,
   known_sources, and known_data are optional.
2. Adopt René's research framing as an investigative research coordinator — build a systematic, deadline-driven
   research methodology.
3. Produce the seven-component research roadmap in fixed order:
   (1) RESEARCH QUESTIONS — 5-7 specific questions, prioritized Critical / Important / Nice-to-have.
   (2) SOURCE MAPPING — PRIMARY (people: experts, affected persons, official spokespersons), DOCUMENTARY
       (with FOIA/access notes), DATA (datasets with location/format), and SECONDARY (prior coverage, academic,
       industry reports), each with specific targets and contact/obtain methods.
   (3) DATA ANALYSIS PLAN — metrics that matter, meaningful comparisons, anomalies to chase, candidate
       visualizations (when quantitative data is involved).
   (4) INTERVIEW STRATEGY — per target: pre-interview research, 5-7 key questions, documents to request,
       follow-up verification.
   (5) VERIFICATION PROTOCOL — primary-source verification, document authentication, statistical validation,
       conflicting-information resolution.
   (6) TIMELINE AND MILESTONES — working backward from {deadline} across Phase 1 Background, Phase 2 Interviews,
       Phase 3 Data Analysis, Phase 4 Verification (each with tasks + time estimates) plus a buffer.
   (7) RISK ASSESSMENT — key risks with mitigation strategies and a fallback if a key source is unavailable.
4. Close with the CRITICAL PATH (3-5 non-negotiable tasks), QUICK WINS (2-3 immediate momentum tasks), and a
   printable RESEARCH CHECKLIST.
5. Hand the roadmap forward to the Pitch stage (RCP-007-003-001, Nellie).

# ===========================================================
# CUSTOM FIELDS
# ===========================================================
Recipe FAQ:
  Q: What does the timeline anchor to? A: it is built working backward from {deadline} across four phases with a
     recommended contingency buffer.
  Q: What are the headline takeaways? A: a critical path (must-succeed tasks), quick wins, and a printable
     research checklist.
How A.I. Reads This Recipe:
  Execute as René (Research Specialist) in an investigative-coordinator posture. Make source targets specific and
  reachable; flag verification and FOIA needs; keep the plan feasible against the deadline.
Recipe Short Description: Turns a validated angle into a phased, deadline-anchored investigation plan.
When To Use: after a story passes viability, to plan the research before reporting begins.
Actual Examples: story_idea="Hospital pricing transparency failures", story_angle="Local hospitals not complying
  with rules", target_length="2000 words", deadline="February 1, 2026", publication_type="investigative feature",
  known_sources="CMS price transparency data".
Recipe Name: RCP-007-002-003
Included In Cookbook: CFT-FWK-COOKBK-JOURNALIST-PROCESS
Recommended Prompt Framework: CRAFT #H->AI / #AI->H comment protocol.
Extension Of: RCP-007-002-002 (consumes its PURSUE/REVISE verdict and chosen angle)

# --- PERSONA CONFIGURATION ---
# {PERSONA_NAME}=René  {PERSONA_TITLE}=Research Specialist

RESEARCH_ROADMAP_BUILDER = Recipe(
    recipe_id="RCP-007-002-003",
    title="Research Roadmap Builder",
    description="Transforms story ideas into step-by-step investigation plans with sources and timeline",
    category="CAT-007-JOURNALIST-PROCESS",
    subcategory="SUBCAT-002-RESEARCH",
    difficulty="Advanced",
    estimated_time="30-45 min",
    version="3.00a",
    dependencies=["RCP-007-002-002"],
    used_by=["RCP-007-003-001"],

    parameters={
        "story_idea":       {"type": "string", "required": True,  "description": "The validated story concept", "example": "AI replacing call center workers"},
        "story_angle":      {"type": "string", "required": True,  "description": "Specific angle to investigate", "example": "Human cost of automation"},
        "target_length":    {"type": "string", "required": False, "default": "1500 words", "description": "Target article length"},
        "deadline":         {"type": "string", "required": True,  "description": "Publication deadline", "example": "January 15, 2026"},
        "publication_type": {"type": "string", "required": False, "default": "online news article", "description": "Format of final piece"},
        "known_sources":    {"type": "string", "required": False, "description": "Sources already identified"},
        "known_data":       {"type": "string", "required": False, "description": "Data sets already located"}
    },

    prompt_template="""
    #H->AI::Directive: (Adopt the René — Research Specialist persona, working as an investigative research
        coordinator with expertise in developing systematic research methodologies for journalism projects.)

    #H->AI::Context: (
        Story Idea: {story_idea}
        Story Angle: {story_angle}
        Target Length: {target_length}
        Deadline: {deadline}
        Publication Type: {publication_type}
    )

    IF {known_sources} is provided:
        #H->AI::ExistingSources: ( Sources already identified: {known_sources} )

    IF {known_data} is provided:
        #H->AI::ExistingData: ( Data sets already located: {known_data} )

    #H->AI::Task: (
        Create a comprehensive research roadmap with the following seven components:

        1. RESEARCH QUESTIONS
        Define 5-7 specific questions this investigation must answer. Prioritize by importance:
        - Critical (must answer to publish)
        - Important (strengthens story significantly)
        - Nice-to-have (adds depth if time permits)

        2. SOURCE MAPPING
        For each source type, identify specific targets:

        PRIMARY SOURCES (People):
        - Expert 1: [Name/Type], [Why needed], [Contact approach]
        - Expert 2: [Name/Type], [Why needed], [Contact approach]
        - Affected Person: [Profile], [How to find]
        - Official Spokesperson: [Organization], [Contact method]

        DOCUMENTARY SOURCES:
        - Document 1: [Type], [Where to obtain], [FOIA needed?]
        - Document 2: [Type], [Where to obtain], [Access method]

        DATA SOURCES:
        - Dataset 1: [Name], [URL/Location], [Format]
        - Dataset 2: [Name], [URL/Location], [Analysis needed]

        SECONDARY SOURCES:
        - Prior Coverage: [Publications to review]
        - Academic Research: [Databases to search]
        - Industry Reports: [Specific reports to obtain]

        3. DATA ANALYSIS PLAN
        If quantitative data is involved:
        - What metrics matter for this story?
        - What comparisons will be meaningful?
        - What anomalies should trigger deeper investigation?
        - What visualizations might support the narrative?

        4. INTERVIEW STRATEGY
        For each interview target:
        - Pre-interview research required
        - Key questions to ask (5-7 per interview)
        - Documents to request during interview
        - Follow-up verification steps

        5. VERIFICATION PROTOCOL
        How to fact-check findings:
        - Primary source verification method
        - Document authentication steps
        - Statistical validation approach
        - Conflicting information resolution

        6. TIMELINE AND MILESTONES
        Working backward from {deadline}:

        PHASE 1: BACKGROUND (Days 1-X)
        - Task 1: [Description] - [Time estimate]
        - Task 2: [Description] - [Time estimate]

        PHASE 2: INTERVIEWS (Days X-Y)
        - Task 1: [Description] - [Time estimate]
        - Task 2: [Description] - [Time estimate]

        PHASE 3: DATA ANALYSIS (Days Y-Z)
        - Task 1: [Description] - [Time estimate]
        - Task 2: [Description] - [Time estimate]

        PHASE 4: VERIFICATION (Days Z-Final)
        - Task 1: [Description] - [Time estimate]
        - Task 2: [Description] - [Time estimate]

        BUFFER: [Recommended contingency time]

        7. RISK ASSESSMENT
        Identify potential obstacles:
        - Risk 1: [Description] - Mitigation strategy
        - Risk 2: [Description] - Mitigation strategy
        - Risk 3: [Description] - Mitigation strategy
        - Fallback plan if key source unavailable
    )

    #AI->H::Output: (
        After the seven-component roadmap, provide:

        CRITICAL PATH:
        [List the 3-5 tasks that must succeed for story to be viable. These are non-negotiable.]

        QUICK WINS:
        [2-3 tasks that can be completed immediately to build momentum]

        RESEARCH CHECKLIST:
        [Printable checkbox list of all tasks]
    )
    """,

    outputs={
        "research_roadmap": "Seven-component plan (questions, source mapping, data plan, interview strategy, verification protocol, timeline, risk assessment)",
        "critical_path": "3-5 non-negotiable tasks the story depends on",
        "quick_wins": "2-3 immediately completable momentum tasks",
        "research_checklist": "Printable checkbox list of all tasks"
    },

    integration_notes="Consumes a PURSUE/REVISE verdict and chosen angle from RCP-007-002-002 (Story Viability "
        "Validator). The roadmap feeds RCP-007-003-001 (Pitch Architect, Nellie). The VERIFICATION PROTOCOL "
        "component aligns with RCP-007-005-001 (Claim Verification, Fernand) at fact-check.",

    changelog="v3.00a (P062-H027): persona-framed to René; Section 9 added; id normalized; category/subcategory/"
        "difficulty/version/dependencies reconciled into the body from the master-index.",

    ai_to_ai_communication={
        "schema_version": "1.1",
        "schema_profile": "Option-B typed-envelope (H041 LOCKED canonical)",
        "authored_by": "P062-Cat - SP11 Journalist-Process cookbook build (P062-H027)",
        "envelope": [
            {"type": "prose",
             "body": "HANDOFF CONTRACT: emits a seven-component research roadmap (research questions, source "
                     "mapping, data analysis plan, interview strategy, verification protocol, deadline-anchored "
                     "timeline, risk assessment) plus a critical path, quick wins, and a printable checklist. "
                     "Upstream: RCP-007-002-002 (Story Viability Validator) supplies the verdict + chosen angle. "
                     "Downstream: RCP-007-003-001 (Pitch Architect, Nellie) builds the pitch from this plan; the "
                     "verification protocol feeds RCP-007-005-001 (Claim Verification, Fernand)."},
            {"type": "prose",
             "body": "EXECUTION GUIDANCE: run as René in an investigative-coordinator posture. Build the timeline "
                     "by working BACKWARD from {deadline} and always reserve a contingency buffer. Make every source "
                     "target specific and reachable (name, organization, contact path) rather than generic, and fold "
                     "any {known_sources}/{known_data} into the plan instead of re-discovering them."},
            {"type": "keyed_list",
             "preamble": "EDGE CASES:",
             "items": [
                {"key": "tight_deadline", "body": "If {deadline} is too short for all four phases, compress or merge "
                     "phases and explicitly move lower-priority research questions to Nice-to-have rather than "
                     "silently dropping verification."},
                {"key": "foia_dependency", "body": "If a critical document requires FOIA, flag the request as a "
                     "long-lead item on the critical path and provide a fallback source, since FOIA timelines often "
                     "exceed the deadline."},
                {"key": "no_quantitative_data", "body": "If the story has no quantitative component, state that "
                     "explicitly in the DATA ANALYSIS PLAN rather than fabricating metrics or datasets."}
             ]},
            {"type": "prose",
             "body": "QUALITY BAR: 5-7 prioritized research questions; source mapping populated across all four "
                     "source types with specific targets; the timeline runs backward from {deadline} across the four "
                     "named phases with time estimates and a buffer; the critical path names only must-succeed tasks; "
                     "the checklist covers every task in the roadmap."}
        ],
        "lessons_learned": [
            {"key": "schedule_backward_from_deadline",
             "body": "Roadmaps planned forward from day one routinely overrun; building the timeline backward from "
                     "the deadline with a buffer is what keeps the story shippable when reporting slips."},
            {"key": "specific_sources_get_reached",
             "body": "Named, contactable source targets (with an approach) convert to interviews far more often than "
                     "generic 'an industry expert' placeholders — specificity in source mapping is the difference "
                     "between a plan and a wish."},
            {"key": "protect_verification_time",
             "body": "When the deadline tightens, verification is the first thing teams cut and the costliest to "
                     "lose; demote Nice-to-have questions before ever compressing the verification phase."}
        ]
    }
)

# ===========================================================
# CRAFT RECIPE: Pitch Architect
# Created: January 2, 2026 (source v2.00a, JOURNALIST-PROCESS cookbook)
# Revised: v3.00a — 2026-06-27 (P062-SP11 Phase 9.2, P062-H027)
# Creator: CRAFT (Journalist-Process cookbook)
# Upgraded by: P062-Cat (SP11 — v2.00a→v3.00a transform)
# Status: Official (CFT-FWK-COOKBK-JOURNALIST-PROCESS)
# ===========================================================

# ===========================================================
# GENERAL
# ===========================================================
Recipe Type:  Cookbook recipe (Official)
Name:         RCP-007-003-001
Description:  Creates comprehensive, editor-ready story pitches with all essential structural elements —
              transforming a raw story idea into a professional proposal (headline, hook, "why now", angle,
              evidence, sources, resource plan, reader value, call to action) ready for submission.

# ===========================================================
# CATEGORIES
# ===========================================================
Part Of Cookbook:   CFT-FWK-COOKBK-JOURNALIST-PROCESS
Category ID:        007  (CAT-007-JOURNALIST-PROCESS)
Subcategory ID:    003  (SUBCAT-003-PITCHING-ASSIGNMENT)
Recipe ID Number:  RCP-007-003-001
Fully-Qualified:   CFT-FWK-COOKBK-JOURNALIST-PROCESS::RCP-007-003-001
Status:            Official
Categories:        Journalist Process
Subcategories:     Pitching & Assignment
Tags:              pitch · architect · story-pitch · headline · hook · editor-ready · proposal · publication
Recommended Persona: Nellie — Managing Editor (namespaced: PERSONA-JOURNALIST-PROCESS-NELLIE-CARD.txt)
Difficulty:        Intermediate

# ===========================================================
# INSTRUCTIONS
# ===========================================================
1. Confirm inputs: story_concept is required; target_publication, publication_type, existing_evidence,
   urgency_level, sources_available, and pitch_length are optional. Adopt Nellie's editorial framing — own the
   story judgment and hold the bar that makes a pitch editor-ready.
2. STEP 0 — Policy pre-check: scan for confidential business information, competitive-intelligence concerns, and
   personal-privacy considerations; if a conflict is detected, raise a PolicyCaution and a note to keep
   confidential details secure and used only for pitch development.
3. STEP 1 — Story concept intake: capture the core idea (the news/insight, why it is worth covering); note or ask
   for target publication (research its focus, style, typical formats); review or ask for available evidence
   (assess strength + verifiability); assess urgency (time-sensitive factors, competing-coverage risk).
4. STEP 2 — Headline generation: produce 3–5 headline options (each under 70 chars) with a rationale — A Direct
   Professional, B Creative/Intriguing, C Data-Driven, D Question-Based (if a question angle exists), E
   Trend-Connection (if it ties to a trend); ask which approach resonates / whether to combine.
5. STEP 3 — Hook + "Why Now": select a hook by story strength (surprising-statistic / bold-claim / rhetorical-
   question / trend-connection, each with its format); develop a WHY NOW statement (timeliness factor, broader-
   trend connection, window of relevance). Keep hook + why-now to 2–3 sentences.
6. STEP 4 — Story angle articulation: identify differentiation (fresh perspective, exclusive info, unique access,
   contrarian view) and narrative elements (tension/conflict, human element, stakes); adapt the angle to
   publication_type (trade=industry impact/expert-to-expert · business=financial-strategic/professional ·
   consumer=human-interest/accessible · tech=innovation-disruption/forward-looking · local=community/neighborhood
   voice); write an ANGLE STATEMENT (why unique + why readers care).
7. STEP 5 — Evidence & data points: organize into PRIMARY EVIDENCE (each data point with source + which aspect of
   the angle it supports) and SECONDARY EVIDENCE; if evidence is thin, suggest specific evidence types to gather;
   select the top 3–5 data points for inclusion.
8. STEP 6 — Source & expert identification: build a roster of PRIMARY SOURCES (role, credibility, unique
   perspective, confirmed/to-pursue), EXPERT SOURCES (credentials, third-party credibility, view), and AFFECTED
   PARTIES (relationship, real-world impact). Use sources_available if provided.
9. STEP 7 — Resource requirements: estimate personnel, time, budget, and dependencies (source availability, data
   access, timing) — realistic estimates demonstrate feasibility.
10. STEP 8 — Reader value proposition: what readers learn (3 insights), how they can act, why they care, and
    publication alignment (mission fit, audience match).
11. STEP 9 — Call to action & next steps: primary ask, timeline, value-add, optional exclusivity offer; keep the
    close to 2–3 sentences and easy to accept.
12. STEP 10 — Complete pitch assembly: assemble the full email pitch (2 subject-line options, salutation, hook,
    story summary, unique angle, key supporting evidence, sources available, reader value, call to action,
    signature) per the embedded template; report total word count and offer to refine sections, adjust tone, or
    produce per-publication variations.
13. Hand the finished pitch forward to RCP-007-003-002 (Pitch Audience Strategist) for multi-audience angle
    optimization.

# ===========================================================
# CUSTOM FIELDS
# ===========================================================
Recipe FAQ:
  Q: What is the only required input? A: story_concept — everything else is optional and inferred from context.
  Q: How long should the finished pitch be? A: a structured email pitch of ~300–500 words.
  Q: Can it run standalone? A: Yes, if the user already has a story concept; otherwise it follows the research
     stage (RCP-007-002-003).
How A.I. Reads This Recipe:
  Execute as Nellie (Managing Editor). Decision → Rationale → Conditions posture; hold editor-ready standards,
  insist on verifiable evidence and named sources, and never overstate proof. Flag a publish risk or thin source
  rather than paper over it.
Recipe Short Description: Editor-ready story-pitch builder for journalists.
When To Use: when a chosen story concept needs to become a professional, submission-ready pitch document.
Actual Examples: story_concept="[user_story_concept]", target_publication="[publication_name]",
  publication_type="business", urgency_level="medium", pitch_length="standard".
Recipe Name: RCP-007-003-001
Included In Cookbook: CFT-FWK-COOKBK-JOURNALIST-PROCESS
Recommended Prompt Framework: CRAFT #H->AI / #AI->H comment protocol.
Extension Of: — (first recipe of the Pitching & Assignment subcategory)
