# --- PERSONA CONFIGURATION ---
# {PERSONA_NAME}=Nellie  {PERSONA_TITLE}=Managing Editor
# file_reference = PERSONA-JOURNALIST-PROCESS-NELLIE-CARD.txt  (section persona; canonical identity preserved)

PITCH_ARCHITECT = Recipe(
    recipe_id="RCP-007-003-001",
    title="Pitch Architect",
    description="Creates comprehensive, editor-ready story pitches with all essential structural elements; "
        "transforms raw story ideas into professional proposals that meet editorial standards. Guides the user "
        "through headline creation, hook development, angle articulation, source identification, and resource "
        "planning to produce a complete pitch document ready for submission.",
    category="CAT-007-JOURNALIST-PROCESS",
    subcategory="SUBCAT-003-PITCHING-ASSIGNMENT",
    difficulty="Intermediate",
    estimated_time="30-45 minutes",
    version="3.00a",
    dependencies=["RCP-007-002-003"],
    used_by=["RCP-007-003-002"],

    parameters={
        "story_concept":      {"type": "string", "required": True,  "description": "Core story idea to pitch", "example": "[user_story_concept]"},
        "target_publication": {"type": "string", "required": False, "description": "Intended outlet for pitch", "example": "[publication_name]"},
        "publication_type":   {"type": "string", "required": False, "options": ["trade", "business", "consumer", "tech", "local", "national"], "description": "Category of target outlet", "default": "Determined from context"},
        "existing_evidence":  {"type": "list",   "required": False, "description": "Data or proof available", "example": ["statistics", "quotes", "case studies"]},
        "urgency_level":      {"type": "string", "required": False, "options": ["breaking", "high", "medium", "low"], "description": "Timeline pressure for story", "default": "medium"},
        "sources_available":  {"type": "list",   "required": False, "description": "People who can be quoted", "example": ["CEO", "customers", "experts"]},
        "pitch_length":       {"type": "string", "required": False, "options": ["brief", "standard", "comprehensive"], "description": "Desired pitch detail level", "default": "standard"}
    },

    prompt_template="""
    #H->AI::Directive: (Adopt the Nellie — Managing Editor persona: the editor who owns story judgment and
        editorial standards and turns a raw idea into an editor-ready pitch. Decision-first, standards-first;
        insist on verifiable evidence and named sources.)
    #H->AI::Context: (Creating a professional, submission-ready story pitch)

    # STEP 0: POLICY PRE-CHECK
    Scan the prompt for sensitive categories: confidential business information; competitive-intelligence
    concerns; personal-privacy considerations.
    IF potential conflict detected:
        #AI->H::PolicyCaution: (This pitch may involve sensitive business information)
        #AI->H::Note: (Keep confidential details secure and use only for pitch development)

    # STEP 1: STORY CONCEPT INTAKE
    #AI->H::Status: (Gathering story information)
    Story Concept: core idea {story_concept} — what is the news or insight, and what makes it worth covering?
    Target Publication:
        IF target_publication provided: note {target_publication}; research its focus, style, and typical formats.
        ELSE: #AI->H::Question: (What type of publication are you targeting — trade, business, consumer, tech,
            local, or national? Or a specific outlet?)
    Evidence Available:
        IF existing_evidence provided: review {existing_evidence}; assess strength and verifiability.
        ELSE: #AI->H::Question: (What evidence supports this story — data, statistics, quotes, case studies,
            documented results? Even preliminary evidence helps.)
    Urgency Assessment: urgency level {urgency_level}; time-sensitive factors; competing-coverage risk.
    #AI->H::Note: (Confirming understanding of the story concept before developing pitch structure)

    # STEP 2: HEADLINE GENERATION
    #AI->H::Status: (Creating headline options)
    Generate 3-5 headline options (each under 70 characters) with a rationale:
        Option A - Direct Professional: clear, straightforward appeal
        Option B - Creative/Intriguing: curiosity-driven engagement
        Option C - Data-Driven: evidence-first approach
        IF story has a question angle:  Option D - Question-Based: reader-engagement hook
        IF story connects to a trend:   Option E - Trend-Connection: timeliness emphasis
    #AI->H::Question: (Which headline approach resonates most, or should I combine elements?)

    # STEP 3: HOOK AND WHY NOW DEVELOPMENT
    #AI->H::Status: (Crafting opening hook)
    Select a hook by story strength:
        IF strong statistics: surprising-statistic hook -> "[Statistic] - and that changes everything for [audience]."
        IF bold claim supportable: bold-claim hook -> "[Bold statement]. Here is how we know."
        IF audience has a pressing question: rhetorical-question hook -> "[Question everyone is asking]? New evidence provides answers."
        IF timely connection exists: trend-connection hook -> "As [current event/trend], [story subject] reveals [insight]."
    WHY NOW STATEMENT: "[Story] matters now because: [timeliness factor 1] · [connection to broader trend] · [window of relevance]"
    #AI->H::Note: (Hook + Why Now total 2-3 sentences to hold editor attention)

    # STEP 4: STORY ANGLE ARTICULATION
    #AI->H::Status: (Defining unique angle)
    Differentiation: fresh perspective · exclusive information (if any) · unique access (if any) · contrarian view (if any).
    Narrative elements: tension/conflict · human element · stakes involved.
    Adapt angle for publication_type:
        trade    -> Focus: industry impact and implications;          Tone: expert to expert
        business -> Focus: financial or strategic significance;       Tone: professional, outcome-oriented
        consumer -> Focus: human interest and relatability;           Tone: accessible, engaging
        tech     -> Focus: innovation and disruption;                 Tone: forward-looking, analytical
        local    -> Focus: community connection and impact;           Tone: neighborhood voice, pride
    ANGLE STATEMENT: "This story is unique because [differentiation]. Readers will care because [relevance to them]."

    # STEP 5: EVIDENCE AND DATA POINTS
    #AI->H::Status: (Compiling supporting evidence)
    PRIMARY EVIDENCE (strongest proof) - for each: specific figure · Source: [verification source] · Supports: [which aspect of angle].
    SECONDARY EVIDENCE (supporting): additional facts/figures · trend data or context.
    IF evidence is limited:
        #AI->H::Suggestion: (To strengthen this pitch, consider gathering: [specific evidence types that would help])
    Select the top 3-5 data points for pitch inclusion.

    # STEP 6: SOURCE AND EXPERT IDENTIFICATION
    #AI->H::Status: (Identifying credible sources)
    IF sources_available provided: review {sources_available}; assess credibility and access.
    PRIMARY SOURCES (directly involved) - for each: Role/Title · Adds: [credibility element] · Perspective: [unique offer] · Status: [Confirmed/To pursue].
    EXPERT SOURCES (external validation) - for each: Credentials · Adds: [third-party credibility] · Perspective: [industry/academic, or contrarian/balancing view].
    AFFECTED PARTIES (human element): stakeholder · Relationship to story · Adds: [real-world impact illustration].

    # STEP 7: RESOURCE REQUIREMENTS
    #AI->H::Status: (Documenting execution needs)
    RESOURCE ESTIMATE:
        Personnel: writer/reporter (time) · photographer (if visual) · designer (if graphics) · editor (review time).
        Time: research · interviews (number + duration) · writing · review cycle · total timeline.
        Budget: travel (if required) · data/research (subscriptions/purchases) · visuals (photography, graphics).
        Dependencies: source availability · data access · timing factors (deadlines, events).
    #AI->H::Note: (Realistic resource estimates demonstrate feasibility and professionalism)

    # STEP 8: VALUE PROPOSITION FOR READERS
    #AI->H::Status: (Articulating reader benefit)
    READER VALUE STATEMENT:
        What readers learn: 3 specific takeaways.
        How readers can act: actionable application · decision support.
        Why readers care: connection to their interests · impact on their world.
        Publication alignment: mission fit · audience match.

    # STEP 9: CALL TO ACTION AND NEXT STEPS
    #AI->H::Status: (Crafting pitch close)
    CLOSING ELEMENTS:
        Primary Ask: "[Specific action requested - call, meeting, or review of additional materials]"
        Timeline: "Available for [action] at your convenience, with [timeframe] for story execution."
        Value Add: "Happy to provide [additional materials, source connections, data access] upon request."
        Exclusivity Offer (if appropriate): "Offering [publication name] first look before broader outreach."
    Keep the close to 2-3 sentences maximum; make the ask easy to accept.

    # STEP 10: COMPLETE PITCH ASSEMBLY
    #AI->H::Status: (Assembling final pitch document)
    COMPLETE PITCH DOCUMENT:
    ============================================================
    SUBJECT LINE OPTIONS:
        A: [Direct option]
        B: [Creative option]
    ============================================================
    Dear [Editor Name / Editor Title],

    [HOOK - 1-2 sentences from Step 3]

    [STORY SUMMARY - 2-3 sentences explaining the story and why it matters now, from Steps 3-4]

    [UNIQUE ANGLE - 1-2 sentences on differentiation from Step 4]

    KEY SUPPORTING EVIDENCE:
        - [Data point 1 with source]
        - [Data point 2 with source]
        - [Data point 3 with source]

    SOURCES AVAILABLE:
        - [Source 1, title/role]
        - [Source 2, title/role]
        - [Source 3, title/role]

    [READER VALUE - 1-2 sentences on what the audience gains, from Step 8]

    [CALL TO ACTION - 1 sentence from Step 9]

    Best regards,
    [User Name]
    [Contact Information]
    ============================================================
    #AI->H::Note: (Pitch complete. Total length: [word count] words. Review each section and confirm ready for submission.)
    #AI->H::Question: (Would you like to refine any section, adjust the tone, or create variations for different publications?)
    """,

    outputs={
        "PITCH_DOCUMENT": {
            "format": "Structured email pitch",
            "length": "300-500 words",
            "sections": ["Subject lines (2 options)", "Hook and Why Now", "Story summary and angle",
                "Evidence bullets", "Source list", "Reader value", "Call to action"],
            "usage": "Direct submission to editors"
        },
        "HEADLINE_OPTIONS": {
            "format": "3-5 headline variations",
            "purpose": "A/B testing and adaptation",
            "usage": "Select or combine for final pitch"
        },
        "SOURCE_ROSTER": {
            "format": "Categorized source list",
            "purpose": "Interview planning",
            "usage": "Story execution reference"
        }
    },

    integration_notes="First recipe of the Pitching & Assignment subcategory; Stage 2 of 7 in the Journalist "
        "Process. Prerequisite: a researched story concept from RCP-007-002-003 (Research Roadmap) — runs "
        "standalone if the user already has a concept. Feeds RCP-007-003-002 (Pitch Audience Strategist, Nellie) "
        "for multi-audience angle optimization, then the writing/drafting stage. Common modifications: "
        "industry-specific angle guidance, publication-database lookup, extended source contact info, competitive "
        "pitch analysis.",

    changelog="v3.00a (P062-H027): persona-framed to Nellie; Section 9 ai_to_ai added; ids normalized to "
        "RCP-007-003-001; dependency reconciled to RCP-007-002-003 (per master index); no tier/flavor residue.",

    ai_to_ai_communication={
        "schema_version": "1.1",
        "schema_profile": "Option-B typed-envelope (H041 LOCKED canonical)",
        "authored_by": "P062-Cat - SP11 Journalist-Process cookbook build (P062-H027)",
        "envelope": [
            {"type": "prose",
             "body": "HANDOFF CONTRACT: emits PITCH_DOCUMENT (a 300-500 word editor-ready email pitch: 2 subject "
                     "lines, hook+why-now, story summary + unique angle, 3-5 sourced evidence bullets, a source "
                     "list, reader value, and a call to action), plus HEADLINE_OPTIONS (3-5 variants) and a "
                     "categorized SOURCE_ROSTER. Upstream: a researched concept from RCP-007-002-003 (Research "
                     "Roadmap). Downstream consumer: RCP-007-003-002 (Pitch Audience Strategist) imports this "
                     "pitch as its baseline for multi-audience optimization; the chosen pitch then drives the "
                     "writing stage (RCP-007-004-001)."},
            {"type": "prose",
             "body": "EXECUTION GUIDANCE: run as Nellie (Managing Editor) - decision-first, standards-first. Work "
                     "the ten steps in order; do not skip the policy pre-check. Adapt the angle to publication_type "
                     "before assembling. Every evidence bullet must carry a source; every source carries a role and "
                     "a confirmed/to-pursue status. Keep hook+why-now and the close to 2-3 sentences each."},
            {"type": "keyed_list",
             "preamble": "EDGE CASES:",
             "items": [
                {"key": "no_target_publication", "body": "If target_publication is absent, ask for publication "
                     "TYPE and tailor the angle/tone to that category rather than guessing a named outlet."},
                {"key": "thin_evidence", "body": "If evidence is limited, do not pad the pitch - emit the "
                     "Suggestion listing the specific evidence types to gather, and keep only verifiable bullets."},
                {"key": "unverified_sources", "body": "Mark any source whose access is not confirmed as "
                     "'To pursue' rather than presenting it as secured; an overstated roster fails at the editor."}
             ]},
            {"type": "prose",
             "body": "QUALITY BAR: the pitch is 300-500 words, leads with a hook + a why-now, states one distinct "
                     "angle, carries 3-5 sourced evidence bullets and a credible source list, ties to reader value, "
                     "and closes with a single easy-to-accept ask; headlines are under 70 characters with rationales."}
        ],
        "lessons_learned": [
            {"key": "why_now_wins_the_open",
             "body": "Editors decide in the first two sentences; a sharp hook plus an explicit 'why now' clears the "
                     "open far more often than a strong-but-undated angle, so lead with timeliness, not background."},
            {"key": "sourced_bullets_over_adjectives",
             "body": "Three evidence bullets each naming a source beat a paragraph of confident adjectives; "
                     "unsourced claims are the most common reason a promising pitch gets sent back."},
            {"key": "one_ask_easy_to_accept",
             "body": "A pitch that closes with a single, low-friction ask (a 15-minute call, a look at the draft) "
                     "converts better than one offering multiple options; ambiguity in the ask reads as not-ready."}
        ]
    }
)

# START RECIPE-ID: RCP-007-003-002
# ===========================================================
# CRAFT RECIPE: Pitch Audience Strategist
# Created: January 2, 2026 (source v2.00a, JOURNALIST-PROCESS cookbook)
# Revised: v3.00a — 2026-06-27 (P062-SP11 Phase 9.2, P062-H027)
# Creator: CRAFT (Journalist-Process cookbook)
# Upgraded by: P062-Cat (SP11 — v2.00a→v3.00a transform)
# Status: Official (CFT-FWK-COOKBK-JOURNALIST-PROCESS)
# ===========================================================

# ===========================================================
# GENERAL
# ===========================================================
Recipe Type:  Cookbook recipe (Official)
Name:         RCP-007-003-002
Description:  Tests and optimizes pitch angles for different audience segments and publication types — using a
              panel of expert editor perspectives to produce multiple tailored versions of one story pitch,
              prepare for tough questions and objections, and turn a single pitch into a multi-outlet strategy.

# ===========================================================
# CATEGORIES
# ===========================================================
Part Of Cookbook:   CFT-FWK-COOKBK-JOURNALIST-PROCESS
Category ID:        007  (CAT-007-JOURNALIST-PROCESS)
Subcategory ID:    003  (SUBCAT-003-PITCHING-ASSIGNMENT)
Recipe ID Number:  RCP-007-003-002
Fully-Qualified:   CFT-FWK-COOKBK-JOURNALIST-PROCESS::RCP-007-003-002
Status:            Official
Categories:        Journalist Process
Subcategories:     Pitching & Assignment
Tags:              audience · strategist · pitch-optimization · segments · multi-outlet · panel · objections · framing
Recommended Persona: Nellie — Managing Editor (namespaced: PERSONA-JOURNALIST-PROCESS-NELLIE-CARD.txt)
Difficulty:        Advanced

# ===========================================================
# INSTRUCTIONS
# ===========================================================
1. Confirm inputs: story_concept is required; existing_pitch, target_outlets, pitch_goal, internal_audience,
   expert_panel, and previous_rejections are optional. Adopt Nellie's editorial framing — judge each angle the way
   the editors on the panel would, and hold the bar that gets a pitch placed.
2. STEP 0 — Policy pre-check: scan for competitive-intelligence concerns, confidential business strategy, and
   internal-communications sensitivity; if a conflict is detected, raise a PolicyCaution and a note to keep the
   strategy confidential until ready to execute.
3. STEP 1 — Core story input: if existing_pitch provided, import it and extract core narrative, available
   evidence, identified sources, and the hook used (building on the RCP-007-003-001 output); else gather minimum
   story elements (concept, key facts/evidence, available sources, target audiences) and recommend running
   RCP-007-003-001 first. If previous_rejections provided, review them so new angles address prior rejection
   reasons.
4. STEP 2 — Expert panel configuration: start from the DEFAULT_PANEL of three editor archetypes (Skeptical
   Business Editor · Innovation-Focused Tech Journalist · Human Interest Editor — each with focus, publication
   type, example outlets, values, and skepticism level); if target_outlets provided, customize the panel to the
   actual targets (add a trade specialist or local editor as needed); if expert_panel customized, use it.
5. STEP 3 — Panel analysis / angle generation: for each expert, produce a PITCH ANGLE (1-sentence frame), SUBJECT
   LINE (<60 chars), OPENING HOOK (2 sentences), KEY EVIDENCE THIS EXPERT PRIORITIZES (3 items with why), and a
   POTENTIAL OBJECTION; then build the COMPARISON MATRIX (Angle Focus · Key Hook · Evidence · Risk Level per
   expert) and ask which angle resonates.
6. STEP 4 — Tough question preparation: for each angle, prepare Q1 Credibility, Q2 Differentiation, Q3 Relevance,
   Q4 Timing — each with a suggested 2–3 sentence response and the specific evidence to cite.
7. STEP 5 — Red flag identification: per angle, list CRITICAL / IMPORTANT / MINOR issues with remediation; run a
   cross-angle analysis — if the same issue recurs across angles, raise a Caution (a real weakness any editor will
   notice) with a priority remediation.
8. STEP 6 — Angle selection strategy (driven by pitch_goal): single_placement -> Single Best Angle (+ backup
   outlet); maximum_coverage -> Parallel Pitching Strategy (Tier 1/2/3 outlets with angle + exclusivity);
   specific_audience -> Audience-Focused Approach (primary audience, best angle, supporting outlets, consistent
   message); reputation_building -> Credibility Ladder (start small -> leverage -> ultimate target, with timeline).
9. STEP 7 — Internal audience adaptation: if internal_audience is True, produce the INTERNAL PITCH (executive
   summary, strategic alignment, the opportunity, evidence/validation, resource requirements, success metrics,
   risk assessment, recommended action); else skip with a note.
10. STEP 8 — Angle refinement workshop: for each selected angle, refine headline (<60 chars) and hook (<50 words)
    with stated improvements, order the evidence hierarchy strongest-first, run a source-accessibility check
    (Confirmed/Pending/Unknown), sharpen the call to action, and show a before/after comparison.
11. STEP 9 — Objection response playbook: build the quick-reference playbook covering the six standard objections
    (already covered · readers not interested · weak/unverified data · who else is covering this · visual/multimedia
    angle · feels like PR not news), each with response type, answer, and evidence.
12. STEP 10 — Multi-outlet pitch package: compile deliverables — Primary Pitch, Alternative Angles, Tough-Question
    Prep, Objection Playbook, Red-Flag Checklist, Outlet Priority Matrix, and (if internal_audience) the Internal
    Pitch; report the package summary and recommended next steps (immediate / follow-up / contingency).
13. Hand the selected pitch + angle package forward to RCP-007-004-001 (the writing/drafting stage).

# ===========================================================
# CUSTOM FIELDS
# ===========================================================
Recipe FAQ:
  Q: What is required? A: story_concept; an existing_pitch (from RCP-007-003-001) is recommended but optional.
  Q: How many angles does it produce? A: 3-5 distinct, audience-tailored pitch angles from the expert panel.
  Q: What does pitch_goal control? A: the angle-selection strategy (single placement, maximum coverage, specific
     audience, or reputation building).
How A.I. Reads This Recipe:
  Execute as Nellie (Managing Editor). Run the expert panel as distinct editorial lenses, stress-test every angle
  for credibility, differentiation, relevance, and timing, and surface red flags honestly rather than smoothing
  them over. Decision -> Rationale -> Conditions.
Recipe Short Description: Multi-audience pitch-optimization and objection-prep engine.
When To Use: after a baseline pitch exists (RCP-007-003-001), to tailor it across outlets and prepare for editor pushback.
Actual Examples: existing_pitch="[pitch from PITCH-ARCHITECT]", story_concept="[user_story_concept]",
  target_outlets=["TechCrunch", "Forbes", "Trade pub"], pitch_goal="maximum_coverage", internal_audience=False.
Recipe Name: RCP-007-003-002
Included In Cookbook: CFT-FWK-COOKBK-JOURNALIST-PROCESS
Recommended Prompt Framework: CRAFT #H->AI / #AI->H comment protocol.
Extension Of: RCP-007-003-001 (Pitch Architect — optimizes its output)
Version History:
  v3.00a — 2026-06-27 (SP11 P9.2, P062-H027): v2.00a→v3.00a transform. Canonical id RCP-007-003-002 (dropped the
    in-id name "-PITCH-AUDIENCE-STRATEGIST" + the "-v2.00a" suffix; collapsed the source's multiline recipe_id

    Strategist" directive to the Nellie persona (SUBCAT-003-PITCHING-ASSIGNMENT section persona / Managing

    ADDED Section 9 ai_to_ai_communication (Option-B typed envelope, schema 1.1) + 3 content lessons_learned.
    Promoted Version History to its own field. Removed flavor/tier residue (SP09/SP10) — none present in the
    source body; documented here per standard. METADATA reconciled from the source COOKBOOK_MASTER_INDEX entry:
    subcategory SUBCAT-003-PITCHING-ASSIGNMENT (source name, NOT relabeled); difficulty "Advanced" (index
    "advanced"); estimated_time "45-60 minutes"; dependencies ["RCP-007-003-001"]; used_by ["RCP-007-004-001"];
    validated_by Auguste; keywords carried verbatim. No parameter, step, output, table, or template removed.

# --- PERSONA CONFIGURATION ---
# {PERSONA_NAME}=Nellie  {PERSONA_TITLE}=Managing Editor
# file_reference = PERSONA-JOURNALIST-PROCESS-NELLIE-CARD.txt  (section persona; canonical identity preserved)
# NOTE: the DEFAULT_PANEL experts below are AUDIENCE LENSES used inside the recipe, NOT CRAFT personas.

PITCH_AUDIENCE_STRATEGIST = Recipe(
    recipe_id="RCP-007-003-002",
    title="Pitch Audience Strategist",
    description="Tests and optimizes pitch angles for different audience segments and publication types. Creates "
        "multiple tailored versions of a single story pitch using a panel of expert editor perspectives, prepares "
        "the user for tough questions and objections before submission, and transforms one pitch into a "
        "multi-outlet strategy with audience-specific framing.",
    category="CAT-007-JOURNALIST-PROCESS",
    subcategory="SUBCAT-003-PITCHING-ASSIGNMENT",
    difficulty="Advanced",
    estimated_time="45-60 minutes",
    version="3.00a",
    dependencies=["RCP-007-003-001"],
    used_by=["RCP-007-004-001"],

    parameters={
        "existing_pitch":      {"type": "string",  "required": False, "description": "Baseline pitch to optimize", "example": "[pitch from PITCH-ARCHITECT]"},
        "story_concept":       {"type": "string",  "required": True,  "description": "Core story if no pitch exists", "example": "[user_story_concept]"},
        "target_outlets":      {"type": "list",    "required": False, "description": "Specific publications to target", "example": ["TechCrunch", "Forbes", "Trade pub"]},
        "pitch_goal":          {"type": "string",  "required": False, "options": ["single_placement", "maximum_coverage", "specific_audience", "reputation_building"], "description": "Primary objective for pitching", "default": "maximum_coverage"},
        "internal_audience":   {"type": "boolean", "required": False, "description": "Include internal pitch version", "default": False},
        "expert_panel":        {"type": "list",    "required": False, "description": "Custom expert perspectives", "default": ["Business", "Tech", "Human Interest"]},
        "previous_rejections": {"type": "list",    "required": False, "description": "Past rejection feedback", "example": ["Already covered", "Not timely"]}
    },

    prompt_template="""
    #H->AI::Directive: (Adopt the Nellie — Managing Editor persona, and run the expert panel as distinct editorial
        lenses. Stress-test each angle the way these editors would; surface red flags honestly.)
    #H->AI::Context: (Optimizing a pitch for multiple audiences)

    # STEP 0: POLICY PRE-CHECK
    Scan for sensitive categories: competitive-intelligence concerns; confidential business strategy;
    internal-communications sensitivity.
    IF potential conflict detected:
        #AI->H::PolicyCaution: (Multi-audience strategy may reveal positioning decisions)
        #AI->H::Note: (Keep strategy confidential until ready to execute)

    # STEP 1: CORE STORY INPUT
    #AI->H::Status: (Establishing baseline story)
    IF existing_pitch provided:
        Import {existing_pitch}; extract core narrative, evidence available, sources identified, hook approach used.
        #AI->H::Note: (Building on existing RCP-007-003-001 output for optimization)
    ELSE:
        Gather minimum story elements: concept {story_concept}, key facts and evidence, available sources, target audience(s).
        #AI->H::Question: (I recommend completing RCP-007-003-001 (Pitch Architect) first to create a foundational
            pitch. Proceed with a quick baseline, or run RCP-007-003-001?)
    IF previous_rejections provided:
        Review {previous_rejections}.
        #AI->H::Note: (Will ensure new angles address previous rejection reasons)

    # STEP 2: EXPERT PANEL CONFIGURATION
    #AI->H::Status: (Configuring expert perspectives)
    DEFAULT_PANEL = {
        "Expert_1": {"name": "Skeptical Business Editor",
                     "focus": "Hard numbers, economic impact, ROI",
                     "publication_type": "Legacy business media",
                     "examples": "Wall Street Journal, Financial Times",
                     "values": ["Verifiable data", "Market significance", "Executive relevance", "Financial implications"],
                     "skepticism": "High - requires strong evidence"},
        "Expert_2": {"name": "Innovation-Focused Tech Journalist",
                     "focus": "Disruption, trends, what is next",
                     "publication_type": "Digital tech outlets",
                     "examples": "WIRED, Axios, TechCrunch",
                     "values": ["Novel technology", "Future implications", "Industry disruption", "Technical depth"],
                     "skepticism": "Medium - open to bold claims"},
        "Expert_3": {"name": "Human Interest Editor",
                     "focus": "Founder journey, why, relatability",
                     "publication_type": "Entrepreneurial media",
                     "examples": "Inc., Fast Company, Entrepreneur",
                     "values": ["Personal narrative", "Emotional resonance", "Struggle and triumph", "Inspirational angle"],
                     "skepticism": "Low - prioritizes story quality"}
    }
    IF target_outlets provided: review {target_outlets}; customize the panel to match actual targets; add a trade
        specialist (industry pubs) or local editor (regional outlets) as needed.
    IF expert_panel customized: use {expert_panel}; configure perspectives accordingly.
    #AI->H::Note: (Panel configured with [number] expert perspectives; each evaluates your story through its lens.)

    # STEP 3: PANEL ANALYSIS - ANGLE GENERATION
    #AI->H::Status: (Generating angles from each perspective)
    FOR EACH EXPERT in panel:
    ============================================================
    EXPERT [N]: [Expert Name]   Publication Focus: [Type]
    ============================================================
    PITCH ANGLE: [1-sentence story frame from this perspective]
    SUBJECT LINE: [tailored email subject under 60 characters]
    OPENING HOOK: [first 2 sentences targeting this audience]
    KEY EVIDENCE THIS EXPERT PRIORITIZES: 3 items, each "[evidence type]: [why it matters to them]"
    POTENTIAL OBJECTION: [what would make this expert hesitate]
    ============================================================
    [Repeat for each expert]
    COMPARISON MATRIX:
    | Aspect      | Expert 1  | Expert 2  | Expert 3  |
    |-------------|-----------|-----------|-----------|
    | Angle Focus | [focus]   | [focus]   | [focus]   |
    | Key Hook    | [hook]    | [hook]    | [hook]    |
    | Evidence    | [type]    | [type]    | [type]    |
    | Risk Level  | [H/M/L]   | [H/M/L]   | [H/M/L]   |
    #AI->H::Question: (Which angle resonates most with your story strengths and target goals?)

    # STEP 4: TOUGH QUESTION PREPARATION
    #AI->H::Status: (Preparing for editor challenges)
    FOR EACH ANGLE generated - TOUGH QUESTIONS FOR [EXPERT N] ANGLE:
        Q1 Credibility Challenge: "[question about proof]" -> Suggested Response: "[2-3 sentences]" -> Evidence to Cite: "[specific source]"
        Q2 Differentiation Challenge: "How is this different from [similar coverage]?" -> "[2-3 sentences]" -> "[unique element]"
        Q3 Relevance Challenge: "Why should our readers care about this?" -> "[2-3 sentences]" -> "[audience connection]"
        Q4 Timing Challenge: "Why is this news now?" -> "[2-3 sentences]" -> "[timeliness factor]"
    #AI->H::Note: (Tough questions reveal where each angle is vulnerable; strong answers raise acceptance probability.)

    # STEP 5: RED FLAG IDENTIFICATION
    #AI->H::Status: (Identifying potential rejection triggers)
    FOR EACH ANGLE - [EXPERT N] ANGLE RED FLAGS:
        CRITICAL (likely causes rejection): [Issue]: [why it matters] -> Remediation: [specific fix]
        IMPORTANT (address before pitching): [Issue]: [why it matters] -> Remediation: [specific fix]
        MINOR (nice to fix): [Issue]: [why it matters] -> Remediation: [specific fix]
    CROSS-ANGLE ANALYSIS:
        IF the same issue appears in multiple angles:
            #AI->H::Caution: (Multiple perspectives flag [issue] - likely a real weakness any editor will notice.)
            Priority Remediation: [steps to address before any pitch]

    # STEP 6: ANGLE SELECTION STRATEGY
    #AI->H::Status: (Recommending pitch strategy)
    Based on pitch_goal: {pitch_goal}
        IF "single_placement"  -> RECOMMENDED: Single Best Angle. Best Angle [Expert N]; Rationale; Target Outlet; Backup Outlet.
        IF "maximum_coverage"  -> RECOMMENDED: Parallel Pitching Strategy. Tier 1 (highest priority: publication, angle, exclusive offer);
            Tier 2 (simultaneous non-competing: publications + angles); Tier 3 (backup if Tier 1 declines: publication + angle).
        IF "specific_audience" -> RECOMMENDED: Audience-Focused Approach. Primary audience; best angle; supporting outlets; consistent message.
        IF "reputation_building" -> RECOMMENDED: Credibility Ladder. Start with (smaller/trade outlet for proof) -> leverage to (larger
            outlet with the clip) -> ultimate target (Tier 1 publication); Timeline [weeks/months].
    #AI->H::Question: (Does this strategy align with your goals? Any constraints I should factor?)

    # STEP 7: INTERNAL AUDIENCE ADAPTATION
    IF internal_audience == True:
        #AI->H::Status: (Creating internal pitch version)
        INTERNAL PITCH: [Story Title] - Prepared for: [Leadership/Board/Stakeholders]
            EXECUTIVE SUMMARY: [the ask in 2-3 sentences - approval/resources needed]
            STRATEGIC ALIGNMENT: Company Goal 1/2 [how this supports]; Brand/Reputation [expected impact]
            THE OPPORTUNITY: [external pitch reframed as business opportunity - what we gain from coverage]
            EVIDENCE AND VALIDATION: [key metric 1] [key metric 2] [external validation point]
            RESOURCE REQUIREMENTS: Time [estimate]; Budget [costs]; Personnel [who participates]
            SUCCESS METRICS: KPI 1; KPI 2; Timeline [when we will know if successful]
            RISK ASSESSMENT: Risk 1 -> Mitigation; Risk 2 -> Mitigation
            RECOMMENDED ACTION: [specific approval or decision requested]
    ELSE:
        #AI->H::Note: (Skipping internal pitch - external focus only)

    # STEP 8: ANGLE REFINEMENT WORKSHOP
    #AI->H::Status: (Refining selected angle(s))
    FOR EACH selected angle - REFINEMENT ANALYSIS:
        Original Headline [from Step 3] -> Refined Headline [<60 chars] + Improvement [what changed and why]
        Original Hook [from Step 3] -> Refined Hook [<50 words] + Improvement [what changed and why]
        Evidence Hierarchy (strongest first): 1 primary (most compelling) / 2 secondary (supports primary) / 3 tertiary (adds depth)
        Source Accessibility Check: Source 1/2/3 -> [Confirmed/Pending/Unknown]
        Call to Action Clarity: Original [from Step 3] -> Refined [specific, easy to accept]
    BEFORE/AFTER COMPARISON: [original vs refined side by side]

    # STEP 9: OBJECTION RESPONSE PLAYBOOK
    #AI->H::Status: (Creating quick-reference playbook)
    OBJECTION RESPONSE PLAYBOOK - each: Objection -> Response Type -> Answer [2-3 sentences] -> Evidence:
        "We covered something similar recently" -> Differentiation -> [how this is different] -> [unique angle or new data]
        "Our readers are not interested in this" -> Audience Connection -> [why readers care] -> [reader benefit or trend connection]
        "The data seems weak or unverified" -> Credibility -> [source validation] -> [specific sources and methodology]
        "Who else is covering this?" -> Exclusivity/Timing -> [your position] -> [exclusive access or first-mover angle]
        "What is the visual/multimedia angle?" -> Asset Availability -> [visual opportunities] -> [photos, video, graphics available]
        "This feels like a PR pitch, not news" -> News Value -> [news elements] -> [timeliness, impact, significance]
    #AI->H::Note: (Keep this playbook handy during pitch calls or when drafting follow-up responses.)

    # STEP 10: MULTI-OUTLET PITCH PACKAGE
    #AI->H::Status: (Compiling final deliverables)
    PITCH PACKAGE SUMMARY:
        DELIVERABLE 1 Primary Pitch: angle [Expert N], target [publication], ready [Yes/Needs refinement], file [pitch document]
        DELIVERABLE 2 Alternative Angles: A/B/C [Expert N] for [outlet type]
        DELIVERABLE 3 Tough Question Prep: questions covered [number], responses ready [Yes]
        DELIVERABLE 4 Objection Playbook: objections covered [number], response types [Data/Narrative/Reframe]
        DELIVERABLE 5 Red Flag Checklist: critical/important/minor [number - status]
        DELIVERABLE 6 Outlet Priority Matrix: Tier 1/2/3 [publications]
        IF internal_audience: DELIVERABLE 7 Internal Pitch: audience [Leadership/Board], format [business case]
    #AI->H::Note: (Package complete: [number] angles ready, [number] outlets prioritized, prep for [number] objections.)
    RECOMMENDED NEXT STEPS: 1 [immediate action] · 2 [follow-up action] · 3 [contingency action]
    #AI->H::Question: (Ready to execute, or refine any component further?)
    """,

    outputs={
        "ANGLE_VARIATIONS": {"format": "3-5 distinct pitch angles", "purpose": "Multi-audience targeting", "usage": "Select per outlet or A/B test"},
        "TOUGH_QUESTION_PREP": {"format": "Q&A preparation sheet", "purpose": "Interview/call readiness", "usage": "Reference during pitch meetings"},
        "OBJECTION_PLAYBOOK": {"format": "Quick-reference responses", "purpose": "Handle pushback confidently", "usage": "Keep handy during outreach"},
        "RED_FLAG_CHECKLIST": {"format": "Prioritized issue list", "purpose": "Pre-pitch remediation", "usage": "Address before submitting"},
        "OUTLET_MATRIX": {"format": "Tiered publication list", "purpose": "Strategic sequencing", "usage": "Guide outreach order"},
        "INTERNAL_PITCH": {"format": "Business case document", "purpose": "Leadership approval", "usage": "Internal stakeholder buy-in", "conditional": "Only if internal_audience=True"}
    },

    integration_notes="Second recipe of the Pitching & Assignment subcategory; Stage 2 of 7 in the Journalist "
        "Process - the strategic optimization layer. Prerequisite: RCP-007-003-001 (Pitch Architect) output "
        "recommended but not required (runs standalone with minimum story input). Feeds RCP-007-004-001 (the "
        "writing/drafting stage) and the actual submission/follow-up workflow. Common modifications: "
        "industry-specific expert personas, competitor-coverage analysis, social-media angles, a measurement "
        "framework for tracking.",

    changelog="v3.00a (P062-H027): persona-framed to Nellie (expert archetypes retained as audience lenses); "
        "Section 9 ai_to_ai added; ids normalized to RCP-007-003-002; multiline recipe_id collapsed; no tier/flavor residue.",

    ai_to_ai_communication={
        "schema_version": "1.1",
        "schema_profile": "Option-B typed-envelope (H041 LOCKED canonical)",
        "authored_by": "P062-Cat - SP11 Journalist-Process cookbook build (P062-H027)",
        "envelope": [
            {"type": "prose",
             "body": "HANDOFF CONTRACT: emits ANGLE_VARIATIONS (3-5 distinct audience-tailored pitch angles), "
                     "TOUGH_QUESTION_PREP (credibility/differentiation/relevance/timing Q&A per angle), an "
                     "OBJECTION_PLAYBOOK (six standard objections with responses), a prioritized RED_FLAG_CHECKLIST, "
                     "a tiered OUTLET_MATRIX, and - only if internal_audience=True - an INTERNAL_PITCH business "
                     "case. Upstream: the baseline pitch from RCP-007-003-001 (Pitch Architect). Downstream: the "
                     "selected angle + package drives RCP-007-004-001 (writing/drafting) and the submission workflow."},
            {"type": "prose",
             "body": "EXECUTION GUIDANCE: run as Nellie, voicing the panel as distinct editorial lenses (the "
                     "Skeptical Business Editor, Tech Journalist, and Human Interest Editor are AUDIENCE archetypes, "
                     "not CRAFT personas). Generate every angle through all configured experts before selecting; let "
                     "pitch_goal pick the selection strategy. If previous_rejections exist, every new angle must "
                     "answer them. Refine only the angle(s) the user selects in Step 8."},
            {"type": "keyed_list",
             "preamble": "EDGE CASES:",
             "items": [
                {"key": "no_baseline_pitch", "body": "If existing_pitch is absent, do not silently invent one - "
                     "recommend running RCP-007-003-001 first, or build a quick baseline from story_concept with "
                     "the user's consent before generating angles."},
                {"key": "recurring_red_flag", "body": "If the same red flag surfaces across multiple angles, raise "
                     "the cross-angle Caution and require remediation before any pitch - it is a real weakness, not "
                     "an angle-specific one."},
                {"key": "internal_only_when_asked", "body": "Generate the INTERNAL_PITCH deliverable only when "
                     "internal_audience=True; otherwise skip it and keep the package external-focused."}
             ]},
            {"type": "prose",
             "body": "QUALITY BAR: 3-5 genuinely distinct angles (one per lens, not rephrasings); each carries a "
                     "subject line, hook, prioritized evidence, and a named objection; tough-question and objection "
                     "responses cite specific evidence; red flags are tiered with remediation; the outlet strategy "
                     "matches the stated pitch_goal."}
        ],
        "lessons_learned": [
            {"key": "distinct_lenses_not_rephrasings",
             "body": "An angle set only helps if each lens reframes the story on different evidence and stakes; "
                     "three near-identical angles waste the panel - enforce a distinct thesis and hook per expert."},
            {"key": "prep_the_objection_you_fear",
             "body": "The objection most likely to kill the pitch is usually the one the writer avoids; force a "
                     "credibility and a timing answer for every angle, because those are where editors push hardest."},
            {"key": "match_strategy_to_goal",
             "body": "Maximum-coverage parallel pitching and single-placement exclusivity are mutually exclusive; "
                     "picking the outlet strategy from pitch_goal up front prevents burning an exclusive by accident."}
        ]
    }
)

# Created: January 2, 2026 (source v2.00a, JOURNALIST-PROCESS cookbook)

# Creator: CRAFT (Journalist-Process cookbook)

# ===========================================================

# ===========================================================
# GENERAL
# ===========================================================
Recipe Type:  Cookbook recipe (Official)
Name:         RCP-007-004-001
Description:  Transforms research materials into a structured, publication-ready article outline — selecting a
              story angle, a structural framework matched to content type, section headers, content distribution,
              word-count allocation, and multimedia suggestions.

# ===========================================================
# CATEGORIES
# ===========================================================
Part Of Cookbook:   CFT-FWK-COOKBK-JOURNALIST-PROCESS
Category ID:        007  (CAT-007-JOURNALIST-PROCESS)
Subcategory ID:    004  (SUBCAT-004-WRITING-DRAFTING)
Recipe ID Number:  RCP-007-004-001
Fully-Qualified:   CFT-FWK-COOKBK-JOURNALIST-PROCESS::RCP-007-004-001
Status:            Official
Categories:        Journalist Process
Subcategories:     Writing & Drafting
Tags:              blueprint · outline · structure · article · architecture · sections · research-synthesis · drafting
Recommended Persona: Dominique — Writing Specialist (namespaced: PERSONA-JOURNALIST-PROCESS-DOMINIQUE-CARD.txt)
Difficulty:        Beginner

# ===========================================================
# INSTRUCTIONS
# ===========================================================
1. Confirm inputs: research_materials is required; target_word_count (default 800), content_type (default "news";
   one of news/feature/how-to/analysis/profile), target_audience, and publication_style are optional.
2. Adopt Dominique's writing framing: transform research into a publication-ready outline that guides drafting.
3. STEP 1 — Research-materials intake: parse and categorize into Facts, Quotes (with attribution), Statistics, and
   Context; report the counts. If gaps are detected, ask whether to supply more or proceed. If no materials are
   provided, issue a RequiredQuestion requesting them.
4. STEP 2 — Story-angle identification: evaluate newsworthiness (Timeliness, Impact, Prominence, Proximity, Human
   Interest, Novelty); generate ~3 candidate angles with rationale; recommend the strongest and confirm fit.
5. STEP 3 — Structural framework selection by content_type: news→Inverted Pyramid; feature→Narrative Arc;
   how-to→Problem-Solution; analysis→Thesis-Evidence-Conclusion; profile→Chronological or Thematic — each with its
   rationale.
6. STEP 4 — Section-header development: generate headers that describe content clearly, work as standalone
   navigation, maintain logical flow, and cover every material category (example set: LEAD/OPENING ·
   BACKGROUND/CONTEXT · content-specific sections · DATA/EVIDENCE · VOICES/QUOTES · CONCLUSION/NEXT STEPS).
7. STEP 5 — Content distribution: apply inverted-pyramid priority (lead = most newsworthy; then essential facts,
   context, supporting evidence/quotes, background) and map specific materials/quotes/statistics to sections.
8. STEP 6 — Word-count allocation against target_word_count: Lead/Opening 10-15% · Background 15-20% · Main
   Content 40-50% · Evidence/Data 10-15% · Conclusion 5-10% (guidelines, adjustable for substance).
9. STEP 7 — Generate the complete ARTICLE BLUEPRINT (Topic/Angle/Structure/Target Length header; I. LEAD with
   Five Ws + hook; II–IV section headers with subpoints and INSERT QUOTE / INSERT DATA placement markers;
   V. CONCLUSION with significance, forward look, optional CTA). Preserve the outline template structure.
10. STEP 8 — Multimedia suggestions: recommended visual placements (after lead, per-section charts/infographics,
    pull quotes, closing visual).
11. STEP 9 — Delivery and next steps: present the deliverables summary and hand the blueprint forward to the Draft
    Composer (RCP-007-004-002).

# ===========================================================
# CUSTOM FIELDS
# ===========================================================
Recipe FAQ:
  Q: What does it output? A: a complete article outline (angle, structure, headers, content mapping, word-count
     allocation, multimedia cues) ready for drafting.
  Q: What if research is thin? A: the blueprint marks gaps and asks whether to proceed or supply more material.
How A.I. Reads This Recipe:
  Execute as Dominique (Writing Specialist). Structure-first posture; choose the framework that fits content_type;
  map every supplied fact/quote/statistic to a section; never invent facts — mark missing content as placeholders.
Recipe Short Description: Turns raw research into a structured, drafting-ready article outline.
When To Use: after research/pitch is settled, to convert materials into an outline before drafting begins.
Actual Examples: research_materials="interview notes + 3 data points", target_word_count=800,
  content_type="feature", target_audience="general readers".
Recipe Name: RCP-007-004-001
Included In Cookbook: CFT-FWK-COOKBK-JOURNALIST-PROCESS
Recommended Prompt Framework: CRAFT #H->AI / #AI->H comment protocol.
Extension Of: — (entry recipe of the Writing & Drafting subcategory)

    recipe_id="RCP-007-004-001",
    title="Article Blueprint Architect",
    description="Transforms research materials into a structured, publication-ready article outline",
    category="CAT-007-JOURNALIST-PROCESS",
    subcategory="SUBCAT-004-WRITING-DRAFTING",

    version="3.00a",
    dependencies=["RCP-007-003-002"],
    used_by=["RCP-007-004-002"],

    parameters={
        "research_materials": {"type": "string",  "required": True,  "description": "Notes, interviews, data"},
        "target_word_count":  {"type": "integer", "required": False, "default": 800, "description": "Desired article length"},
        "content_type":       {"type": "string",  "required": False, "default": "news", "options": ["news", "feature", "how-to", "analysis", "profile"], "description": "Type of article"},
        "target_audience":    {"type": "string",  "required": False, "description": "Intended readers"},
        "publication_style":  {"type": "string",  "required": False, "description": "Tone and voice"}
    },

    prompt_template="""
# ===========================================================
# ARTICLE BLUEPRINT ARCHITECT
# ===========================================================

#H->AI::Directive: (Adopt the Dominique — Writing Specialist persona and create a structured article outline
    from research materials. Structure-first posture; map every supplied fact/quote/statistic to a section;
    never invent facts — mark missing content as a placeholder.)

#AI->H::Status: (Initializing Article Blueprint Architect)

"I will transform your research into a publication-ready outline. This blueprint will guide your drafting
process with clear structure and content placement."

# ===========================================================
# STEP 1: RESEARCH MATERIALS INTAKE
# ===========================================================

#AI->H::Status: (Processing research materials)

IF research_materials provided:
    Parse and categorize:
        - Facts: [extracted factual statements]
        - Quotes: [extracted quotations with attribution]
        - Statistics: [extracted data points]
        - Context: [background information]

    #AI->H::Note: (I have organized your materials into {count} facts, {count} quotes, {count} statistics,
        and {count} context items.)

    IF gaps_detected:
        #AI->H::Question: (I notice we may be missing [specific element]. Do you have additional materials,
            or should we proceed with what we have?)

ELSE:
    #AI->H::RequiredQuestion: (Please provide your research materials. This can include interview transcripts,
        notes, data, articles, or any information you want to organize into an article structure.)

# ===========================================================
# STEP 2: STORY ANGLE IDENTIFICATION
# ===========================================================

#AI->H::Status: (Analyzing for strongest story angle)

Evaluate materials for newsworthiness:
    - Timeliness: Is there a current hook?
    - Impact: Who does this affect and how?
    - Prominence: Are notable people involved?
    - Proximity: Is there local relevance?
    - Human Interest: Is there emotional resonance?
    - Novelty: What makes this new or different?

Generate potential angles:
    Angle 1: [Description with rationale]
    Angle 2: [Description with rationale]
    Angle 3: [Description with rationale]

#AI->H::Recommendation: (Based on your materials, I recommend Angle [X] because [specific reasons].
    This angle is strongest for [audience benefit].)

#AI->H::Question: (Does this angle align with your vision for the piece? Would you prefer to explore one
    of the alternatives?)

# ===========================================================
# STEP 3: STRUCTURAL FRAMEWORK SELECTION
# ===========================================================

#AI->H::Status: (Selecting optimal article structure)

IF content_type == "news":
    Recommended structure: Inverted Pyramid
    Rationale: "News articles benefit from most important information first, allowing editors to cut from
        bottom and readers to get essentials quickly."

IF content_type == "feature":
    Recommended structure: Narrative Arc
    Rationale: "Feature stories engage through storytelling. Building tension and resolution keeps readers
        invested in longer pieces."

IF content_type == "how-to":
    Recommended structure: Problem-Solution
    Rationale: "Instructional content works best when it establishes the need before providing steps."

IF content_type == "analysis":
    Recommended structure: Thesis-Evidence-Conclusion
    Rationale: "Analytical pieces require clear argument structure with supporting evidence."

IF content_type == "profile":
    Recommended structure: Chronological or Thematic
    Rationale: "Profiles work as timeline or by grouping traits and achievements thematically."

#AI->H::Note: (I recommend the {structure} approach for this {content_type} piece. This will [specific
    benefit for the content].)

# ===========================================================
# STEP 4: SECTION HEADER DEVELOPMENT
# ===========================================================

#AI->H::Status: (Creating section framework)

Based on selected structure and materials, generate headers that:
    - Describe content clearly
    - Work as standalone navigation
    - Maintain logical flow
    - Cover all material categories

Example header set:
    - LEAD/OPENING
    - BACKGROUND/CONTEXT
    - [Content-specific section]
    - [Content-specific section]
    - DATA/EVIDENCE
    - VOICES/QUOTES
    - CONCLUSION/NEXT STEPS

# ===========================================================
# STEP 5: CONTENT DISTRIBUTION
# ===========================================================

#AI->H::Status: (Assigning content to sections)

Apply inverted pyramid principles:
    - Lead: Most newsworthy element
    - Second: Essential supporting facts
    - Third: Important context
    - Middle: Supporting evidence and quotes
    - End: Background and additional detail

Map specific materials to sections:
    [Material 1] -> [Section]
    [Material 2] -> [Section]
    [Quote 1] -> [Section with placement note]
    [Statistic 1] -> [Section with context]

# ===========================================================
# STEP 6: WORD COUNT ALLOCATION
# ===========================================================

#AI->H::Status: (Allocating word counts by section)

Total target: {target_word_count} words

Distribution:
    - Lead/Opening: 10-15% ({calculated} words)
    - Background: 15-20% ({calculated} words)
    - Main Content: 40-50% ({calculated} words)
    - Evidence/Data: 10-15% ({calculated} words)
    - Conclusion: 5-10% ({calculated} words)

#AI->H::Note: (These are guidelines. Sections with more substantive content may warrant additional words.)

# ===========================================================
# STEP 7: OUTLINE GENERATION
# ===========================================================

#AI->H::Status: (Generating complete outline)

============================================================
ARTICLE BLUEPRINT
Topic: [Derived from materials]
Angle: [Selected angle]
Structure: [Selected structure]
Target Length: {target_word_count} words
============================================================

HEADLINE: [Placeholder - generate in RCP-007-004-003]

I. LEAD PARAGRAPH ({word_count} words)
    - Key news element
    - Five Ws addressed
    - Hook for reader

II. [SECTION HEADER] ({word_count} words)
    A. [Subpoint]
        - [Specific content note]
    B. [Subpoint]
        - [Specific content note]

III. [SECTION HEADER] ({word_count} words)
    A. [Subpoint]
        - INSERT QUOTE: [Attribution]
    B. [Subpoint]
        - INSERT DATA: [Statistic description]

IV. [SECTION HEADER] ({word_count} words)
    A. [Subpoint]
    B. [Subpoint]

V. CONCLUSION ({word_count} words)
    - Summary of significance
    - Forward-looking statement
    - Call to action (if appropriate)

============================================================

# ===========================================================
# STEP 8: MULTIMEDIA SUGGESTIONS
# ===========================================================

#AI->H::Status: (Identifying visual opportunities)

Recommended visual placements:
    - After Lead: [Image type suggestion]
    - Section [X]: [Chart or infographic idea]
    - Section [Y]: [Pull quote suggestion]
    - Conclusion: [Supporting visual]

#AI->H::Note: (Visual elements enhance engagement and break up text. Consider these suggestions as you
    develop the piece or coordinate with designers.)

# ===========================================================
# STEP 9: DELIVERY AND NEXT STEPS
# ===========================================================

#AI->H::Deliverable: (Article Blueprint complete)

"Your article blueprint is ready. This structure provides a roadmap for drafting your piece efficiently."

Summary of deliverables:
    - Story angle selection with rationale
    - Structural framework aligned to content type
    - Section headers with content mapping
    - Word count allocations
    - Multimedia placement suggestions

#AI->H::Recommendation: (Next step: Use RCP-007-004-002 (Draft Composer and Refiner) to transform this
    blueprint into a complete first draft with iterative refinement.)

#AI->H::Question: (Would you like to proceed to drafting, or would you like to refine any aspect of this
    blueprint first?)
    """,

    outputs={
        "story_angle": "Selected story angle with rationale (chosen from ~3 candidates)",
        "structural_framework": "Article structure matched to content_type, with rationale",
        "section_headers": "Header set covering all material categories, with content mapped to each section",
        "word_count_allocation": "Per-section word budget against target_word_count",
        "article_blueprint": "Complete outline (lead, section subpoints, INSERT QUOTE/DATA markers, conclusion)",

                {"key": "raw_materials_no_angle", "body": "If no clear angle emerges, present the ~3 candidate "

            {"key": "outline_before_prose", "body": "A drafting stage given a mapped outline (materials already "

            {"key": "structure_follows_type", "body": "Choosing the framework from content_type up front prevents "

            {"key": "mark_gaps_dont_fill", "body": "Leaving explicit [PLACEHOLDER] markers where research is thin "
                     "keeps the writer in control and prevents invented facts from entering the draft pipeline."}
        ]
    }

# CRAFT RECIPE: Draft Composer and Refiner
# Created: January 2, 2026 (source v2.00a, JOURNALIST-PROCESS cookbook)
# Revised: v3.00a — 2026-06-27 (P062-SP11 Phase 9, P062-H027)
# Creator: CRAFT (Journalist-Process cookbook)
# Upgraded by: P062-Cat (SP11 — v2.00a→v3.00a transform)
# Status: Official (CFT-FWK-COOKBK-JOURNALIST-PROCESS)
# ===========================================================

# ===========================================================
# GENERAL
# ===========================================================
Recipe Type:  Cookbook recipe (Official)
Name:         RCP-007-004-002
Description:  Composes a complete first draft from a blueprint/outline or raw materials, then iteratively refines
              it across structured revision passes (clarity & conciseness, structure & flow, lead, quote/data
              integration, tone & voice) and delivers a polished final draft plus a revision summary.

# ===========================================================
# CATEGORIES
# ===========================================================
Part Of Cookbook:   CFT-FWK-COOKBK-JOURNALIST-PROCESS
Category ID:        007  (CAT-007-JOURNALIST-PROCESS)
Subcategory ID:    004  (SUBCAT-004-WRITING-DRAFTING)
Recipe ID Number:  RCP-007-004-002
Fully-Qualified:   CFT-FWK-COOKBK-JOURNALIST-PROCESS::RCP-007-004-002
Status:            Official
Categories:        Journalist Process
Subcategories:     Writing & Drafting
Tags:              draft · composer · refiner · writing · prose · revision · tone · voice · drafting
Recommended Persona: Dominique — Writing Specialist (namespaced: PERSONA-JOURNALIST-PROCESS-DOMINIQUE-CARD.txt)
Difficulty:        Intermediate

# ===========================================================
# INSTRUCTIONS
# ===========================================================
1. Confirm inputs: source_materials is required; target_word_count (default 800), publication_style (default
   "professional"; one of professional/conversational/technical/academic), revision_depth (default "full"; one of
   quick/standard/full), and target_audience are optional.
2. Adopt Dominique's writing framing: turn materials into a polished draft through systematic composition and
   revision, each pass targeting a specific improvement.
3. STEP 1 — Source-material assessment: detect input type (outline from RCP-007-004-001, raw research notes,
   interview transcripts, or a combination); state which foundation will be used; run a completeness check
   (facts/quotes/data); mark [PLACEHOLDER] where content is missing. If no materials are provided, issue a
   RequiredQuestion.
4. STEP 2 — Initial draft composition (Phase 1 of 2): write a complete draft without over-editing, following the
   outline if present (else inverted-pyramid for news / narrative arc for features), to target_word_count in
   publication_style; emit the INITIAL DRAFT block (lead, sections, conclusion, word count, status).
5. STEP 3 — Revision Pass 1, Clarity & Conciseness: passive→active, filler removal, redundancy elimination,
   sentence simplification, one-point-per-paragraph; report per-paragraph before/after and a change summary.
6. STEP 4 — Revision Pass 2, Structure & Flow: information-priority order, paragraph sequence, transitions,
   narrative momentum, sustained engagement; report structural adjustments and a change summary.
7. STEP 5 — Revision Pass 3, Lead & Opening: Five Ws check; assess hook strength, standalone capability, and
   engagement; if needed, supply an improved lead, an alternative lead, and rationale.
8. STEP 6 — Quote & data integration: verify attribution and natural flow of quotes; verify statistics have
   context, are reader-friendly, and support the narrative; record adjustments.
9. STEP 7 — Tone & voice alignment: enforce the publication_style tone across opening/middle/conclusion; check
   audience alignment (language level, jargon, reader assumptions); record any adjustments.
10. STEP 8 — Final draft assembly: compile the FINAL DRAFT block (word count, style, passes completed) with all
    revisions integrated.
11. STEP 9 — Revision summary: deliver the REVISION SUMMARY (per-pass key improvements, overall metrics, remaining
    items for the writer) and hand the polished draft forward to RCP-007-004-003 (Headline and Lead Generator).
    NOTE: revision_depth scales how many passes are applied (quick/standard/full).

# ===========================================================
# CUSTOM FIELDS
# ===========================================================
Recipe FAQ:
  Q: What does it output? A: a polished final draft plus a structured revision summary and a list of remaining
     items for the writer.
  Q: Does it work without an outline? A: yes — it can draft from raw materials, building structure during
     composition; an outline (from RCP-007-004-001) yields cleaner results.
How A.I. Reads This Recipe:
  Execute as Dominique (Writing Specialist). Draft first, then refine in ordered passes; preserve attributed
  quotes verbatim; never invent facts — mark [PLACEHOLDER] and flag items for the writer to verify.
Recipe Short Description: Composes and iteratively refines a complete article draft.

  publication_style="conversational", revision_depth="full".

    verbatim; never invent facts — mark [PLACEHOLDER] and flag items for the writer to verify.)

"I will transform your materials into a polished draft through systematic composition and revision. Each pass
focuses on specific improvements."

# ===========================================================
# STEP 1: SOURCE MATERIAL ASSESSMENT
# ===========================================================

#AI->H::Status: (Assessing source materials)

    Analyze input type:

        - Raw research notes
        - Interview transcripts
        - Combination of materials

    #AI->H::Note: (I have received {material_type}. I will use this as the foundation for drafting.)

    IF outline_detected:
        "Using your outline as the structural guide. I will follow its section order and word count allocations."

    IF raw_materials_only:
        "Working from raw materials. I will create structure during drafting, following inverted pyramid
        principles for news or narrative arc for features."

    Completeness check:
        - Sufficient facts for all sections?
        - Quotes available for integration?
        - Data points ready for context?

    IF gaps_detected:
        #AI->H::Caution: (I notice we may be missing [specific content]. I will proceed but mark [PLACEHOLDER]
            where this content should be inserted.)

    #AI->H::RequiredQuestion: (Please provide your source materials. This can be an outline, research notes,
        interview transcripts, or other content to transform into a draft.)

# ===========================================================

    - Apply {publication_style} tone

============================================================
Word Count: [actual count]
Draft Status: Initial - Ready for Revision
============================================================

    - Redundant phrase elimination
    - Complex sentence simplification
    - One point per paragraph rule

Process each paragraph:
    Original: [text]
    Revised: [improved text]
    Changes: [specific improvements made]

    - Passive to active: [count] instances
    - Filler words removed: [count]
    - Sentences simplified: [count]

# ===========================================================
# STEP 4: REVISION PASS TWO - STRUCTURE AND FLOW
# ===========================================================

    - Information priority order

    - Transition quality between sections
    - Narrative momentum maintenance
    - Reader engagement throughout

Structural adjustments:
    - [Specific reordering if needed]
    - [Transition improvements]
    - [Flow enhancements]

    - Paragraphs reordered: [count]
    - Transitions added/improved: [count]
    - Sections reorganized: [yes/no]

# ===========================================================

    - Who: [present/missing]

    - When: [present/missing]

============================================================

#AI->H::Recommendation: (Your draft is polished and ready. Use RCP-007-004-003 (Headline and Lead Generator)
    to create compelling headlines and refine the opening hook further.)

    section of the draft first?)
    """,

    outputs={

# ===========================================================
# GENERAL
# ===========================================================
Recipe Type:  Cookbook recipe (Official)
Name:         RCP-007-004-003
Description:  Generates multiple ranked headline options and multiple lead-paragraph options for completed
              content, matches the best headline/lead combinations, and produces SEO and platform variations plus
              an A/B testing suggestion.

# ===========================================================
# CATEGORIES
# ===========================================================
Part Of Cookbook:   CFT-FWK-COOKBK-JOURNALIST-PROCESS
Category ID:        007  (CAT-007-JOURNALIST-PROCESS)
Subcategory ID:    004  (SUBCAT-004-WRITING-DRAFTING)
Recipe ID Number:  RCP-007-004-003
Fully-Qualified:   CFT-FWK-COOKBK-JOURNALIST-PROCESS::RCP-007-004-003
Status:            Official
Categories:        Journalist Process
Subcategories:     Writing & Drafting
Tags:              headline · lead · generator · opening · hook · attention · seo · click-through · drafting
Recommended Persona: Dominique — Writing Specialist (namespaced: PERSONA-JOURNALIST-PROCESS-DOMINIQUE-CARD.txt)
Difficulty:        Beginner

# ===========================================================
# INSTRUCTIONS
# ===========================================================
1. Confirm inputs: article_content is required; headline_count (default 5), lead_count (default 3),
   max_headline_words (default 12), content_type (default "news"; news/feature/analysis/how-to/profile),
   target_platform (default "web"; web/print/social/email), and seo_keywords (list) are optional.
2. Adopt Dominique's writing framing: create multiple headline and lead options, each using a different technique
   to engage readers.
3. STEP 1 — Content analysis: extract core message/thesis, most newsworthy fact, key numbers, notable quotes, and
   the unique angle; assess type, length, primary/secondary news value. If no content is provided, RequiredQuestion.
4. STEP 2 — Headline-style selection by content_type: news→Declarative/Data-driven/Action-oriented;
   feature→Narrative/Character-driven/Scene-setting; analysis→Question/Thesis/Provocative;
   how-to→Instructional/Benefit-focused/Numbered; apply target_platform constraints (word limit
   max_headline_words, character considerations, tone).
5. STEP 3 — Headline generation: produce {headline_count} diverse headlines (News, Data-Driven, Curiosity/Hook,
   Benefit/Reader-Focused, Alternative/Creative), each with approach and word count, under max_headline_words.
6. STEP 4 — Headline analysis and ranking: score each on Clarity / Accuracy / Engagement / SEO Value / Platform
   Fit (1-5 each, /25 total) and rank with rationale.
7. STEP 5 — Lead-paragraph style selection: choose {lead_count} approaches from Summary / Anecdotal /
   Scene-Setting / Question / Contrast / Expert, matched to content_type.
8. STEP 6 — Lead generation: produce {lead_count} distinct leads (e.g. Summary style with a Five Ws check;
   Anecdotal/Human-Interest with hook + transition; a third content-type-specific style), each with word count.
9. STEP 7 — Lead analysis and matching: present recommended headline+lead combinations (Best Overall, Alternative
   Strong, Social/Sharing-Optimized) with rationale and best-for context, plus combinations to avoid.
10. STEP 8 — SEO and platform optimization: integrate seo_keywords if provided; produce an SEO title (<60 chars)
    and meta description draft (~155 chars); produce platform variations (Twitter/X, LinkedIn, email subject lines).
11. STEP 9 — Final recommendations: primary and secondary headline/lead picks, an A/B testing suggestion
    (test/hypothesis/metric), and the complete asset package summary.

# ===========================================================
# CUSTOM FIELDS
# ===========================================================
Recipe FAQ:
  Q: What does it output? A: {headline_count} ranked headlines, {lead_count} leads, recommended combinations,
     SEO/platform variations, and an A/B test suggestion.
  Q: How are headlines ranked? A: scored 1-5 on Clarity, Accuracy, Engagement, SEO Value, and Platform Fit (/25).
How A.I. Reads This Recipe:
  Execute as Dominique (Writing Specialist). Generate diverse, accurate options that represent the content
  faithfully; respect max_headline_words and platform limits; never overstate beyond what the article supports.
Recipe Short Description: Produces ranked headlines and leads with SEO and platform variations.
When To Use: after a draft is polished (from RCP-007-004-002), to title and open the piece.
Actual Examples: article_content="full draft", headline_count=5, lead_count=3, content_type="news",
  target_platform="web", seo_keywords=["renewable energy", "grid storage"].

        "lead_count":        {"type": "integer", "required": False, "default": 3, "description": "Number of lead options"},
        "max_headline_words":{"type": "integer", "required": False, "default": 12, "description": "Maximum words per headline"},

        "target_platform":   {"type": "string",  "required": False, "default": "web", "options": ["web", "print", "social", "email"], "description": "Primary distribution"},
        "seo_keywords":      {"type": "list",    "required": False, "description": "Keywords to incorporate"}
    },

    prompt_template="""
# ===========================================================
# HEADLINE AND LEAD GENERATOR
# ===========================================================

#H->AI::Directive: (Adopt the Dominique — Writing Specialist persona and generate compelling headlines and lead
    paragraphs for completed content. Generate diverse, accurate options that represent the content faithfully;
    respect max_headline_words and platform limits; never overstate beyond what the article supports.)

#AI->H::Status: (Initializing Headline and Lead Generator)

"I will create multiple headline and lead paragraph options for your content, each using different techniques to
engage readers."

# ===========================================================
# STEP 1: CONTENT ANALYSIS
# ===========================================================

        - Unique angle or hook

        - Type: {content_type}

    #AI->H::Note: (I have identified [count] potential headline angles from your content.)

        The more complete the content, the more accurate the headlines.)

# ===========================================================

IF content_type == "news":
    Primary styles:
        - Declarative (states the news)
        - Data-driven (leads with numbers)
        - Action-oriented (emphasizes verb)

IF content_type == "feature":
    Primary styles:
        - Narrative (hints at story)
        - Character-driven (focuses on people)
        - Scene-setting (evokes place/time)

IF content_type == "analysis":
    Primary styles:
        - Question (poses the issue)
        - Thesis (states the argument)
        - Provocative (challenges assumption)

IF content_type == "how-to":
    Primary styles:
        - Instructional (How to...)
        - Benefit-focused (Learn/Discover...)
        - Numbered (X Ways to...)

Platform considerations for {target_platform}:
    - Word limit: {max_headline_words}
    - Character considerations: [platform-specific]
    - Tone expectations: [platform-specific]

# ===========================================================

# ===========================================================

============================================================

Content: [brief summary]
Max Words: {max_headline_words}
============================================================

    "[Text under max_headline_words]"
    Approach: [style used]
    Word count: [count]

    "[Text with number or statistic]"
    Approach: [style used]
    Word count: [count]

    "[Text that creates interest gap]"
    Approach: [style used]
    Word count: [count]

    "[Text emphasizing reader value]"
    Approach: [style used]
    Word count: [count]

HEADLINE 5: [Alternative/Creative]
    "[Text using unique angle]"
    Approach: [style used]
    Word count: [count]

============================================================

# ===========================================================
# STEP 4: HEADLINE ANALYSIS AND RANKING
# ===========================================================

#AI->H::Status: (Evaluating and ranking headlines)

Evaluation criteria:
    - Clarity (1-5): Does it communicate clearly?
    - Accuracy (1-5): Does it represent content?
    - Engagement (1-5): Does it compel clicks?
    - SEO Value (1-5): Does it include keywords?
    - Platform Fit (1-5): Does it suit {target_platform}?

============================================================
HEADLINE RANKINGS
============================================================

RANK 1: Headline [X]
    Scores: Clarity [X] | Accuracy [X] | Engagement [X]
            SEO [X] | Platform [X] | TOTAL: [X/25]
    Rationale: [Why this ranks highest]

RANK 2: Headline [X]
    Scores: [breakdown]
    Rationale: [Why this ranks second]

RANK 3: Headline [X]
    Scores: [breakdown]
    Rationale: [Key trade-offs]

RANK 4: Headline [X]
    Scores: [breakdown]
    Best for: [Specific use case]

RANK 5: Headline [X]
    Scores: [breakdown]
    Best for: [Specific use case]

============================================================

# ===========================================================
# STEP 5: LEAD PARAGRAPH STYLE SELECTION
# ===========================================================

#AI->H::Status: (Selecting lead paragraph approaches)

Based on content_type = {content_type}:

Lead style options:
    - Summary: Covers Five Ws concisely
    - Anecdotal: Opens with human moment
    - Scene-Setting: Establishes place/time
    - Question: Poses central issue
    - Contrast: Juxtaposes then/now
    - Expert: Leads with authoritative voice

Selected approaches for {lead_count} variations:
    1. [Primary approach based on content type]
    2. [Secondary approach for variety]
    3. [Alternative for different effect]

# ===========================================================
# STEP 6: LEAD PARAGRAPH GENERATION
# ===========================================================

#AI->H::Status: (Generating {lead_count} lead variations)

Generate distinct lead approaches:

============================================================

============================================================

LEAD 1: SUMMARY STYLE
    "[One-two sentences covering Five Ws. Who did what, when, where, and why it matters.]"

    Five Ws Check:
        - Who: [present/addressed]
        - What: [present/addressed]
        - When: [present/addressed]
        - Where: [present/addressed]
        - Why: [present/addressed]

    Word count: [count]
    Standalone test: [Can this summarize the article? Y/N]

    "[Opens with specific human moment, scene, or detail that draws reader in before delivering news value.]"

    Word count: [count]

    "[Alternative approach providing different entry point to the same content.]"

    Word count: [count]

# ===========================================================

============================================================

    Headline: [Rank 1 headline]
    Lead: [Best matching lead]

    Lead: [Matching lead]
    Rationale: [Why these work together]

    Lead: [Engaging lead]
    Rationale: [Why these drive shares]

# ===========================================================

        - Headline integration: [which headlines include it]

    - Under 60 characters: [optimized version]
    - Meta description draft: [155 characters]

    Social Media (Short):
        - Twitter/X: [Under 100 characters]
        - LinkedIn: [Professional tone version]

        - Option 2: [Benefit-focused]
        - Option 3: [News-driven]

# ===========================================================

============================================================

    Headline: [Top ranked]
    Lead: [Best match]
    Use case: [Primary publication]

    Headline: [Alternative]
    Lead: [Match]
    Use case: [Alternative context]
