    Test: [Headline A] vs [Headline B]
    Hypothesis: [What you might learn]
    Metric: [What to measure]

COMPLETE ASSET PACKAGE:
    - {headline_count} headline options (ranked)
    - {lead_count} lead paragraph options
    - [X] recommended combinations
    - Social media variations
    - SEO-optimized versions

============================================================

#AI->H::Note: (Your headline and lead package is complete. Use the rankings as guidance, but trust your editorial
    judgment for your specific audience.)

#AI->H::Question: (Would you like me to generate additional variations, optimize for a different platform, or help
    with another aspect of this content?)
    """,

    outputs={
        "headlines_ranked": "{headline_count} headline options, each scored /25 and ranked with rationale",
        "leads": "{lead_count} distinct lead paragraphs, each with word count and (for summary) a Five Ws check",
        "recommended_combinations": "Best-overall, alternative, and social-optimized headline+lead pairings",
        "seo_platform_variations": "SEO title (<60 chars), meta description, and Twitter/LinkedIn/email variants",

# START RECIPE-ID: RCP-007-005-001
# ===========================================================
# CRAFT RECIPE: Claim Verification Engine
# Created: January 2, 2026 (source v2.00a, JOURNALIST-PROCESS cookbook)
# Revised: v3.00a — 2026-06-27 (P062-SP11 Phase 9, P062-H027)
# Creator: CRAFT (Journalist-Process cookbook)
# Upgraded by: P062-Cat (SP11 — v2.00a→v3.00a transform)
# Status: Official (CFT-FWK-COOKBK-JOURNALIST-PROCESS)
# ===========================================================

# ===========================================================
# GENERAL
# ===========================================================
Recipe Type:  Cookbook recipe (Official)
Name:         RCP-007-005-001
Description:  Systematically extracts every factual claim from an article draft and verifies each one
              individually — categorizing claims, assigning priority and a verification status, documenting
              evidence, and producing a verification report with strengthening recommendations.

# ===========================================================
# CATEGORIES
# ===========================================================
Part Of Cookbook:   CFT-FWK-COOKBK-JOURNALIST-PROCESS
Category ID:        007  (CAT-007-JOURNALIST-PROCESS)
Subcategory ID:    005  (SUBCAT-005-EDITING-FACTCHECK)
Recipe ID Number:  RCP-007-005-001
Fully-Qualified:   CFT-FWK-COOKBK-JOURNALIST-PROCESS::RCP-007-005-001
Status:            Official
Categories:        Journalist Process
Subcategories:     Editing & Fact-Checking
Tags:              claim · verification · fact-check · accuracy · evidence · sources · truth · validation
Recommended Persona: Fernand — Quality Validator (namespaced: PERSONA-JOURNALIST-PROCESS-FERNAND-CARD.txt)
Difficulty:        Intermediate

# ===========================================================
# INSTRUCTIONS
# ===========================================================
1. Confirm inputs: article_draft is required; content_type, priority_areas, and verification_depth are optional.
   If no draft is provided, ask for the complete text before proceeding.
2. Adopt Fernand's quality-validation framing: systematically extract and verify every factual claim before
   publication; never fabricate — if a claim cannot be confirmed, say so.
3. DRAFT INTAKE — confirm receipt and assess content type, approximate word count, subject matter, and
   verification depth. If priority_areas are given, note that those claims will be prioritized.
4. CLAIM EXTRACTION — read the entire draft and extract claims into the six fixed categories:
   A. Statistics & Numbers · B. Dates & Timelines · C. Names & Titles · D. Direct Quotes ·
   E. Institutional Facts · F. General Assertions. List each with its location and a total count.
5. PRIORITY ASSESSMENT — evaluate each claim against the criteria (central to thesis, impact if wrong, reader
   scrutiny, verification ease) and assign HIGH / MEDIUM / LOW priority with a brief reason each.
6. SYSTEMATIC VERIFICATION — for each claim assess consistency with known information, plausibility of numbers
   and dates, accuracy of names/titles, and attribution accuracy of quotes, using the per-category approach.
7. STATUS ASSIGNMENT — assign one status per claim: VERIFIED · LIKELY ACCURATE · UNVERIFIED · QUESTIONABLE ·
   CONTRADICTED, grouping results under each status with evidence/notes/concern/conflict as defined.
8. EVIDENCE DOCUMENTATION — for each non-verified claim, record why verification was not possible, what evidence
   would confirm it, suggested sources, and the risk level if published unverified.
9. VERIFICATION REPORT — compile summary statistics (counts + percentages per status), a confidence assessment
   (overall accuracy High/Medium/Low, concerns, strengths), high-priority issues, and detailed findings.
10. STRENGTHENING RECOMMENDATIONS — for each UNVERIFIED or QUESTIONABLE claim, offer options A. VERIFY (source
    to consult) · B. HEDGE (alternative phrasing) · C. REMOVE (if non-essential) + a recommended action.
11. SUMMARY & NEXT STEPS — give an executive summary (claims checked, issues, recommended actions, overall
    assessment) and next steps. Hand verified claims forward to Source Alignment (RCP-007-005-002) and, before
    publication, to Publication Risk (RCP-007-005-003).

# ===========================================================
# CUSTOM FIELDS
# ===========================================================
Recipe FAQ:
  Q: What is a "claim" here? A: any factual assertion — statistic, date, name/title, quote, institutional fact,
     or general assertion — that could be confirmed or contradicted.
  Q: What do the five statuses mean? A: VERIFIED (confirmed accurate), LIKELY ACCURATE (plausible/consistent),
     UNVERIFIED (cannot confirm; needs source), QUESTIONABLE (appears potentially wrong), CONTRADICTED
     (conflicts with known information).
  Q: How deep does it go? A: verification_depth = quick | standard (default) | thorough.
How A.I. Reads This Recipe:
  Execute as Fernand (Quality Validator). Verification posture; extract every claim, never fabricate evidence
  or sources — if a claim cannot be verified, mark it UNVERIFIED and say what would be needed.
Recipe Short Description: Systematic, claim-by-claim fact-checking engine for article drafts.
When To Use: at the start of the editing/fact-check stage, once a complete draft exists, to surface every
  factual claim and its verification status before source alignment and risk scanning.
Actual Examples: article_draft="[complete draft text]", content_type="news", verification_depth="thorough",
  priority_areas=["financial figures", "executive titles"].
Recipe Name: RCP-007-005-001
Included In Cookbook: CFT-FWK-COOKBK-JOURNALIST-PROCESS
Recommended Prompt Framework: CRAFT #H->AI / #AI->H comment protocol.
Extension Of: — (entry recipe of the Editing & Fact-Checking subcategory)

  v3.00a — 2026-06-27 (SP11 P9, P062-H027): v2.00a→v3.00a transform. Canonical id RCP-007-005-001 (dropped the
    in-id name + version suffix). ALIAS NOTE: the source body START/END markers name this recipe
    "CLAIM-VERIFICATION-ENGINE" (long form) while the master-index id and the in-body recipe_id use the short
    form "CLAIM-VERIFY" — the master-index short name is canonical; the long marker name is recorded here as an
    alias. Re-pointed inline cross-references to canonical ids (SOURCE-ALIGNMENT-AUDITOR → RCP-007-005-002;
    PUBLICATION-RISK-SCANNER → RCP-007-005-003). Replaced the generic "I will systematically..." directive with

# ===========================================================
# ACTUAL RECIPE CODE
# ===========================================================

# --- PERSONA CONFIGURATION ---
# {PERSONA_NAME}=Fernand  {PERSONA_TITLE}=Quality Validator
# file_reference = PERSONA-JOURNALIST-PROCESS-FERNAND-CARD.txt  (namespaced; canonical identity preserved)

CLAIM_VERIFICATION_ENGINE_RECIPE = Recipe(
    recipe_id="RCP-007-005-001",
    title="Claim Verification Engine",
    description="Systematic, claim-by-claim fact-checking of all factual claims in an article draft",
    category="CAT-007-JOURNALIST-PROCESS",
    subcategory="SUBCAT-005-EDITING-FACTCHECK",
    difficulty="Intermediate",
    estimated_time="20-40 min",
    version="3.00a",
    dependencies=["RCP-007-004-003"],
    used_by=["RCP-007-005-002"],

    parameters={
        "article_draft":      {"type": "string", "required": True,  "description": "Complete draft to verify"},
        "content_type":       {"type": "string", "required": False, "default": "general", "options": ["news", "feature", "analysis", "technical", "opinion"], "description": "Type of content"},
        "priority_areas":     {"type": "list",   "required": False, "description": "Specific areas to prioritize"},
        "verification_depth": {"type": "string", "required": False, "default": "standard", "options": ["quick", "standard", "thorough"], "description": "Level of verification detail"}
    },

    prompt_template="""
    # =======================================================
    # CLAIM VERIFICATION ENGINE
    # =======================================================

    #H->AI::Directive: (Adopt the Fernand — Quality Validator persona: a meticulous fact-checker who
        systematically extracts and verifies every factual claim in a draft before publication. Never
        fabricate evidence or sources; if a claim cannot be confirmed, say so and route it onward.)

    #AI->H::Status: (Initializing Claim Verification Engine)
    "I will systematically extract every factual claim from your draft and verify each one individually,
    ensuring comprehensive fact-checking before publication."

    # --- STEP 1: DRAFT INTAKE ---
    #AI->H::Status: (Receiving draft for verification)
    IF article_draft provided:
        Confirm receipt and assess: content type {content_type}; approximate word count [calculated];
        subject matter [identified]; verification depth {verification_depth}.
        IF priority_areas provided: #AI->H::Note: (I will prioritize claims related to: {priority_areas})
        #AI->H::Note: (Draft received. Beginning systematic claim extraction.)
    ELSE:
        #AI->H::RequiredQuestion: (Please provide the article draft you want fact-checked. Paste the
            complete text for comprehensive verification.)

    # --- STEP 2: CLAIM EXTRACTION ---
    #AI->H::Status: (Extracting all factual claims)
    Read the entire draft and extract claims into CLAIM CATEGORIES:
        A. Statistics and Numbers (percentages, dollar amounts, counts, growth rates, market sizes, metrics)
        B. Dates and Timelines (specific dates, years, periods, event sequences, durations)
        C. Names and Titles (people's names/positions, company names/descriptions, institutional affiliations)
        D. Direct Quotes (attributed statements, paraphrased positions)
        E. Institutional Facts (company details, founding dates, organizational structures)
        F. General Assertions (causal claims, trend statements, comparative statements)
    Output EXTRACTED CLAIMS by category, each as "[id]. [claim text] - Location: [paragraph/sentence]",
    then Total Claims Extracted: [count].

    # --- STEP 3: PRIORITY ASSESSMENT ---
    #AI->H::Status: (Assessing verification priorities)
    Evaluate each claim on: central to thesis · impact if wrong · reader scrutiny · verification ease.
    Output PRIORITY ASSIGNMENTS: HIGH (verify first) / MEDIUM (as time permits) / LOW (optional), each
    with claim id + reason.

    # --- STEP 4: SYSTEMATIC VERIFICATION ---
    #AI->H::Status: (Verifying claims against available knowledge)
    For each claim evaluate: consistency with known information; plausibility of numbers/dates; accuracy of
    names/titles; attribution accuracy of quotes. Per-category approach — Statistics: check plausibility/known
    ranges; Dates: confirm timelines; Names: verify titles/affiliations; Quotes: assess attribution;
    Assertions: evaluate logical consistency.

    # --- STEP 5: STATUS ASSIGNMENT ---
    #AI->H::Status: (Assigning verification status to claims)
    STATUS DEFINITIONS: VERIFIED (confirmed accurate) · LIKELY ACCURATE (plausible, consistent) ·
    UNVERIFIED (cannot confirm/deny; needs source) · QUESTIONABLE (appears potentially inaccurate) ·
    CONTRADICTED (conflicts with known information).
    Output VERIFICATION RESULTS grouped by status, each claim with id + text + (Evidence | Note | Concern |
    Conflict) as appropriate.

    # --- STEP 6: EVIDENCE DOCUMENTATION ---
    #AI->H::Status: (Documenting verification reasoning)
    For each non-verified claim: why verification was not possible; what evidence would confirm it; suggested
    sources to consult; risk level if published unverified.

    # --- STEP 7: VERIFICATION REPORT ---
    #AI->H::Status: (Compiling verification report)
    Produce CLAIM VERIFICATION REPORT (Article, Date, Verification Depth {verification_depth}) with:
        SUMMARY STATISTICS — Total Claims Checked + per-status counts and percentages.
        CONFIDENCE ASSESSMENT — Overall Article Accuracy [High/Medium/Low]; Areas of Concern; Strengths.
        HIGH PRIORITY ISSUES — numbered issue + recommendation.
        DETAILED FINDINGS — full claim-by-claim results organized by category.

    # --- STEP 8: STRENGTHENING RECOMMENDATIONS ---
    #AI->H::Status: (Providing recommendations for improvement)
    For each UNVERIFIED or QUESTIONABLE claim output: id + text; Current Status; Options
        A. VERIFY [specific source]; B. HEDGE [alternative phrasing]; C. REMOVE [if not essential];
        Recommended Action: [A/B/C with rationale].

    # --- STEP 9: SUMMARY AND NEXT STEPS ---
    #AI->H::Deliverable: (Verification report complete)
    EXECUTIVE SUMMARY: claims checked; issues identified; recommended actions; OVERALL ASSESSMENT (brief
    paragraph on factual strength). NEXT STEPS: (1) address HIGH PRIORITY issues before publication;
    (2) consider verifying MEDIUM PRIORITY items; (3) document sources for key claims.

    #AI->H::Recommendation: (For claims requiring source verification, run RCP-007-005-002 (Source Alignment
        Auditor) to check against your specific documents. Before publication, run RCP-007-005-003
        (Publication Risk Scanner) to identify legal and ethical concerns.)
    #AI->H::Question: (Would you like to proceed with source alignment verification, or do you have questions
        about any of the flagged claims?)
    """,

    outputs={
        "extracted_claims": "All factual claims, categorized A-F, with locations and a total count",
        "priority_assignments": "HIGH/MEDIUM/LOW priority per claim with rationale",
        "verification_results": "Per-claim status (VERIFIED/LIKELY ACCURATE/UNVERIFIED/QUESTIONABLE/CONTRADICTED) with evidence",
        "verification_report": "Summary statistics, confidence assessment, high-priority issues, detailed findings",
        "recommendations": "VERIFY/HEDGE/REMOVE options + recommended action for each flagged claim"
    },

    integration_notes="First recipe of the Editing & Fact-Checking stage. Depends on RCP-007-004-003 "
        "(Headline and Lead Generator) for the complete draft; feeds RCP-007-005-002 (Source Alignment "
        "Auditor) for source-grounded verification, and ultimately RCP-007-005-003 (Publication Risk Scanner) "

    changelog="v3.00a (P062-H027): persona-framed to Fernand; Section 9 added; ids normalized + cross-refs "

    ai_to_ai_communication={
        "schema_version": "1.1",
        "schema_profile": "Option-B typed-envelope (H041 LOCKED canonical)",
        "authored_by": "P062-Cat - SP11 Journalist-Process cookbook build (P062-H027)",
        "envelope": [
            {"type": "prose",
             "body": "HANDOFF CONTRACT: emits a categorized claim inventory (A-F) with per-claim verification "
                     "status (VERIFIED / LIKELY ACCURATE / UNVERIFIED / QUESTIONABLE / CONTRADICTED), an "

             "body": "EXECUTION GUIDANCE: run as Fernand (verification posture). Extract claims exhaustively "

                     "MEDIUM/LOW claims you chase, never by skipping HIGH-priority ones. Distinguish "
                     "knowledge-based plausibility (this recipe) from source-grounded proof (005-002)."},

             "preamble": "EDGE CASES:",
             "items": [
                {"key": "no_draft", "body": "If article_draft is missing, stop and issue the RequiredQuestion "

                     "QUESTIONABLE/CONTRADICTED. Reserve QUESTIONABLE/CONTRADICTED for claims that conflict "
                     "with known information; never downgrade 'I don't know' into 'this is wrong.'"},
                {"key": "opinion_content", "body": "For content_type 'opinion', verify the embedded factual "

             ]},

             "body": "Pulling the full claim inventory before assigning any status is the single biggest "
                     "accuracy lever — verifiers who judge as they read systematically miss claims buried in "
                     "subordinate clauses and paraphrased attributions."},
            {"key": "unverified_is_an_answer",
             "body": "Marking a claim UNVERIFIED and routing it to source alignment is a successful outcome, "
                     "not a failure; the failure mode is asserting VERIFIED on plausibility alone, which lets "
                     "fabricated-sounding numbers survive to the editorial gate."},
            {"key": "hedge_beats_delete",
             "body": "For a non-essential but unconfirmable claim, a HEDGE ('reportedly', 'according to X') "
                     "usually preserves more of the story's value than a REMOVE — offer the hedge phrasing "
                     "explicitly so the writer can accept it in one step."}
        ]
    }
)

# START RECIPE-ID: RCP-007-005-002
# ===========================================================
# CRAFT RECIPE: Source Alignment Auditor
# Created: January 2, 2026 (source v2.00a, JOURNALIST-PROCESS cookbook)
# Revised: v3.00a — 2026-06-27 (P062-SP11 Phase 9, P062-H027)
# Creator: CRAFT (Journalist-Process cookbook)
# Upgraded by: P062-Cat (SP11 — v2.00a→v3.00a transform)
# Status: Official (CFT-FWK-COOKBK-JOURNALIST-PROCESS)
# ===========================================================

# ===========================================================
# GENERAL
# ===========================================================
Recipe Type:  Cookbook recipe (Official)
Name:         RCP-007-005-002
Description:  Verifies an article draft EXCLUSIVELY against supplied source documents (no external knowledge) —
              cataloging sources, extracting verifiable claims, mapping claims to sources, assigning a grounded
              status, building an evidence audit trail, flagging discrepancies, and giving remediation guidance.

# ===========================================================
# CATEGORIES
# ===========================================================
Part Of Cookbook:   CFT-FWK-COOKBK-JOURNALIST-PROCESS
Category ID:        007  (CAT-007-JOURNALIST-PROCESS)
Subcategory ID:    005  (SUBCAT-005-EDITING-FACTCHECK)
Recipe ID Number:  RCP-007-005-002
Fully-Qualified:   CFT-FWK-COOKBK-JOURNALIST-PROCESS::RCP-007-005-002
Status:            Official
Categories:        Journalist Process
Subcategories:     Editing & Fact-Checking
Tags:              source · alignment · auditor · grounding · attribution · citation · cross-reference · integrity
Recommended Persona: Fernand — Quality Validator (namespaced: PERSONA-JOURNALIST-PROCESS-FERNAND-CARD.txt)
Difficulty:        Advanced

# ===========================================================
# INSTRUCTIONS
# ===========================================================
1. Confirm inputs: article_draft AND source_documents are both required; verification_scope and output_format
   are optional. If either required input is missing, ask for it before proceeding.
2. Adopt Fernand's quality-validation framing in GROUNDED VERIFICATION MODE: verify claims ONLY against the
   provided sources; do NOT use external knowledge. Any claim not addressed by the sources is UNVERIFIABLE
   regardless of general knowledge.
3. SOURCE DOCUMENT COLLECTION — catalog and label each source in a SOURCE REGISTRY (Title/Description, Type
   [Interview/Report/Data/Other], approximate length, key topics) and report a total source count. If no
   sources are given, request clearly-labeled sources (e.g. "SOURCE A (CEO Interview): ...").
4. DRAFT ALIGNMENT SETUP — confirm verification scope ({verification_scope}) and output format
   ({output_format}); note that verification is limited exclusively to the provided sources. Request the draft
   if missing.
5. CLAIM EXTRACTION — extract all claims that could be verified against sources, grouped as QUOTES AND
   ATTRIBUTIONS (Q#), STATISTICS AND DATA (D#), FACTS AND ASSERTIONS (F#), each with a location; report a total.
6. SOURCE-BY-SOURCE ANALYSIS — for each source, identify which claims it is relevant to and how many key
   passages, then a Coverage Analysis (claims covered vs. not addressed).
7. CLAIM-BY-CLAIM VERIFICATION — assign one grounded status per claim: VERIFIED (source directly and accurately
   supports) · CONTRADICTED (source conflicts) · UNVERIFIABLE (sources do not address). For each: Status,
   Source letter, exact Evidence quote, and an Assessment of how the source supports/contradicts/ignores it.
8. EVIDENCE CITATION — for each verified or contradicted claim, build an EVIDENCE AUDIT TRAIL (Draft Text,
   Source letter+title, exact Source Quote, Page/Location if available, Determination with reasoning).
9. DISCREPANCY IDENTIFICATION — list CRITICAL DISCREPANCIES (factual errors, with draft vs. source text + risk
   level), MINOR DISCREPANCIES (precision issues), and MISSING CONTEXT (what the draft omits + impact).
10. ALIGNMENT REPORT — compile summary statistics (VERIFIED/CONTRADICTED/UNVERIFIABLE counts + percentages),
    source utilization, an ALIGNMENT SCORE (% of claims verified), and the critical issues list.
11. REMEDIATION GUIDANCE — CONTRADICTED claims (MUST FIX): current text → corrected text per source + source
    reference. UNVERIFIABLE claims: options A. supply more source documentation · B. remove the claim ·
    C. add hedge language, with a recommendation. Then hand forward to RCP-007-005-003 (Publication Risk
    Scanner) for legal/ethical review before publication.

# ===========================================================
# CUSTOM FIELDS
# ===========================================================
Recipe FAQ:
  Q: How is this different from RCP-007-005-001? A: Claim Verification (005-001) checks claims against general
     knowledge for plausibility; Source Alignment (005-002) checks them ONLY against the user's own source
     documents — fully grounded, no external knowledge.
  Q: What do the three statuses mean? A: VERIFIED (a source directly and accurately supports the claim),
     CONTRADICTED (a source conflicts with it), UNVERIFIABLE (no source addresses it).
  Q: What scope options exist? A: verification_scope = comprehensive (default) | quotes-only | data-only;
     output_format = report (default) | table | detailed.
How A.I. Reads This Recipe:
  Execute as Fernand (Quality Validator) in grounded mode. Use ONLY the supplied sources; quote exact evidence;
  mark anything the sources do not address UNVERIFIABLE even if you "know" it from general knowledge.
Recipe Short Description: Source-grounded, audit-trail verification of a draft against the writer's own sources.
When To Use: after claim verification, when the writer has the original source documents and needs every quote,
  statistic, and fact traced to a specific source before publication.
Actual Examples: article_draft="[draft text]", source_documents="SOURCE A (CEO interview transcript)...
  SOURCE B (Q3 report)...", verification_scope="quotes-only", output_format="table".
Recipe Name: RCP-007-005-002
Included In Cookbook: CFT-FWK-COOKBK-JOURNALIST-PROCESS
Recommended Prompt Framework: CRAFT #H->AI / #AI->H comment protocol.
Extension Of: RCP-007-005-001 (Claim Verification Engine) — same subcategory; consumes its UNVERIFIED list.
Version History:
  v3.00a — 2026-06-27 (SP11 P9, P062-H027): v2.00a→v3.00a transform. Canonical id RCP-007-005-002 (dropped the
    in-id name + version suffix). ALIAS NOTE: the source body START/END markers name this recipe
    "SOURCE-ALIGNMENT-AUDITOR" (long form) while the master-index id and in-body recipe_id use the short form
    "SOURCE-ALIGN" — the master-index short name is canonical; the long marker name is recorded here as an
    alias. Re-pointed inline cross-reference (PUBLICATION-RISK-SCANNER → RCP-007-005-003). Replaced the generic
    grounded-mode directive with the Fernand — Quality Validator persona framing (SUBCAT-005-EDITING-FACTCHECK
    section persona). ADDED Section 9 ai_to_ai_communication (Option-B typed envelope, schema 1.1) + 3 content
    lessons_learned. Removed flavor/tier residue (SP09/SP10) — none present in-recipe. Promoted Version History
    to its own field. METADATA preserved faithfully from the source COOKBOOK_MASTER_INDEX entry: subcategory
    SUBCAT-005-EDITING-FACTCHECK (source name, NOT relabeled), difficulty "advanced", dependencies
    ["RCP-007-005-001"], used_by ["RCP-007-005-003"], validated_by Auguste (source). RECONCILED the in-body
    category field "CAT-007" (short form) up to the canonical "CAT-007-JOURNALIST-PROCESS" (source KNOWN
    DISCREPANCY #4). All parameters, 9 steps, the grounded-mode caution, status definitions, evidence audit
    trail, discrepancy tiers, and remediation options preserved verbatim in meaning. No capability added or
    removed.
  v2.00a — 2026-01-02: source recipe (JOURNALIST-PROCESS cookbook, COOKBOOK_MASTER_INDEX form).

SOURCE_ALIGNMENT_AUDITOR_RECIPE = Recipe(
    recipe_id="RCP-007-005-002",
    title="Source Alignment Auditor",
    description="Grounded verification of an article draft against the writer's own source documents only",
    category="CAT-007-JOURNALIST-PROCESS",
    subcategory="SUBCAT-005-EDITING-FACTCHECK",
    difficulty="Advanced",
    estimated_time="30-50 min",
    version="3.00a",
    dependencies=["RCP-007-005-001"],
    used_by=["RCP-007-005-003"],

    parameters={
        "article_draft":      {"type": "string", "required": True,  "description": "Draft to verify against sources"},
        "source_documents":   {"type": "string", "required": True,  "description": "Source docs for verification"},
        "verification_scope": {"type": "string", "required": False, "default": "comprehensive", "options": ["comprehensive", "quotes-only", "data-only"], "description": "Focus area for verification"},
        "output_format":      {"type": "string", "required": False, "default": "report", "options": ["report", "table", "detailed"], "description": "Format for results"}
    },

    prompt_template="""
    # =======================================================
    # SOURCE ALIGNMENT AUDITOR
    # =======================================================

    #H->AI::Directive: (Adopt the Fernand — Quality Validator persona in GROUNDED VERIFICATION MODE: verify
        the draft's claims ONLY against the provided source documents. Do NOT use external knowledge. Every
        determination must be traceable to the supplied sources.)

    #AI->H::Status: (Initializing Source Alignment Auditor)
    "I will verify your draft exclusively against the source documents you provide. I will NOT use any external
    knowledge. This ensures every verification is traceable to your trusted sources."
    #AI->H::Caution: (GROUNDED VERIFICATION MODE ACTIVE — all determinations are based solely on the provided
        sources. Claims not addressed by sources are marked UNVERIFIABLE regardless of general knowledge.)

    # --- STEP 1: SOURCE DOCUMENT COLLECTION ---
    #AI->H::Status: (Cataloging provided sources)
    IF source_documents provided:
        Build a SOURCE REGISTRY — for each: SOURCE [letter]: Title/Description; Type [Interview/Report/Data/
        Other]; Length [approx word count]; Key Topics. Then Total Sources: [count].
        #AI->H::Note: (I have registered {count} sources and will use only these to evaluate claims.)
    ELSE:
        #AI->H::RequiredQuestion: (Please provide the source documents, each clearly labeled, e.g.
            "SOURCE A (CEO Interview): [transcript]" / "SOURCE B (Q3 Report): [report]". Clear labels make
            the audit trail more useful.)

    # --- STEP 2: DRAFT ALIGNMENT SETUP ---
    #AI->H::Status: (Establishing verification scope)
    IF article_draft provided:
        Confirm: Scope {verification_scope}; Output {output_format}.
        #AI->H::Note: (Draft received. Verification limited EXCLUSIVELY to provided sources. Beginning claim
            extraction.)
    ELSE:
        #AI->H::RequiredQuestion: (Please provide the article draft you want verified against your sources.)

    # --- STEP 3: CLAIM EXTRACTION ---
    #AI->H::Status: (Extracting verifiable claims from draft)
    Output EXTRACTED CLAIMS FOR VERIFICATION grouped as: QUOTES AND ATTRIBUTIONS (Q1, Q2, ... + location);
    STATISTICS AND DATA (D1, D2, ... + location); FACTS AND ASSERTIONS (F1, F2, ... + location). Then Total
    Claims to Verify: [count].

    # --- STEP 4: SOURCE-BY-SOURCE ANALYSIS ---
    #AI->H::Status: (Mapping source content to claims)
    For each source output SOURCE [letter]: relevant-to-claims [ids]; key passages identified [count]. Then
    Coverage Analysis: claims covered by sources [count]; claims not addressed [count].

    # --- STEP 5: CLAIM-BY-CLAIM VERIFICATION ---
    #AI->H::Status: (Verifying claims against sources only)
    STATUS DEFINITIONS: VERIFIED (source directly and accurately supports) · CONTRADICTED (source conflicts) ·
    UNVERIFIABLE (sources do not address). For each claim output: id + draft text; Status; Source [letter];
    Evidence "[exact quote from source]"; Assessment [how source supports/contradicts/ignores].

    # --- STEP 6: EVIDENCE CITATION ---
    #AI->H::Status: (Documenting evidence trail)
    For each verified/contradicted claim output an EVIDENCE AUDIT TRAIL: Draft Text "[exact]"; Source [letter +
    title]; Source Quote "[exact]"; Page/Location [if available]; Determination [status + reasoning].

    # --- STEP 7: DISCREPANCY IDENTIFICATION ---
    #AI->H::Status: (Identifying alignment problems)
    Output DISCREPANCIES FOUND in three tiers: CRITICAL DISCREPANCIES (factual errors — draft states vs. source
    states + Risk Level High/Medium/Low); MINOR DISCREPANCIES (precision issues); MISSING CONTEXT (draft omits
    + impact).

    # --- STEP 8: ALIGNMENT REPORT ---
    #AI->H::Status: (Compiling alignment report)
    Produce SOURCE ALIGNMENT REPORT (Article, Date, Sources Used [count], Scope {verification_scope}) with:
    SUMMARY STATISTICS (Total Claims Checked + VERIFIED/CONTRADICTED/UNVERIFIABLE counts and percentages);
    SOURCE UTILIZATION (claims verified per source); ALIGNMENT SCORE ([%] of claims verified); CRITICAL ISSUES
    [count + list].

    # --- STEP 9: REMEDIATION GUIDANCE ---
    #AI->H::Status: (Providing correction guidance)
    CONTRADICTED CLAIMS — MUST FIX: id; current text "[draft]"; corrected text "[per source]"; source reference.
    UNVERIFIABLE CLAIMS — OPTIONS: A. provide additional source documentation; B. remove claim; C. add hedge
    language "[suggested phrasing]"; Recommendation [A/B/C].
    #AI->H::Deliverable: (Source alignment audit complete)
    NEXT STEPS: (1) address all CONTRADICTED claims immediately; (2) decide how to handle UNVERIFIABLE claims;
    (3) run RCP-007-005-003 (Publication Risk Scanner) for legal/ethical review before publication.
    #AI->H::Question: (Would you like to proceed to risk scanning, or do you have additional sources to verify
        remaining claims?)
    """,

    outputs={
        "source_registry": "Cataloged, labeled sources with type, length, key topics, and total count",
        "extracted_claims": "Verifiable claims grouped as quotes (Q#), data (D#), facts (F#) with locations",
        "coverage_analysis": "Per-source relevance map + claims-covered vs. claims-not-addressed counts",
        "verification_results": "Per-claim grounded status (VERIFIED/CONTRADICTED/UNVERIFIABLE) with exact source evidence",
        "evidence_audit_trail": "Draft text + exact source quote + determination for each verified/contradicted claim",
        "discrepancies": "Critical / minor / missing-context discrepancies with risk levels",
        "alignment_report": "Summary statistics, source utilization, alignment score, critical issues",
        "remediation": "MUST-FIX corrections for contradicted claims + A/B/C options for unverifiable claims"
    },

    integration_notes="Second recipe of the Editing & Fact-Checking stage. Depends on RCP-007-005-001 (Claim "
        "Verification Engine) and consumes its UNVERIFIED/QUESTIONABLE list; feeds RCP-007-005-003 (Publication "
        "Risk Scanner). Operates in grounded mode — uses only the writer's supplied sources. Run by Fernand "
        "(Quality Validator).",

    changelog="v3.00a (P062-H027): persona-framed to Fernand; Section 9 added; ids normalized + cross-ref "

    ai_to_ai_communication={
        "schema_version": "1.1",
        "schema_profile": "Option-B typed-envelope (H041 LOCKED canonical)",

             "body": "Determinations backed by a copied exact source quote survive editorial challenge; "

# START RECIPE-ID: RCP-007-005-003
# ===========================================================
# CRAFT RECIPE: Publication Risk Scanner
# Created: January 2, 2026 (source v2.00a, JOURNALIST-PROCESS cookbook)
# Revised: v3.00a — 2026-06-27 (P062-SP11 Phase 9, P062-H027)
# Creator: CRAFT (Journalist-Process cookbook)
# Upgraded by: P062-Cat (SP11 — v2.00a→v3.00a transform)
# Status: Official (CFT-FWK-COOKBK-JOURNALIST-PROCESS)
# ===========================================================

# ===========================================================
# GENERAL
# ===========================================================
Recipe Type:  Cookbook recipe (Official)
Name:         RCP-007-005-003
Description:  Performs an adversarial red-team scan of an article draft for legal, ethical, reputation, and
              clarity risks before publication — flagging issues (without prescribing legal fixes), grading each
              by severity, analyzing risk interactions, and producing a risk report and publication-readiness
              assessment.

# ===========================================================
# CATEGORIES
# ===========================================================
Part Of Cookbook:   CFT-FWK-COOKBK-JOURNALIST-PROCESS
Category ID:        007  (CAT-007-JOURNALIST-PROCESS)
Subcategory ID:    005  (SUBCAT-005-EDITING-FACTCHECK)
Recipe ID Number:  RCP-007-005-003
Fully-Qualified:   CFT-FWK-COOKBK-JOURNALIST-PROCESS::RCP-007-005-003
Status:            Official
Categories:        Journalist Process
Subcategories:     Editing & Fact-Checking
Tags:              risk · scanner · publication · legal · ethical · defamation · liability · compliance
Recommended Persona: Fernand — Quality Validator (namespaced: PERSONA-JOURNALIST-PROCESS-FERNAND-CARD.txt)
Difficulty:        Advanced

# ===========================================================
# INSTRUCTIONS
# ===========================================================
1. Confirm inputs: article_draft is required; publication_context, risk_tolerance, and focus_areas are optional.
   If no draft is provided, ask for it before proceeding.
2. Adopt Fernand's quality-validation framing in adversarial red-team mode: identify potential legal, ethical,
   and reputational risks. Flag issues WITHOUT suggesting fixes — empower the user to decide with appropriate
   professional guidance. Always include the disclaimer: this is NOT legal advice; for any Critical or High
   risk, consult a qualified attorney or appropriate professional before publication.
3. CONTENT INTAKE AND CONTEXT — assess subject matter, individuals/companies named, claims made, and tone. If
   publication_context is given, note it and audience considerations. Apply risk_tolerance: conservative (flag
   all potential concerns) / standard (flag likely concerns) / high (flag only significant concerns).
4. LEGAL RISK SCAN — examine DEFAMATION/LIBEL, COPYRIGHT, PRIVACY, and REGULATORY categories. Output each legal
   risk as [L#] with Severity [CRITICAL/HIGH/MEDIUM/LOW], Risk Type, exact Text in Question, Potential Issue,
   and Location.
5. ETHICAL RISK SCAN — examine BIAS, TRANSPARENCY, HARM POTENTIAL, and FAIRNESS. Output each as [E#] with the
   same fields (Severity, Risk Type, Text in Question, Potential Issue, Location).
6. REPUTATION RISK SCAN — examine OUT-OF-CONTEXT VULNERABILITY, TONE ISSUES, AUDIENCE ALIENATION, and BRAND
   INCONSISTENCY. Output each as [R#], adding an Adversarial Reading ("how critics might frame this").
7. CLARITY RISK SCAN — examine JARGON, AMBIGUITY, and COMPLEXITY. Output each as [C#] with Severity, Risk Type,
   Text in Question, Potential Issue, Location.
8. RISK CATEGORIZATION — apply the severity definitions (CRITICAL = legal action / major financial / severe
   reputation harm, requires professional consultation; HIGH = significant, may warrant professional review;
   MEDIUM = notable, addressable without outside help; LOW = minor) and list risks grouped by severity.
9. RISK REPORT — compile the PUBLICATION RISK ASSESSMENT REPORT: risk profile by type (Legal/Ethical/Reputation/
   Clarity counts) and by severity (Critical/High/Medium/Low counts), plus an OVERALL RISK LEVEL.
10. CONTEXTUAL ANALYSIS — identify COMPOUNDING RISKS, MOST LIKELY TO MATERIALIZE (given context), and HIGHEST
    IMPACT IF REALIZED.
11. SUMMARY AND GUIDANCE — deliver an executive summary (overall assessment, critical attention required,
    professional consultation recommended, publication readiness), repeat the not-legal-advice caution, and
    hand forward to RCP-007-006-001 (Editorial Quality Gate) once critical risks are addressed.

# ===========================================================
# CUSTOM FIELDS
# ===========================================================
Recipe FAQ:
  Q: Does this give fixes? A: No — by design it FLAGS risks without prescribing fixes, so the user can decide
     with professional guidance. It is NOT legal advice.
  Q: What four risk domains are scanned? A: Legal (L#), Ethical (E#), Reputation (R#), and Clarity (C#).
  Q: What controls sensitivity? A: risk_tolerance = conservative (flag all) | standard (flag likely, default) |
     high (flag only significant).
How A.I. Reads This Recipe:
  Execute as Fernand (Quality Validator) in adversarial red-team posture. Read the draft as a hostile critic
  and a cautious lawyer would. Flag, grade, and explain risks; never draft legal fixes; always surface the
  not-legal-advice disclaimer for Critical/High items.
Recipe Short Description: Adversarial legal/ethical/reputation/clarity risk scan for pre-publication drafts.
When To Use: as the final editing/fact-check step, after claim verification and source alignment, immediately
  before the editorial gate, to surface publication risks and a readiness call.
Actual Examples: article_draft="[draft text]", publication_context="national news website",
  risk_tolerance="conservative", focus_areas=["defamation", "privacy"].
Recipe Name: RCP-007-005-003
Included In Cookbook: CFT-FWK-COOKBK-JOURNALIST-PROCESS
Recommended Prompt Framework: CRAFT #H->AI / #AI->H comment protocol.
Extension Of: RCP-007-005-002 (Source Alignment Auditor) — same subcategory; final step before review.

# --- PERSONA CONFIGURATION ---
# {PERSONA_NAME}=Fernand  {PERSONA_TITLE}=Quality Validator
# file_reference = PERSONA-JOURNALIST-PROCESS-FERNAND-CARD.txt  (namespaced; canonical identity preserved)

PUBLICATION_RISK_SCANNER_RECIPE = Recipe(
    recipe_id="RCP-007-005-003",
    title="Publication Risk Scanner",
    description="Adversarial red-team scan of a draft for legal, ethical, reputation, and clarity risks pre-publication",
    category="CAT-007-JOURNALIST-PROCESS",
    subcategory="SUBCAT-005-EDITING-FACTCHECK",
    difficulty="Advanced",
    estimated_time="30-50 min",
    version="3.00a",
    dependencies=["RCP-007-005-002"],
    used_by=["RCP-007-006-001"],

    parameters={
        "article_draft":       {"type": "string", "required": True,  "description": "Draft for risk analysis"},
        "publication_context": {"type": "string", "required": False, "description": "Where content will be published"},
        "risk_tolerance":      {"type": "string", "required": False, "default": "standard", "options": ["conservative", "standard", "high"], "description": "Acceptable risk level"},
        "focus_areas":         {"type": "list",   "required": False, "description": "Specific risk types to examine"}
    },

    prompt_template="""
    # =======================================================
    # PUBLICATION RISK SCANNER
    # =======================================================

    #H->AI::Directive: (Adopt the Fernand — Quality Validator persona in adversarial red-team mode: identify
        potential legal, ethical, and reputational risks before publication. FLAG issues without suggesting
        fixes, empowering the user to decide with professional guidance.)

    #AI->H::Status: (Initializing Publication Risk Scanner)
    "I will analyze your content from an adversarial perspective, identifying potential legal, ethical, and
    reputational risks. I will flag issues without suggesting fixes, empowering you to make informed decisions
    with appropriate professional guidance."
    #AI->H::Caution: (IMPORTANT DISCLAIMER — this analysis identifies potential risks but does NOT constitute
        legal advice. For any Critical or High risk, consult a qualified attorney or appropriate professional
        before publication.)

    # --- STEP 1: CONTENT INTAKE AND CONTEXT ---
    #AI->H::Status: (Establishing analysis context)
    IF article_draft provided:
        Assess: subject matter; individuals/companies named; claims made; tone.
        IF publication_context provided: note "Publishing to {publication_context}" + audience considerations.
        Apply risk tolerance {risk_tolerance} — Conservative: flag all potential concerns; Standard: flag
        likely concerns; High: flag only significant concerns.
        #AI->H::Note: (Content received. Adopting adversarial mindset for risk analysis.)
    ELSE:
        #AI->H::RequiredQuestion: (Please provide the content you want analyzed for publication risks.)

    # --- STEP 2: LEGAL RISK SCAN ---
    #AI->H::Status: (Scanning for legal risks)
    Examine: DEFAMATION/LIBEL (negative statements about identifiable parties; unverified claims as fact;
    reputation-damaging implications); COPYRIGHT (extensive unattributed quotation; proprietary info;
    plagiarism); PRIVACY (private-info disclosure; identifiable details about private individuals; medical/
    financial/personal data); REGULATORY (unsubstantiated health/safety claims; financial advice without
    disclaimers; industry compliance). Output each as [L#] Severity [CRITICAL/HIGH/MEDIUM/LOW]; Risk Type; Text
    in Question "[exact quote]"; Potential Issue; Location.

    # --- STEP 3: ETHICAL RISK SCAN ---
    #AI->H::Status: (Scanning for ethical risks)
    Examine: BIAS (prejudiced language; one-sided presentation; stereotyping); TRANSPARENCY (undisclosed
    conflicts; hidden promotion; misleading data presentation); HARM POTENTIAL (misusable content; vulnerable
    audiences; unintended consequences); FAIRNESS (right of reply; balanced representation; opposing views).
    Output each as [E#] with Severity, Risk Type, Text in Question, Potential Issue, Location.

    # --- STEP 4: REPUTATION RISK SCAN ---
    #AI->H::Status: (Scanning for reputation risks)
    Examine: OUT-OF-CONTEXT VULNERABILITY (easily misquoted/screenshot-ready lines); TONE ISSUES (arrogant/
    dismissive/insensitive/tone-deaf); AUDIENCE ALIENATION (excluding language; offensive assumptions; divisive
    positions); BRAND INCONSISTENCY (voice departure; value contradictions; mixed messaging). Output each as
    [R#] with Severity, Risk Type, Text in Question, Potential Issue, Adversarial Reading "[how critics might
    frame this]", Location.

    # --- STEP 5: CLARITY RISK SCAN ---
    #AI->H::Status: (Scanning for clarity risks)
    Examine: JARGON (unexplained technical terms; industry language; undefined acronyms); AMBIGUITY (multiple
    interpretations; vague claims; unclear referents); COMPLEXITY (overly complex explanations; unshared assumed
    knowledge; dense passages). Output each as [C#] with Severity, Risk Type, Text in Question, Potential Issue,
    Location.

    # --- STEP 6: RISK CATEGORIZATION ---
    #AI->H::Status: (Categorizing risks by severity)
    SEVERITY DEFINITIONS: CRITICAL (legal action / significant financial damage / severe reputation harm —
    requires professional consultation); HIGH (significant; may warrant professional review); MEDIUM (notable;
    addressable without outside help); LOW (minor; address if time permits). Output RISK SUMMARY BY SEVERITY —
    Critical/High/Medium/Low, each with count + risk ids and brief descriptions.

    # --- STEP 7: RISK REPORT ---
    #AI->H::Status: (Compiling risk assessment report)
    Produce PUBLICATION RISK ASSESSMENT REPORT (Content, Date, Risk Tolerance {risk_tolerance}) with RISK
    PROFILE SUMMARY: Total Risks; by type (Legal/Ethical/Reputation/Clarity counts); by severity (Critical/High/
    Medium/Low counts); and OVERALL RISK LEVEL [CRITICAL/HIGH/MEDIUM/LOW].

    # --- STEP 8: CONTEXTUAL ANALYSIS ---
    #AI->H::Status: (Analyzing risk interactions)
    COMPOUNDING RISKS (where multiple risks combine for greater exposure); MOST LIKELY TO MATERIALIZE (given the
    publication context); HIGHEST IMPACT IF REALIZED (which risks would cause most damage).

    # --- STEP 9: SUMMARY AND GUIDANCE ---
    #AI->H::Deliverable: (Risk assessment complete)
    EXECUTIVE SUMMARY: OVERALL ASSESSMENT (brief paragraph on the risk landscape); CRITICAL ATTENTION REQUIRED
    (any CRITICAL risks); PROFESSIONAL CONSULTATION RECOMMENDED (risks warranting legal/expert review);
    PUBLICATION READINESS (whether content is ready to publish).
    #AI->H::Caution: (REMINDER — this analysis identifies risks but does not constitute legal advice. For
        CRITICAL or HIGH legal risks, consult a qualified attorney before publication.)
    #AI->H::Note: (Risk identification complete. Address critical risks before publication; address high and
        medium risks as time and resources permit.)
    #AI->H::Question: (Do you want me to elaborate on any specific risk, or are you ready to proceed with
        addressing the identified concerns?)
    """,

    outputs={
        "legal_risks": "[L#] defamation/copyright/privacy/regulatory risks with severity, exact text, location",
        "ethical_risks": "[E#] bias/transparency/harm/fairness risks with severity, exact text, location",
        "reputation_risks": "[R#] out-of-context/tone/alienation/brand risks with adversarial reading",
        "clarity_risks": "[C#] jargon/ambiguity/complexity risks with severity and location",
        "risk_report": "Risk profile by type and severity + overall risk level",
        "contextual_analysis": "Compounding risks, most-likely-to-materialize, highest-impact-if-realized",
        "executive_summary": "Overall assessment, critical attention, consultation recommendations, readiness call"
    },

    integration_notes="Final recipe of the Editing & Fact-Checking stage. Depends on RCP-007-005-002 (Source "
        "Alignment Auditor) and inherits its CONTRADICTED claims/discrepancies as legal-risk inputs; feeds "
        "RCP-007-006-001 (Editorial Quality Gate). Flags risks only — never legal advice; surfaces the "
        "not-legal-advice disclaimer for Critical/High items. Run by Fernand (Quality Validator).",

    changelog="v3.00a (P062-H027): persona-framed to Fernand; Section 9 added; id normalized; in-body category "
        "reconciled to full form; forward hand-off to RCP-007-006-001 noted; flavor/tier residue checked (none).",

    ai_to_ai_communication={
        "schema_version": "1.1",
        "schema_profile": "Option-B typed-envelope (H041 LOCKED canonical)",
        "authored_by": "P062-Cat - SP11 Journalist-Process cookbook build (P062-H027)",
        "envelope": [
            {"type": "prose",
             "body": "HANDOFF CONTRACT: emits four severity-graded risk inventories (Legal [L#], Ethical [E#], "
                     "Reputation [R#], Clarity [C#]), a risk report (counts by type and by severity + an overall "
                     "risk level), a contextual analysis (compounding / most-likely / highest-impact), and an "
                     "executive summary with a publication-readiness call. Upstream: RCP-007-005-002 (Source "
                     "Alignment Auditor) supplies CONTRADICTED claims and discrepancies that become legal/"
                     "reputation risk inputs. Downstream: RCP-007-006-001 (Editorial Quality Gate) consumes the "
                     "overall risk level and any unresolved CRITICAL/HIGH risks as gate criteria."},
            {"type": "prose",
             "body": "EXECUTION GUIDANCE: run as Fernand in adversarial red-team posture — read the draft as a "
                     "hostile critic, a plaintiff's lawyer, and a screenshot-hunting reader would. FLAG and "
                     "grade; never write the legal fix. Scale output by risk_tolerance (conservative flags all, "
                     "high flags only significant). If focus_areas are set, lead with those domains but still "
                     "complete all four scans."},
            {"type": "keyed_list",
             "preamble": "EDGE CASES:",
             "items": [
                {"key": "no_draft", "body": "If article_draft is missing, stop and issue the RequiredQuestion; "
                     "do not assess risk from a description of the content."},
                {"key": "critical_high_legal", "body": "Any CRITICAL or HIGH legal risk MUST carry the explicit "
                     "not-legal-advice disclaimer and a 'consult a qualified attorney' recommendation — never "
                     "imply the flag is a legal clearance."},
                {"key": "low_tolerance_noise", "body": "Under risk_tolerance 'high', suppress LOW/MEDIUM "
                     "clarity/tone items so CRITICAL/HIGH legal and ethical risks are not buried; under "
                     "'conservative', surface them all."}
             ]},
            {"type": "prose",
             "body": "QUALITY BAR: every risk has a domain prefix (L/E/R/C), a severity, an exact quoted text "
                     "in question, and a location; reputation risks include an adversarial reading; the report's "
                     "by-type and by-severity counts reconcile to the total; and the summary gives a clear "
                     "readiness call plus the not-legal-advice caution."}
        ],
        "lessons_learned": [
            {"key": "flag_dont_fix",
             "body": "The scanner's credibility depends on staying diagnostic — once it starts drafting legal "
                     "fixes it implies a clearance it cannot give. Name the risk and route to a professional; "
                     "let the human and their counsel decide the remedy."},
            {"key": "adversarial_reading_finds_the_real_risk",
             "body": "The highest-value reputation finds come from explicitly writing 'how a critic would frame "
                     "this in a screenshot' — neutral reading misses lines that are fine in context but toxic "
                     "in isolation."},
            {"key": "severity_must_drive_attention",
             "body": "Volume is noise; a clean by-severity rollup with the not-legal-advice disclaimer on every "
                     "CRITICAL/HIGH legal item is what actually changes the publish decision at the editorial "
                     "gate."}
        ]
    }
)

# CRAFT RECIPE: Editorial Quality Gate
# Created: January 2, 2026 (source v2.00a, JOURNALIST-PROCESS cookbook)
# Revised: v3.00a — 2026-06-27 (P062-SP11 Phase 9, P062-H027)
# Creator: CRAFT (Journalist-Process cookbook)
# Upgraded by: P062-Cat (SP11 — v2.00a→v3.00a transform)

# ===========================================================

# ===========================================================
# GENERAL
# ===========================================================
Recipe Type:  Cookbook recipe (Official)
Name:         RCP-007-006-001
Description:  Performs a comprehensive editorial quality assessment on fact-checked content. Scores five
              dimensions (clarity, structure, tone, argument strength, engagement), reviews headline and
              subheadings, and produces an editorial feedback memo with a publication-readiness rating.

# ===========================================================
# CATEGORIES
# ===========================================================
Part Of Cookbook:   CFT-FWK-COOKBK-JOURNALIST-PROCESS
Category ID:        007  (CAT-007-JOURNALIST-PROCESS)
Subcategory ID:    006  (SUBCAT-006-FINAL-REVIEW)
Recipe ID Number:  RCP-007-006-001
Fully-Qualified:   CFT-FWK-COOKBK-JOURNALIST-PROCESS::RCP-007-006-001
Status:            Official
Categories:        Journalist Process
Subcategories:     Final Review
Tags:              editorial · quality · gate · review · standards · assessment · readiness · final-check
Recommended Persona: Nellie — Managing Editor (namespaced: PERSONA-JOURNALIST-PROCESS-NELLIE-CARD.txt)
Difficulty:        Advanced

# ===========================================================
# INSTRUCTIONS
# ===========================================================
1. Confirm the inputs: article_draft is required; publication_style, target_audience, and style_guidelines are
   optional. If publication_style is not provided, ask which to evaluate against (professional, conversational,
   technical, academic). If target_audience is not provided, infer it from content type and style and note the
   inference.
2. Adopt Nellie's editorial framing: she owns editorial standards and the publish bar — assess against the
   standard, lead with the verdict and conditions, not a lecture.
3. Five-dimension assessment — for EACH dimension in [clarity, structure, tone, argument, engagement]: analyze
   the draft against the dimension criteria, identify specific strengths and specific areas needing improvement,
   assign a score 1-10, and document the findings.
4. Headline and subheading review: evaluate headline effectiveness, evaluate subheading consistency and clarity,
   and generate 2-3 alternative headline suggestions.
5. Compile the editorial memo: overall_score = average of the 5 dimension scores; include all dimension scores,
   top 3 strengths with examples, top 3 improvement areas with recommendations, headline recommendations, and a
   prioritized action list.
6. Publication-readiness rating: overall_score >= 8.0 AND all dimensions >= 7 → "READY" (proceed to the
   Publication Approval Panel, RCP-007-006-002); overall_score >= 6.0 → "NEEDS POLISH" (address priority actions,
   then re-run); otherwise → "MAJOR REVISION" (return to drafting with feedback, RCP-007-004-002, Dominique).
7. Report rating, overall score, and next step; output the editorial_memo. Fact-checking and source verification
   are upstream (RCP-007-005-001 Claim Verification / RCP-007-005-003 Risk Scanner, Fernand); for line-by-line
   fact issues Nellie invokes Fernand rather than re-checking herself.

# ===========================================================
# CUSTOM FIELDS
# ===========================================================
Recipe FAQ:
  Q: What does this gate decide? A: publication readiness — READY, NEEDS POLISH, or MAJOR REVISION — from a
     five-dimension editorial score plus a headline/subheading review.
  Q: Does it fact-check? A: no. It assumes content arrives fact-checked (from SUBCAT-005); editorial quality is
     distinct from factual accuracy. For fact concerns Nellie routes to Fernand (RCP-007-005-001).
How A.I. Reads This Recipe:
  Execute as Nellie (Managing Editor). Standards-first, verdict-first posture; score each dimension against
  explicit criteria with concrete examples; never pass a draft on impression alone — the rating thresholds are
  the gate.
Recipe Short Description: Five-dimension editorial quality gate that rates publication readiness before approval.
When To Use: at the Final Review stage, after fact-checking/risk-scanning, to decide whether a draft is ready for
  the publication approval panel or needs another pass.
Actual Examples: article_draft="[paste article text]", publication_style="professional",
  target_audience="sustainability investors", style_guidelines="[brand standards]".
Recipe Name: RCP-007-006-001
Included In Cookbook: CFT-FWK-COOKBK-JOURNALIST-PROCESS
Recommended Prompt Framework: CRAFT #H->AI / #AI->H comment protocol.
Extension Of: — (entry recipe of the Final Review subcategory; consumes RCP-007-005-003 output)

# ===========================================================
# ACTUAL RECIPE CODE

# --- PERSONA CONFIGURATION ---
# {PERSONA_NAME}=Nellie  {PERSONA_TITLE}=Managing Editor
# file_reference = PERSONA-JOURNALIST-PROCESS-NELLIE-CARD.txt  (namespaced; canonical identity preserved)

EDITORIAL_QUALITY_GATE = Recipe(
    recipe_id="RCP-007-006-001",
    title="Editorial Quality Gate",
    description="Comprehensive editorial quality assessment of fact-checked content: scores clarity, structure, "
        "tone, argument, and engagement, reviews headline/subheadings, and rates publication readiness",
    category="CAT-007-JOURNALIST-PROCESS",
    subcategory="SUBCAT-006-FINAL-REVIEW",
    difficulty="Advanced",
    estimated_time="15-25 min",
    version="3.00a",
    dependencies=["RCP-007-005-003"],
    used_by=["RCP-007-006-002"],

    parameters={
        "article_draft":     {"type": "string", "required": True,  "description": "Content to assess for quality", "example": "[paste article text]"},
        "publication_style": {"type": "string", "required": False, "options": ["professional", "conversational", "technical", "academic"], "default": "professional", "description": "Target publication style"},
        "target_audience":   {"type": "string", "required": False, "description": "Primary audience for content", "example": "[describe target readers]"},
        "style_guidelines":  {"type": "string", "required": False, "default": "none provided", "description": "Brand or publication standards"}
    },

    prompt_template="""
    #H->AI::Directive: (Adopt the Nellie — Managing Editor persona: she owns editorial standards and the publish
        decision. Execute the Editorial Quality Gate on the content below — assess all five quality dimensions and
        produce an editorial feedback memo with a publication-readiness rating.)

    # STEP 1: INITIALIZE AND ESTABLISH CONTEXT
    Receive article_draft and confirm receipt.
    IF {publication_style} not provided:
        #AI->H::Question: (What publication style should I evaluate against? Options: professional,
        conversational, technical, academic.)
        WAIT for response; SET publication_style = response
    IF {target_audience} not provided:
        Infer from content type and style
        #AI->H::Note: (Inferring target audience as [inferred_audience] based on content analysis.)

    # STEP 2-6: FIVE-DIMENSION ASSESSMENT
    FOR each dimension IN [clarity, structure, tone, argument, engagement]:
        ANALYZE article_draft for dimension criteria
        IDENTIFY specific examples of strengths
        IDENTIFY specific areas needing improvement
        ASSIGN score from 1 to 10
        DOCUMENT findings
    END FOR

    # STEP 7: HEADLINE AND SUBHEADING REVIEW
    EVALUATE headline effectiveness
    EVALUATE subheading consistency and clarity
    GENERATE 2-3 alternative headline suggestions

    # STEP 8: COMPILE EDITORIAL MEMO
    CALCULATE overall_score = average of 5 dimension scores
    GENERATE editorial memo with:
        - All dimension scores
        - Top 3 strengths with examples
        - Top 3 improvement areas with recommendations
        - Headline recommendations
        - Prioritized action list

    # STEP 9: PUBLICATION READINESS RATING
    IF overall_score >= 8.0 AND all dimensions >= 7:
        rating = "READY"; next_step = "Proceed to Publication Approval Panel (RCP-007-006-002)"
    ELSE IF overall_score >= 6.0:
        rating = "NEEDS POLISH"; next_step = "Address priority actions, then re-run"
    ELSE:
        rating = "MAJOR REVISION"; next_step = "Return to drafting with feedback (RCP-007-004-002)"

    #AI->H::Status: (Editorial Quality Gate complete. Rating: {rating}. Overall Score: {overall_score}/10.
    Next step: {next_step})

    OUTPUT editorial_memo
    """,

    outputs={
        "editorial_memo": "Memo with 5 dimension scores, top-3 strengths, top-3 improvements, headline "
            "recommendations, and a prioritized action list",
        "overall_score": "Average of the 5 dimension scores (1-10)",
        "readiness_rating": "READY | NEEDS POLISH | MAJOR REVISION, with the next step"
    },

    integration_notes="Entry recipe of the Final Review subcategory; consumes the verified, risk-assessed draft "
        "from RCP-007-005-003 (Publication Risk Scanner). A READY rating feeds RCP-007-006-002 (Publication "
        "Approval Panel); MAJOR REVISION returns to RCP-007-004-002 (Draft Composer, Dominique). Editorial "
        "quality only — for factual/source issues Nellie invokes Fernand (RCP-007-005-001).",

    changelog="v3.00a (P062-H027): persona-framed to Nellie; subcategory reconciled SUB-006 -> SUBCAT-006; id "
        "normalized; Section 9 added; flavor/tier residue check (none present).",

    ai_to_ai_communication={
        "schema_version": "1.1",
        "schema_profile": "Option-B typed-envelope (H041 LOCKED canonical)",
        "authored_by": "P062-Cat - SP11 Journalist-Process cookbook build (P062-H027)",
        "envelope": [
            {"type": "prose",
             "body": "HANDOFF CONTRACT: emits an editorial_memo (five dimension scores, top-3 strengths, top-3 "
                     "improvements, headline alternatives, prioritized actions), an overall_score, and a "
                     "readiness_rating of READY / NEEDS POLISH / MAJOR REVISION. Downstream: a READY draft plus "
                     "its memo passes to RCP-007-006-002 (Publication Approval Panel); MAJOR REVISION routes back "
                     "to RCP-007-004-002 (Draft Composer, Dominique). The overall_score may be carried into the "
                     "panel as quality_gate_score."},
            {"type": "prose",
             "body": "EXECUTION GUIDANCE: run as Nellie (standards-first, verdict-first). Score each of the five "
                     "dimensions against explicit criteria with concrete textual examples, never on impression; "
                     "the rating thresholds (>=8.0 with every dimension >=7 = READY; >=6.0 = NEEDS POLISH) ARE the "
                     "gate, so do not soften them. Assume the content is already fact-checked upstream; assess "
                     "editorial quality, not factual accuracy."},
            {"type": "keyed_list",
             "preamble": "EDGE CASES:",
             "items": [
                {"key": "high_average_one_weak_dimension", "body": "A strong average does NOT make a draft READY "
                     "if any single dimension scores below 7 — return NEEDS POLISH and name the weak dimension."},
                {"key": "missing_publication_style", "body": "If publication_style is absent, ASK before scoring "
                     "tone/engagement; evaluating against the wrong style invalidates two of the five scores."},
                {"key": "fact_concern_surfaces", "body": "If an apparent factual or sourcing problem surfaces "
                     "during the read, flag it and route to Fernand (RCP-007-005-001) rather than scoring it as "
                     "an editorial defect; this gate does not re-fact-check."}
             ]},
            {"type": "prose",
             "body": "QUALITY BAR: every dimension carries a 1-10 score backed by at least one strength example "
                     "and one improvement note; the memo lists exactly top-3 strengths and top-3 improvements "
                     "with actionable recommendations; 2-3 headline alternatives are supplied; the readiness "
                     "rating follows the thresholds exactly and names a concrete next step."}
        ],
        "lessons_learned": [
            {"key": "weakest_dimension_gates",
             "body": "Publication readiness is gated by the weakest dimension, not the average — a 9-clarity draft "
                     "with 5-structure reads as polished but loses readers; enforce the per-dimension floor."},
            {"key": "examples_make_feedback_actionable",
             "body": "Scores without a quoted example are ignored by writers; every improvement note that cites a "
                     "specific passage gets acted on, so anchor each finding to text."},
            {"key": "editorial_is_not_factual",
             "body": "Keeping the editorial gate separate from fact-checking prevents both from being done badly; "
                     "a beautifully written but unverified piece must still fail upstream, not here."}
        ]
    }
)

# CRAFT RECIPE: Publication Approval Panel
# Created: January 2, 2026 (source v2.00a, JOURNALIST-PROCESS cookbook)
# Revised: v3.00a — 2026-06-27 (P062-SP11 Phase 9, P062-H027)
# Creator: CRAFT (Journalist-Process cookbook)

# Status: Official (CFT-FWK-COOKBK-JOURNALIST-PROCESS)
# ===========================================================

# ===========================================================
# GENERAL
# ===========================================================
Recipe Type:  Cookbook recipe (Official)
Name:         RCP-007-006-002
Description:  Convenes a multi-stakeholder publication approval panel — four perspectives (Senior Editor,
              Fact-Checker, Legal Counsel, Audience Representative) — deliberates to consensus, and produces a
              consolidated go/no-go verdict (APPROVED / CONDITIONAL / REJECTED) with prioritized action items.

# ===========================================================
# CATEGORIES
# ===========================================================
Part Of Cookbook:   CFT-FWK-COOKBK-JOURNALIST-PROCESS
Category ID:        007  (CAT-007-JOURNALIST-PROCESS)
Subcategory ID:    006  (SUBCAT-006-FINAL-REVIEW)
Recipe ID Number:  RCP-007-006-002
Fully-Qualified:   CFT-FWK-COOKBK-JOURNALIST-PROCESS::RCP-007-006-002
Status:            Official
Categories:        Journalist Process
Subcategories:     Final Review
Tags:              approval · panel · publication · multi-perspective · sign-off · stakeholder · consensus · go-no-go
Recommended Persona: Nellie — Managing Editor (namespaced: PERSONA-JOURNALIST-PROCESS-NELLIE-CARD.txt)
Difficulty:        Advanced

# ===========================================================
# INSTRUCTIONS
# ===========================================================
1. Confirm the inputs: article_content is required; quality_gate_score, content_type (news, analysis, opinion,
   feature, investigative), and risk_level (low, medium, high) are optional. Note the quality_gate_score if
   provided, and use content_type + risk_level to calibrate the review.
2. Adopt Nellie's editorial framing: as Managing Editor she chairs the panel and owns the final publish decision.
   She invokes the Fact-Checker perspective (Fernand's QA function) as one of the four panel seats.
3. Convene the panel: assemble four stakeholder perspectives — Senior Editor, Fact-Checker, Legal Counsel,
   Audience Representative — and announce the convening.
4. Stakeholder assessments — FOR each stakeholder in [senior_editor, fact_checker, legal_counsel, audience_rep]:
   analyze the content from that perspective, evaluate against that stakeholder's criteria, determine the
   stakeholder verdict, identify the key concern if any, and document the assessment in a structured format.
5. Panel deliberation: compile all stakeholder verdicts; identify points of consensus and divergence; list any
   blocking issues and any conditional issues.
6. Determine the consolidated verdict: if ANY stakeholder verdict == "BLOCK" → REJECTED; else if the count of
   concern verdicts >= 2 → CONDITIONAL; else if all verdicts are positive or neutral → APPROVED; otherwise →
   CONDITIONAL.
7. Generate a formal approval decision document with: consolidated verdict, stakeholder summary, key strengths,
   required actions (if CONDITIONAL or REJECTED), publication recommendation (if APPROVED), and panel
   certification.
8. Next-steps guidance: APPROVED → proceed to Publishing & Distribution (RCP-007-007-001, Auguste); CONDITIONAL →
   address required actions and re-submit for expedited review; REJECTED → return to the appropriate earlier stage
   with the panel feedback. Output the approval_decision_document.

# ===========================================================
# CUSTOM FIELDS
# ===========================================================
Recipe FAQ:
  Q: Who is on the panel? A: four simulated perspectives — Senior Editor, Fact-Checker, Legal Counsel, Audience
     Representative — chaired by Nellie, who owns the final call.
  Q: How is the verdict decided? A: any single BLOCK forces REJECTED; two or more concern verdicts force
     CONDITIONAL; all-positive/neutral yields APPROVED; anything else is CONDITIONAL.
How A.I. Reads This Recipe:
  Execute as Nellie (Managing Editor) chairing the panel. Voice each stakeholder honestly against its own
  criteria before consolidating; the verdict rules are mechanical — apply them exactly, then own the go/no-go.
Recipe Short Description: Four-perspective publication approval panel that returns a go/no-go verdict with actions.
When To Use: after the Editorial Quality Gate returns READY, as the final sign-off before content moves to
  publishing and distribution.
Actual Examples: article_content="[paste article text]", quality_gate_score=8.4, content_type="investigative",
  risk_level="high".
Recipe Name: RCP-007-006-002
Included In Cookbook: CFT-FWK-COOKBK-JOURNALIST-PROCESS
Recommended Prompt Framework: CRAFT #H->AI / #AI->H comment protocol.
Extension Of: RCP-007-006-001 (Editorial Quality Gate) — consumes its READY draft + quality_gate_score.

    used_by=["RCP-007-007-001"],

    parameters={
        "article_content":    {"type": "string", "required": True,  "description": "Content for approval review", "example": "[paste article text]"},
        "quality_gate_score": {"type": "float",  "required": False, "default": "not provided", "description": "Quality Gate score from RCP-007-006-001 (optional)"},
        "content_type":       {"type": "string", "required": False, "options": ["news", "analysis", "opinion", "feature", "investigative"], "default": "analysis", "description": "Type of content being reviewed"},
        "risk_level":         {"type": "string", "required": False, "options": ["low", "medium", "high"], "default": "medium", "description": "Anticipated risk level"}
    },

    prompt_template="""

        owns the final publish decision. Convene the panel for final content review — simulate four stakeholder
        perspectives, deliberate to consensus, and produce a consolidated verdict.)

    # STEP 1: CONVENE PANEL
    #AI->H::Status: (Publication Approval Panel convened. Four stakeholders assembled: Senior Editor,
    Fact-Checker, Legal Counsel, Audience Representative.)
    RECEIVE article_content
    NOTE quality_gate_score if provided
    NOTE content_type and risk_level for calibration

    # STEPS 2-5: STAKEHOLDER ASSESSMENTS

        ANALYZE article_content from stakeholder perspective
        EVALUATE against stakeholder-specific criteria
        DETERMINE stakeholder verdict
        IDENTIFY key concern if applicable
        DOCUMENT assessment in structured format
    END FOR

    # STEP 6: PANEL DELIBERATION
    COMPILE all stakeholder verdicts
    IDENTIFY points of consensus
    IDENTIFY points of divergence
    LIST any blocking issues
    LIST any conditional issues

    # STEP 7: DETERMINE CONSOLIDATED VERDICT
    IF any stakeholder verdict == "BLOCK":
        verdict = "REJECTED"
    ELSE IF count of concern verdicts >= 2:
        verdict = "CONDITIONAL"
    ELSE IF all verdicts positive or neutral:
        verdict = "APPROVED"
    ELSE:
        verdict = "CONDITIONAL"

    # STEP 8: GENERATE APPROVAL DOCUMENT
    GENERATE formal approval decision document with:
        - Consolidated verdict
        - Stakeholder summary
        - Key strengths
        - Required actions (if CONDITIONAL or REJECTED)
        - Publication recommendation (if APPROVED)
        - Panel certification

    # STEP 9: NEXT STEPS GUIDANCE
    IF verdict == "APPROVED":
        #AI->H::Status: (APPROVED. Proceed to Publishing and Distribution stage (RCP-007-007-001).)
    ELSE IF verdict == "CONDITIONAL":
        #AI->H::Status: (CONDITIONAL. Address required actions and re-submit for expedited review.)
    ELSE:
        #AI->H::Status: (REJECTED. Return to appropriate earlier stage with panel feedback.)

    OUTPUT approval_decision_document
    """,

    outputs={

    },
